§ 1 pratijñāsūtra pjs

viśuddhajñānadehāya trivedīdivyacakṣuṣe | śreyaḥprāptinimittāya namaḥ somārdhadhāriṇe ||
abhivandya gurūnādau śiṣyadhīpadminīravīn | tatprasādātkariṣye 'haṃ mīmāṃsāślokavārttikaṃ ||
tadvidvāṃso 'nugṛhṇantu cittaśrotraiḥ prasādibhiḥ | santaḥ praṇayivākyāni gṛhṇanti hyanasūyavaḥ ||
na cātrātiva kartavyaṃ doṣadṛṣṭiparaṃ manaḥ | doṣo hyavidyamāno 'pi taccittānāṃ prakāśate ||
kuto vā gṛhṇate doṣaṃ sūrayo madvidhoktiṣu | neṣyate yaḥ parastho 'pi sa svayaṃ gṛhyate katham ||
nirdoṣatvaikavākyatvaṃ kva vā lokasya dṛśyate | sāpavādā yataḥ ke cinmokṣasvargāvapi prati ||
āgamapravaṇaścāhaṃ nāpavādyaḥ skhaliteṣvapyapodyate | na hi sadvartmanā gacchan skhaliteṣvapyapodyate ||
yathā kathañcidārabdhā trayīmārgānusāriṇī | vāgvṛttiralpasārāpi śraddadhānasya śobhate ||
mīmāṃsāśāstratejobhirviśeṣeṇojjvalīkṛte | vedārthajñānaratne me tṛṣṇātīva vijṛmbhate ||
prāyenaiva hi mīmāṃsā loke lokāyatīkṛtā | tāmāstikapathe kartumayaṃ yatnaḥ kṛto mayā ||
athāto dharmajijñāsā sūtramādyamidaṃ kṛtam | dharmākhyaṃ viṣayaṃ vaktuṃ mīmāṃsāyāḥ prayojanam ||
sarvasyaiva hi śāstrasya karmaṇo vāpi kasya cit | yāvatprayojanaṃ noktaṃ tāvattatkena gṛhyate ||
mīmāṃsākhyā tu vidyeyaṃ bahuvidyāntarāśritā | na śuśrūṣayituṃ śakyā prāganuktvā prayojanam ||
vidyāntareṣu nāpyetadyadyabhīṣṭaṃ prayojanam | anarthaprāpaṇaṃ tāvattebhyo nāśaṅkyate kva cit ||
mīmāṃsāyāṃ tvihājñāte durjñāte vāvivekataḥ | nyāyamārge mahāndoṣa iti yatnopacaryatā ||
tasmātprayojanaṃ pūrvamuktaṃ sūtrakṛtā svayam | yatsvenoktaṃ vadeyustadbhāṣyakārādayaḥ katham ||
siddhārthaṃ jñātasambandhaṃ śrotuṃ śrotā pravartate | śāstrādau tena vaktavyaḥ sambandhaḥ saprayojanaḥ ||
śāstraṃ prayojanaṃ caiva sambandhasyāśrayāvubhau | taduktyantargatastasmādbhinno noktaḥ prayojanāt ||
siddhiḥ śrotṛpravṛttīnāṃ sambandhakathanādyataḥ | tasmātsarveṣu śāstreṣu sambandhaḥ pūrvamucyate ||
yāvatprayojanenāsya sambandho nābhidhīyate | asambaddhapralāpitvādbhavettāvadasaṃgatiḥ ||
iha tvākṣipya sambandhaṃ bhāṣya evābhidhāsyate | dharmaprasiddhyasiddhibhyāṃ, tasmānnānyo 'bhidhīyate ||
na cāpyatrāthaśabdena śāstrasambandha ucyate | sambandhaṃ kriyayorhyeṣa brūte śāstrācca te pṛthak ||
yo 'pyayaṃ śāstrasambandho varṇyate kaiścidāditaḥ | kriyānantaryarūpo vā guruparvakramo 'pi vā ||
sadasadbhāvayostasya viśeṣo nopalabhyate | śroturvidhau niṣedhe vā jñāne vā śāstragocare ||
tasmādvyākhyāṅgamicchadbhiḥ sahetuḥ saprayojanaḥ | śāstrāvatārasambandho vācyo nānyastu niṣphalaḥ ||
loke ityādibhāṣyasya ṣaḍarthān sampracakṣate | bhāṣyakārānusāreṇa, prayuktasyāditaḥ pṛthak ||
sarvavyākhyāmupālambhaṃ pratyākhyānaṃ tathā pare | parisaṃkhyāstutī kecidathaśabdasya dūṣaṇam ||
sādhāraṇī viśiṣṭā ca sūtravyākhyā dvidhā matā | viśiṣṭā pratisūtraṃ yā sarvārthā tviyamucyate ||
pravṛttistu padeṣveva nivṛttiḥ sūtrasaṃśrayā | vedavākyāviruddheṣu na tu sarveṣu keṣu cit ||
adhyāhārasya vākyeṣu vyatyāsasya ca sambhavāt | tenaiṣāmiti sūtrāṇāṃ pārārthye satyapi grahaḥ ||
evaśabdo 'lpavācyatvād, asyāvṛttau tu gauravam | prasiddhatvādavācyaṃ cet, na doṣaḥ puṅgirāmayam ||
vyākhyāṅgatvābhimānena yo 'dhyāhārādyapekṣate | svasaṃjñāṃ vāpi tasyedaṃ śāstrarūpaṃ nirūpyate ||
vṛtyantareṣu keṣāñcillaukikārthavyatikramaḥ | śabdānāṃ dṛśyate teṣamupālambho 'yamucyate ||
athāta ityayaṃ loke nānantarye prayujyate | tasmāttādarthyametasya paribhāṣādibhirbhavet ||
prasiddhahāniḥ śabdānāmaprasiddhe ca kalpanā | na kāryā vṛttikāreṇa sati siddhārthasambhave ||
sūtrārthe kliśyataścaivaṃ dūre vedārthanirṇayaḥ | tatra yatnasya bhāratvaṃ vaktṛśrotroḥ prasajyate ||
na vyākhyāsyati sūtrāṇi codanārthaparatvataḥ | yattasya parihāro 'yaṃ pratyākhyānena cocyate ||
prayāso vedavākyeṣu kāryaḥ sūtreṣvanena kim | phalavattvāphalatvābhyām, ebhiḥ karaṇasammataiḥ ||
codanārtha upetavyaḥ, nobhayaṃ yatnagauravāt | padārthānāṃ prasiddhatvāt vyākhyeyaṃ nāvaśiṣyate ||
evaṃśabdādiko granthaḥ pakṣe cāsmin samarthyate | padacchedādyabhāvena pratyākhyānamatistviyam ||
brabītyeva hi sūtrārtham, atiriktādi ceṣyate | nanvaśaktamidaṃ sūtraṃ samyaksūtritamityapi ||
sūtre cāgamakatvādi pratyākhyāne virudhyate | na copāyānabhijñena śakyopeyāvadhāraṇā ||
nānyato vedavidbhyaśca sūtravṛttikriyeṣyate | pratyākhyānasya hetuśca padārthānāṃ prasiddhatā ||
yoktā sā vedavākyānaṃ tulyārthatvānnivārayet | vākyārthe tatra sandehādvyākhyānaṃ cetpravartate ||
sūtreṣvapi samānatvātpratyākhyānaṃ na yujyate | na vyākhyātavyamityevaṃ pratyākhyāne ca sidhyati ||
duṣṭavyākhyā niṣedhena tadapetā na vāryate | asya dṛṣṭaviruddhatvātphalgutvāccāpi parvayoḥ ||
madhyame cātidaurjanyātparisaṃkhyaiva yujyate | vaidikaṃ jaiminīyaṃ ca yatra vākyaṃ virudhyate ||
yathāśrutagṛhīte 'rthe tatredamupadiśyate | adhyāhārādibhiḥ sūtraṃ vaidikaṃ tu yathāśrutam ||
neyam, virodhe 'nyonyasya vaidikānāṃ bhavantu te | yathā dharmāvabodhasya pramāṇaṃ vaidikaṃ vacaḥ ||
tadarthanirṇaye heturjaiminīyaṃ tathaiva naḥ | vākyasāmarthyatulyatvāttathā padatadarthayoḥ ||
adhyāhārādibhirmuktā vyākhyā sarvatra yujyate | asambhavādavaśyaṃ yā virodhe 'nyatarasya tu ||
anyāyyakalpanā sāpi vikalpena prasajyate | prāthamyenāvaruddhatvādupāyavaśato 'tha vā ||
yathāśrutena sūtreṇa nyāyyāṃ bādheta codanām | tena vedāviruddhasya sati sambhava ityayam ||
vidhīyate 'rthaḥ, śeṣaṃ tu yathāprāptamanūdyate | śeṣabhājāṃ bhavellopa ityadhyāhārakalpanā ||
viprakarṣātpaśośceti vibhaktiḥ pariṇamyate | padena vyavadhānaṃ tu loke saṃniyamāditi ||
sūtreṇa vyavadhānaṃ tu pānavyāpadi kalpitam | paśusāmānyavidhyādau sūtramevānyathā kṛtam ||
agnayaśca svakālatvāddeyadharmāpayātanam | vyākhyānaṃ vākyabhedena, guṇakalpāstvamī kṛtāḥ ||
autpattikastu gavyasya tathoṣṇikkakubhoriti | darśanācca viśeṣasya tathābhyudaya ityapi ||
sūtrakārapraśaṃsā vā loka ityādinocyate | prasiddhairabhidhānāddhi na śiṣyāḥ kleśitā yataḥ ||
bhavitavyaṃ tu teneti prāgasmādekavākyatā | vedādhyayanavākyādvā tenāthetyasya dūṣaṇam ||
prasiddhārthapadaiḥ śakyaḥ sūtrairvedārthanirṇayaḥ | na ca so 'styathaśabdasya vinā te pūrvakarmaṇā ||
prasiddhārthaṃ padaṃ yuktaṃ tacca nāstīti dūṣaṇam | prasiddho 'pyathaśabdādeḥ kiṃpadārtho 'tra varṇyate ||
pradarśanārthamityeke, ke cinnānārthavācinaḥ | samudāyādavacchidya bhavadāsena kalpitāt ||
śaktito 'vayavaṃ caiva varṇayantyaṣṭamādivat | na cātra codanāvyākhyā gauravaṃ tatra coditam ||
yadvākṣepo yathoktasya vṛttābhāvādasambhavāt | yadi lokaprasiddhārthagrahaṇaṃ kriyate pade ||
sa nāstyatrāthaśabdasyetyadhyāhārādikalpanam | vedādhyayanavṛttatvaṃ snānasyotkarṣakalpanā ||
nāvyākhyāte 'thaśabdārthe jñāyate tena varṇyate | anarthake 'tha vānyārthe prasiddhirbādhyate dhruvam ||
tasmāc chrutārthasiddhyarthaṃ vṛttaṃ kimapi gamyate | viśiṣṭaliṅgavijñānādviśiṣṭe liṅginīkṣite ||
sūtreṇāsambhavaṃ matvā naitadityabravītparaḥ | ānantaryopadeśena taddṛṣṭārthatayāpi ca ||
vedādhyayanamākṣiptaṃ kimasūtritacodanā | yena vṛttena jijñāsā vinā naivopapadyate ||
tadānantaryamuktaṃ hi dṛṣṭārthamavakalpate | kriyamāṇā ca jijñāsā niyamādyasya kasya cit ||
kriyetānantaraiveti vyarthaṃ tadupadeśanam | saṅkalpādibhirapyeṣā vinā satyaṃ na sidhyati ||
sādhāraṇyāttu te 'pyatra nopadeśyāḥ kathañcana | tasmāddharmabubhutsāyāmasādhāraṇakāraṇam ||
nirvṛttaṃ sūtrakāreṣṭaṃ tacca nākhyayanādṛte | anyasyāpītyanenaiva vedapāṭhe prabādhite ||
prāgapīti hi vaktavyaṃ tatrāpyanyasya sambhavāt | pūrveṇaiva hi labdhārthe tādṛśīṃ tvityanena kim ||
vakṣyamāṇamanālocya sambhavetparicodanā | na tāvatsādhyate 'dyāpi codanā dharmasādhanam ||
iha vā kāni vākyāni vivariṣyati jaiminiḥ | dharmamātrābhidhānāddhi buddhādivacanānyapi ||
paṭhitvā dharmajijñāsetyanyasyāpīti codanā | yadvā bhavatu nāmedṛksūtraṃ vedamadhītya tu ||
jijñāsānantaraṃ kāryetyatrāpi dvayamīpsitam | nānadhītya na cāpyanyatkṛtvetyetanna labhyate ||
vakṣyamāṇavacobhaṅgyorvākyabhedaprasaṅgataḥ | adhītyaiveti hi vidhau snānāderapyanantarā ||
bhaveddharmasya jijñāsā nānantaryavidhistadā | ānantaryavidhāne tu yā vedādhyayane kṛte ||
ityevamanuvādatvātprāgapyeṣā prasajyate | buddhavākyādipāṭhasya tādṛśīṃ tvityapākriyā ||
prāgapīti ca codyasya, sāmarthyādvedalābhataḥ | naivaitayorvacobhaṅgyoreko 'pyartho vidhīyate ||
api cetyādikenoktam, kin tvityetadvidhīyate | ānantaryaṃ parastācca nāpi śiṃṣma itīha tu ||
ke cidadhyāharanti, asya sūtrasyānyaparatvataḥ | na vāryate 'nadhītatvaṃ nānantaryaṃ vidhīyate ||
sāmarthyāsiddhyadṛṣṭārthaprasaṅgāttena lakṣaṇā | ānantaryavacovyaktirāśritaivātra lakṣyate ||
śrutārthaṃ tvaparityajya lakṣaṇārtho vidhīyate | pratītā dharmajijñāsā vedādhyāyādanantarā ||
tatkālasyāvaruddhatvātsnānābhāvaṃ hi lakṣayet | virodho yugapatprāpteḥ, daurbalyaṃ vedabādhanāt ||
snānasya tena bādhaḥ syāddharmajijñāsayā balāt | dṛṣṭārthatvādisaṃyuktaṃ vākyaṃ lakṣaṇayā tviti ||
punaruktyā gatārthatvāttyaktaṃ kaiścit, taducyate | yadyapyasya bhavedvācyamānantaryamasaṃśayam ||
tathāpi pūrvatāmātraṃ lakṣayedavirodhataḥ | granthagrahaṇamātre ca kṛte snānaṃ virudhyate ||
adhītyetyadhigamyeti vyākhyāne tvavirodhitā | yastvevamavirodhitvaṃ kurvannāplavanaṃ vadet ||
adṛṣṭāyātha vāpyanyaḥ saṃskāraṃ tasya cottaram | ihāsnānādiniyamo yaḥ kṛto brahmacāriṇaḥ ||
avidhitvamanāśritya so 'vasānamapekṣate | tato 'pekṣāvaśātsnānamasnānādinivartanam ||
virodhasāhacaryābhyāṃ dṛṣṭārthatvena lakṣayet | tasmādadhyayanasnānajijñāsākramavācinām ||
dṛṣṭārthatvāya śabdānāmevaṃ vyākhyeyamāśritā | snātvā jijñāsamāno 'pi nanu vedaṃ na bādhate ||
tenāvirodhitā tasya, ityevaṃ vadata uttaram | yathaivādhyayanātsnānaṃ smaryate samanantaram ||
tathā tataḥ paro 'pyanyaḥ padārtho 'nyaḥ parastataḥ | tataścāvaśyakartavye bādhe smārtasya kasya cit ||
yogyatvādāgate kāle prāthamyātsnānabādhanam | so 'yaṃ pāṭhakramasyārthādbādha ityavagamyate ||
guṇapradhānayorvāpi virodhādguṇabādhanam | snānopalakṣitā cātra nivṛttirguruveśmanaḥ ||
virodhitvena bādhyeta na tu madhvādibhakṣaṇam | tasmādgurukule tiṣṭhanmadhumāṃsādyavarjayan ||
jijñāsetāviruddhatvāddharmamityavagamyate | gurugehanivṛttyaṃśo yāvacca na samāpyate ||
tāvatsakalavācitvānna snānaṃ paryavasyati | gurugehādanāvṛttaḥ snātako hi na kathyate ||
tatparatvavidhānācca na tāvaddārasaṅgrahaḥ | vyākhyāya kīrtitā cātra snāyāditi punaḥ smṛtiḥ ||
smāvartiṣṭa metyādi smṛteryadyapyanantaram | viparītārthamityasmāttadvākyādapanīyate ||
athaśabdena yo bādhaḥ purastādupavarṇitaḥ | tanmātrasyaiva bādho 'tra dṛṣṭārthatvātpradarśitaḥ ||
smṛtiprāptamidānīṃ tu madhumāṃsādyavarjanam | pratiṣedhannadṛṣṭārthaṃ sūtrakāro na śobhate ||
nivṛttya gurugehācca jijñāsārthaḥ punarbhavet | praveśaḥ so 'pyadṛṣṭārtha iti naiveha sūtritaḥ ||
nirgamo hi kṛtārthasya dṛṣṭārtho guruveśmanaḥ | smaryate tasya nārthaḥ syādakṛtārthasya nirgame ||
athaśabdaprasiddhyaiva vedagrahaṇahetutā | ānantaryopadeśitvādataḥ śabdena kiṃ punaḥ ||
yogyatvamathaśabdena yadyapi pratipāditam | tadeva heturatreti nātaḥśabdādvinā bhavet ||
lakṣaṇaṃ puruṣasyaiva tadā taddhi prasajyate | jijñāsāyāśca hetutve phalārthatvādi sambhavet ||
ataḥśabdagṛhītaṃ vā tatrādhyayanamāśritam | hetāvakathyamāne hi maṅgalādyapyasau vadet ||
snānabādhasya vā heturata ityucyate punaḥ | yogyasyādhītavedatvānnāvasthātuṃ hi labhyate ||
sanvācyecchāntaraṃ karma jñānaṃ vyāpnoti tāvatā | jñānopasarjanā saiva na tu vidhyādi gamyate ||
iṣestu karma bāhyaḥ syāddharmaḥ sā vātha vā dvayam | samānakartṛkatvaṃ tu tumunoktaṃ liṅā vidhiḥ ||
evaṃ viṣayanānātvānna kā citpunaruktatā | sūtritecchābhinirvṛttyai dvitīyecchātra sūtritā ||
prakṛtyā vikṛtiryasmāccaturthyantā samasyate | tādarthye yūpadārvādau tenāsminnasamāsatā ||
sa hi tasyetyanenokto dharmasyetyeṣa vigrahaḥ | dharmāyeti tu tādarthye ṣaṣṭhī vṛtteti kathyate ||
prāpnotyatra caturthyeva viśeṣaścedvivakṣitaḥ | sāmānyasya vivakṣāyāṃ tādṛśaṃ kathyate katham ||
sambandhamātra evaiṣā ṣaṣṭhyutpannā tathāpi tu | viśeṣaniṣṭhatā tasyā bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇyate ||
sādhanābhāsatā cātra pūrvapakṣārthagocarā | anyasādhanamanyasya sādhanābhāsa ucyate ||
kratvarthaṃ puruṣārthasya tadarthaṃ ca kratoriti | śeṣalakṣaṇaśabdaśca kṛtsnaśāstravivakṣayā ||
prasiddhaḥ śakyate jñātum prasiddhatvāttu neṣyate | aprasiddhastvaśakyatvānnatarāmityato 'bravīt ||
jijñāsyaḥ saṃśayāddharmaḥ śreyaskaratayāpi ca | asandigdho hyajijñāsyo yo vā syānniṣprayojanaḥ ||
svarūpādiṣu dharmasya dvidhā vipratipadyate | pūrvaṃ pramāṇarūpābhyām, pādenādyasya nirṇayaḥ ||
sthite vedapramāṇatve punarvākyārthanirṇaye | matirbahuvidāṃ puṃsāṃ saṃśayānnopajāyate ||
ke cidāhurasāvarthaḥ, ke cinnāsāvayaṃ tviti | tannirṇayārthamapyetatparaṃ śāstraṃ praṇīyate ||

§ 2 codanāsūtra cds

dharme sāmānyataḥ siddhe pramāṇaṃ codanocyate | svarūpādestataḥ siddhaḥ, svarūpaṃ ceha sūtryate ||
dvayamekena sūtreṇa śrutyarthābhyāṃ nirūpyate | svarūpe 'pi hi tasyokte pramāṇaṃ kathyate 'rthataḥ ||
kimādyapekṣitaiḥ pūrṇaḥ samarthaḥ pratyayo vidhau | tena pravartakaṃ vākyaṃ śāstre 'smin codanocyate ||
codanaiva pramāṇaṃ cetyetaddharme 'vadhāritam | sākāṅkṣamiti manvāno yuktileśaṃ dvaye 'spṛśat ||
sambhāvyate pramāṇatvaṃ śabdasyaivaṃvidheṣvapi | indriyāderasāmarthyaṃ vakṣyamāṇamadīdiśat ||
atyantāsatyapi jñānamarthe śabdaḥ karoti hi | tenotsarge sthite tasya doṣābhāvātpramāṇatā ||
codanetyabravīccātra śabdamātravivakṣayā | na hi bhūtādiviṣayaḥ kaścidasti vidhāyakaḥ ||
indriyādivyudāsena śabdo yāvanna sādhyate | tāvacca tadviśeṣasya kuto vāvasaro bhavet ||
nimittamātraṃ vocyeta pramāṇaṃ ceha lakṣaṇam | pramāṇaṃ tvapi śabdo vā tajjñānaṃ vā nirūpyate ||
padārthastanmatirvā syādvākyārthādhigamo 'pi vā | pūrveṣāṃ tu pramāṇatve phalatvaṃ tasya gamyate ||
jñāne lakṣaṇaśabdo 'yaṃ yadi nāma prayujyate | codanoktistadā kāryaṃ tatkāryaṃ cāpi lakṣayet ||
nimittamātre śabde ca pramāṇe mukhyavṛttayoḥ | sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ syāccodanālakṣaṇatvayoḥ ||
dravyakriyāguṇādīnāṃ dharmatvaṃ sthāpayiṣyate | teṣāmaindriyakatve 'pi na tādrūpyeṇa dharmatā ||
śreyaḥsādhanatā hyeṣāṃ nityaṃ vedātpratīyate | tādrūpyeṇa ca dharmatvaṃ tasmānnendriyagocaraḥ ||
pradarśanārthamatroktamindriyaṃ sūtrakāravat | nānyatkiñceti vācchedaḥ sāmānyārthaḥ prayujyate ||
tadasāmarthyasiddhyai ca punarindriyakīrtanam | kiñceti madhyamacchedo hetupraśne prayujyate ||
yadyapi tvanumānasyāpyevamādau samarthatā | vinā sambandhabodhena na tu tasyodbhavaḥ kva cit ||
na sāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ dharmasambandhadarśanam | liṅgasya kasya citsiddhaṃ yena syādanumānatā ||
nanu śabdo 'pi sambandhabodhānnarte pravarttate | padaṃ tat, na ca tadvācyo dharmaḥ, vākyārtha eva saḥ ||
vākyasyāvācakatvaṃ ca, padārthānāṃ ca hetutā | sambandhasyānapekṣāṇāṃ vākyārthe sthāpayiṣyate ||
nityatvāderasiddhatvād, abhyupetyocyate 'tha vā | sutarāmapramāṇatvaṃ vaktṛprāmāṇyavarjanāt ||
pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭaṃ hi śabdo 'rthaṃ prāpayetsadā | smṛtivacca svayaṃ tasya prāmāṇyaṃ nopapadyate ||
nūnaṃ tatrānubhūto 'sāvityāptoktinibandhanā | buddhiḥ sākṣādadṛṣṭe 'pi yuktārthe puruṣoktitaḥ ||
nātmīyādanyadīyādvā pratyakṣādervinā kva cit | vacasaḥ satyatā dṛṣṭā tathā syāccodanāsvapi ||
tena satyapi vijñāne pratijñāderyathaiva hi | svātantryānna pramāṇatvaṃ tathā vede 'pi dṛśyatām ||
svargayāgādisambandhaviṣayā codanā mṛṣā | pratyakṣādyagatārthatvādīdṛgbuddhādivākyavat ||
yadvāptenāpraṇītatvādbālonmattādivākyavat | vyomādivacca nityatvātprāmāṇyasya nirākṛtiḥ ||
yadi vā puruṣādhīnaprāmāṇyāḥ sarvacodanāḥ | svato vā na pramāṇaṃ syurvākyatvātpuruṣoktivat ||
prāmāṇyaṃ vā narāpekṣaṃ sarvaśabdeṣu gamyatām | śabdaiḥ sambandhyamānatvādapramāṇyaṃ tathaiva hi ||
na syādvaktṛguṇānāṃ cedvacaḥ prāmāṇyahetutā | taddoṣairapramāṇatvaṃ kimityasya bhaviṣyati ||
evaṃ sthite tu vedasya sati vāsati vā nare | prāmāṇyaṃ durlabhaṃ matvā nanvityetadacūcudat ||
tatra vipratiṣiddhatvaṃ buddhavākye 'pi yujyate | tato 'pi pratyayotpattestasmājjātyuttaraṃ tvidam ||
sarvavijñānaviṣayamidaṃ tāvatparīkṣyatām | pramāṇatvāpramāṇatve svataḥ kiṃ parato 'tha vā ||
svato 'satāmasādhyatvātke cidāhurdvayaṃ svataḥ | apare kāraṇotpannaguṇadoṣāvadhāraṇāt ||
svatastāvaddvayaṃ nāsti, virodhāt, parato na ca | niḥsvabhāvatvamevaṃ hi jñānarūpe prasajyate ||
kathaṃ hyanyānapekṣasya viparītātmasambhavaḥ | kimātmakaṃ bhavettacca svabhāvadvayavarjitam ||
vijñānavyaktibhedena bhaveccedaviruddhatā | tathāpyanyānapekṣatve kiṃ kveti na nirūpyate ||
tasmātsvābhāvikaṃ teṣāmapramāṇatvamiṣyatām | prāmāṇyañca parāpekṣam, atra nyāyo 'bhidhīyate ||
aprāmānyamavastutvānna syātkāraṇadoṣataḥ | vastutvāttu guṇaisteṣāṃ prāmāṇyamupajanyate ||
prāmāṇyaṃ hi yadotsargāttadabhāvo 'tha kṛtrimaḥ | tadā svapnādibodhe 'pi prāmāṇyaṃ kena vāryate ||
matpakṣe kāraṇābhāvātprāmānyaṃ nopajāyate | hetumattvaprasaṅgo 'to na bhaviṣyatyavastunaḥ ||
indriyādiguṇāścāsya kāraṇam, tadasaddvidhā | duṣṭatvādindriyādīnāmabhāve 'nyatamasya vā ||
ata eva ca vo bhrāntirdoṣairmithyātvadhīriti | tadvyāptestu guṇābhāvastatkṛtā hyapramāṇatā ||
tasmātkāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ jñānaprāmāṇyakāraṇam | svabhāvato 'pramāṇatvaṃ tadabhāvena lakṣyate ||
anvayavyatirekābhyāmaprāmāṇyaṃ na doṣataḥ | nājñāne dṛśyate hyetatkāraṇābhāvahetuke ||
tataśca puruṣābhāvātsati vā śuddhyasambhavāt | nirmūlatvātpramāṇatvaṃ codanāyāṃ na yujyate ||
svataḥ sarvapramāṇānāṃ prāmāṇyamiti gamyatām | na hi svato 'satī śaktiḥ kartumanyena śakyate ||
ātmalābhe ca bhāvānāṃ kāraṇāpekṣatā bhavet | labdhātmanāṃ svakāryeṣu pravṛttiḥ svayameva tu ||
jāte 'pi yadi vijñāne tāvannārtho 'vadhāryate | yāvatkāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ na pramāṇāntarādbhavet ||
tatra jñānāntarotpādaḥ pratīkṣyaḥ kāraṇāntarāt | yāvaddhi na paricchinnā śuddhistāvadasatsamā ||
tasyāpi kāraṇe śuddhe tajjñāne syātpramāṇatā | tasyāpyevamitīcchaśca na kva cidvyavatiṣṭhate ||
yadā svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ tadānyannaiva gṛhyate | nivarttatte hi mithyātvaṃ doṣājñānādayatnataḥ ||
tasmādbodhātmakatvena prāptā buddheḥ pramāṇatā | arthānyathātvahetūtthadoṣajñānādapodyate ||
aprāmāṇyaṃ tridhā bhinnaṃ mithyātvājñānasaṃśayaiḥ | vastutvāddvividhasyātra sambhavo duṣṭakāraṇāt ||
avijñāne tu doṣāṇāṃ vyāpāro naiva kalpyate | kāraṇābhāvatastveva tatsiddhaṃ nastvaduktivat ||
doṣataścāpramāṇatve svataḥprāmāṇyavādinām | guṇajñānānavasthāvanna doṣeṣu prasajyate ||
sākṣādviparyayajñānāllaghvyeva tvapramāṇatā | pūrvābādhena notpattiruttarasya hi sidhyati ||
duṣṭakāraṇabodhe tu siddhe 'pi viṣayāntare | arthāttulyārthatāṃ prāpya bādho godohanādivat ||
tatra doṣāntarajñānaṃ bādhadhīrvā parā na cet | tadudbhūtau dvitīyasya mithyātvādādyamānatā ||
svata eva hi tatrāpi doṣājñānātpramāṇatā | doṣajñāne tvanutpanne na śaṅkyā niṣpramāṇatā ||
evaṃ tricaturajñānajanmano nādhikā matiḥ | prārthyate tāvataivaikaṃ svataḥ prāmāṇyamaśnute ||
śabde doṣodbhavastāvadvaktradhīna iti sthitiḥ | tadabhāvaḥ kva cittāvadguṇavadvaktṛkatvataḥ ||
tadguṇairapakṛṣṭānāṃ śabde saṃkrāntyasambhavāt | yadā vakturabhāvena na syurdoṣā nirāśrayāḥ ||
pauruṣeye dvayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ doṣābhāvo guṇāstathā | prāmāṇyaṃ tatra guṇato naiva syādityudāhṛtam ||
tasmādguṇebhyo doṣāṇāmabhāvastadabhāvataḥ | aprāmāṇyadvayāsattvaṃ tenotsargo 'napoditaḥ ||
pratyayotpattihetutvātprāmāṇyaṃ nāpanīyate | doṣābhāvo guṇebhyaścennanu saivāsthitirbhavet ||
tadā tu vyāpriyante hi jñāyamānatayā guṇāḥ | doṣābhāve tu vijñeye sattāmātropakāriṇaḥ ||
tatrāpavādanirmuktirvaktrabhāvāllaghīyasī | vede tenāpramāṇatvaṃ nāśaṅkāmapi gacchati ||
ato vaktranadhīnatvātprāmāṇye tadupāsanam | na yuktam, apramāṇatve kalpye tatprārthanā bhavet ||
tataścāptāpraṇītatvaṃ na doṣāyātra jāyate | prayogāṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ vakṣyāmaḥ pratisādhanam ||
pauruṣeye tu vacane pramāṇāntaramūlatā | tadabhāve hi tadduṣyeditaranna kadā cana ||
tenetaraiḥ pramāṇairyā codanānāmasaṅgatiḥ | tayaiva syātpramāṇatvamanuvādatvamanyathā ||
anyasyāpi pramāṇatve saṅgatirnaiva kāraṇam | tulyārthānāṃ vikalpyatvādekaṃ tatra hi bodhakam ||
yatrāpi syātparicchedaḥ pramāṇairuttaraiḥ punaḥ | nūnaṃ tatrāpi pūrveṇa so 'rtho nāvadhṛtastathā ||
saṅgatyā yadi ceṣyeta pūrvapūrvapramāṇatā | pramāṇāntaramicchanto na vyavasthāṃ labhemahi ||
kasya cittu yadīṣyeta svata eva pramāṇatā | prathamasya tathābhāve pradveṣaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ ||
śrotradhīścāpramāṇaṃ syāditarābhirasaṅgateḥ | syāccettajjanitenaiva jñānenānyena saṅgatiḥ ||
vede 'pi śatakṛtvaḥ syādbuddhiruccāraṇānugā | sādhanāntarajanyā tu buddhirnāsti dvayorapi ||
yathā tvekendriyādhīnajñānāntaranibandhanā | saṅgatiḥ kāraṇaṃ prāptā tathā vede 'pi kalpyatām ||
tasmāddṛḍhaṃ yadutpannaṃ nāpi saṃvādamṛcchati | jñānāntareṇa vijñānaṃ tatpramāṇaṃ pratīyatām ||
na cānumānataḥ sādhyā śabdādīnāṃ pramāṇatā | sarvasyaiva hi mā prāpatpramāṇāntarasādhyatā ||
nanu pramāṇamityevaṃ pratyakṣādi na gṛhyate | na cetthamagṛhītena vyavahāro 'vakalpate ||
prāmāṇyaṃ grahaṇātpūrvaṃ svarūpeṇaiva saṃsthitam | nirapekṣaṃ svakāryeṣu gṛhyate pratyayāntaraiḥ ||
tenāsya jñāyamānatvaṃ prāmāṇye nopayujyate | viṣayānubhavo hyatra pūrvasmādeva labhyate ||
apramāṇaṃ punaḥ svārthagrāhakaṃ syātsvarūpataḥ | nivṛttistasya mithyātve nāgṛhīte parairbhavet ||
na hyarthasyātathābhāvaḥ pūrveṇārthastathātvavat | tatrāpyarthānyathābhāve dhīryadvā duṣṭakāraṇe ||
tāvataiva ca mithyātvaṃ gṛhyate nānyahetukam | utpattyavasthaṃ caivedaṃ pramāṇamiti mīyate ||
ato yatrāpi mithyātvaṃ parebhyaḥ pratipādyate | tatrāpyetaddvayaṃ vācyaṃ na tu sādharmyamātrakam ||
codanārthānyathābhāvaṃ kurvataścānumānataḥ | tajjñānenaiva yo bādhaḥ sa kathaṃ vinivāryate ||
tanmithyātvādabādhaścet, prāptamanyonyasaṃśrayam | nānumānādato 'nyaddhi bādhakaṃ kiñcidasti te ||
na cānyairagrahe 'rthasya syādabhāvo rasādivat | teṣāṃ jihvādibhiryasmānniyamo grahaṇe 'sti hi ||
taddhiyaivārthabodhaścet, tādṛgdharme bhaviṣyati | mamāsiddhamidaṃ kin tu vedājjāte 'vabodhane ||
vaktuṃ na dveṣamātreṇa yujyate satyavādinā | dveṣādasammatatvādvā na ca syādapramāṇatā ||
na cātmecchābhyanujñābhyāṃ prāmāṇyamavakalpate | agnidāhādiduḥkhasya na hyapratyakṣateṣyate ||
na cābhilāpikaṃ jñānaṃ prāmāṇyenāvadhāryate | tasmādālokavadvede sarvasādhāraṇe sati ||
naivaṃ vipratipattavyam, bauddhādervakṣyate 'ntaram | puruṣāśaktitastatra sāpavādatvasambhavaḥ ||
vedasyāpauruṣeyatve siddhā tvevaṃ pramāṇatā | kartṛmattve tu vedasya samyaṅmithyātvavādibhiḥ ||
kartā guṇāśca doṣāśca mahājanaparigrahaḥ | evamādi vinā yuktyā kalpyam, mīmāṃsakaiḥ punaḥ ||
idānīmiva sarvatra dṛṣṭānnādhikamiṣyate | evambhūtasya vedasya jñānotpattiṃ prakurvataḥ ||
svarūpaviparītatvasaṃśayau bhāṣyavāritau | nivārayiṣyate cāpi duṣṭakāraṇakalpanā ||
puruṣābhāvatastena taddvāreṇāpyaśaṅkitau | tathā satyatathābhāvo buddhyanutpattimāśritaḥ ||
tatra vipratiṣiddhatvaṃ bravītītyevamādinā | yathādṛṣṭārthavāditvaṃ taccetpratyayitāditi ||
indriyeti tu mūlaṃ cedasyāstītyevamabravīt | draṣṭṛtvasatyavāditve taccetpratyayitāditi ||
dṛśyamānārthavāditve syādanāptoktisatyatā | evaṃ tvekāṅgavaikalyātpratyudāharaṇasthitiḥ ||
ekaikābhāvamātre syādāptatvaindriyakatvayoḥ | apratyayitapakṣe syādaindriyasyāpyasatyatā ||
anindriyatvapakṣe vā satpratyayitabhāṣitam | vyāhatagranthataivaṃ syāt, tasmātpūrveṇa satyatā ||
pareṇa mūlasadbhāva indriyeṇa tu darśitaḥ | aprāmāṇyanivṛttyarthaṃ doṣābhāvopavarṇanam ||
guṇātprāmāṇyamityevaṃ tatpūrvaṃ sunirākṛtam | pūrvatra pratiṣiddhatvānnaitatprāmāṇyakāraṇam ||
samuccayārtho vāśabdaḥ pūrvasmin, uttaratra ca | vikalpenobhayorāha pratyudāharaṇe pṛthak ||
śakye 'pyasatye mithyātvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ satye 'pyaśaktike | nānena vacaneneha sarvajñatvanirākriyā ||
vacanādṛta ityevamapavādo hi saṃśritaḥ | yadi ṣaḍbhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ syātsarvajñaḥ kena vāryate ||
ekena tu pramāṇena sarvajño yena kalpyate | nūnaṃ sa cakṣuṣā sarvānrasādīn pratipadyate ||
yajjātīyaiḥ pramāṇaistu yajjātīyārthadarśanam | bhavedidānīṃ lokasya tathā kālāntare 'pyabhūt ||
yatrāpyatiśayo dṛṣṭaḥ sa svārthānatilaṅghanāt | dūrasūkṣmādidṛṣṭau syānna rūpe śrotravṛttitā ||
bhaviṣyati na dṛṣṭaṃ ca pratyakṣasya manāgapi | sāmarthyam, nānumānāderliṅgādirahite kva cit ||
sarvajñakalpanānyaistu vede cāpauruṣeyatā | tulyatā kalpitā yena tenedaṃ sampradhāryatām ||
sarvajño dṛśyate tāvannedānīmasmadādibhiḥ | nirākaraṇavacchakyā na cāsīditi kalpanā ||
na cāgamena sarvajñaḥ, tadīye 'nyonyasaṃśrayāt | narāntarapraṇītasya prāmāṇyaṃ gamyate katham ||
na cāpyevamparo nityaḥ śakyo labdhumihāgamaḥ | nityaścedarthavādatvaṃ tatpare syādanityatā ||
āgamasya ca nityatve siddhe tatkalpanā vṛthā | yatastaṃ pratipadyante dharmameva tato narāḥ ||
yo 'pīndriyārthasambandhaviṣaye satyavāditām | dṛṣṭvā tadvacanatvena śraddheye 'rthe 'pi kalpayet ||
tenāpi pāratantryeṇa bādhitā syātpramāṇatā | prāmāṇyaṃ cetsvayaṃ tasya kāpekṣānyendriyādiṣu ||
yathaivātrendriyādibhyaḥ paricchedātpramāṇatā | śraddheye 'pi tathaiva syānna svātantryeṇa labhyate ||
yathā ca teṣāṃ satyatvaṃ sidhyatyetena hetunā | tathānyānavabuddhārthaprāmāṇyābhāvasādhanam ||
aśraddheyārthasatyatvaṃ śraddheye cāpyasatyatā | pūrvajñānānuvāditvaṃ dṛṣṭāntavadiheṣyatām ||
api cālaukikārthatve sati puṃvākyahetukam | mithyātvaṃ bauddhavākyānāṃ syādanyonyaṃ sapakṣataḥ ||
dharmādharmātiriktārthe prāmāṇyaṃ ca prasajyate | sāṃkhyādiṣu ca jīvatsu dṛṣṭānto durlabho 'sya ca ||
alaukikārthavācitvaṃ nṛvākyatve satīti ca | parasparamapekṣyaiva bauddhādeḥ syānmṛṣārthatā ||
vadedevaṃ ca yo nāma vādī prathamasaṅgataḥ | tasyāpi hetuḥ syādeṣa bhavantaṃ pratyasaṃśayam ||
buddhādīnāmasarvajñamiti satyaṃ vaco mama | maduktatvādyathaivāgniruṣṇo bhāsvara ityapi ||
pratyakṣaṃ ca maduktatvaṃ tvayā sādhyā taduktatā | tena heturmadīyaḥ syātsandigdhāsiddhatā tava ||
pratyakṣādyavisaṃvādi prameyatvādi yasya ca | sadbhāvavāraṇe śaktaṃ ko nu taṃ kalpayiṣyati ||
na cāpi smṛtyavicchedātsarvajñaḥ parikalpyate | vigānāt, chinnamūlatvāt, kaiścideva parigrahāt ||
sarvajño 'sāviti hyeva tatkāle tu bubhutsubhiḥ | tajjñānajñeyavijñānarahitairgamyate katham ||
kalpanīyāśca sarvajñā bhaveyurbahavastava | ya eva syādasarvajñaḥ sa sarvajñaṃ na budhyate ||
sarvajño 'navabuddhaśca yenaiva syānna taṃ prati | tadvākyānāṃ pramāṇatvaṃ mūlājñāne 'nyavākyavat ||
rāgādirahite cāsminnirvyāpāre vyavasthite | deśanānyapraṇītaiva syādṛte pratyavekṣaṇāt ||
sānnidhyamātratastasya puṃsaścintāmaṇeriva | niḥsaranti yathākāmaṃ kuḍyādibhyo 'pi deśanāḥ ||
evamādyucyamānaṃ tu śraddadhānasya śobhate | kuḍyādiniḥsṛtatvācca nāśvāso deśanāsu naḥ ||
kinnu buddhapraṇītāḥ syuḥ kimu kaiściddurātmabhiḥ | adṛśyairvipralambhārthaṃ piśācādibhirīritāḥ ||
evaṃ yaiḥ kevalaṃ jñānamindriyādyanapekṣiṇaḥ | sūkṣmātītādiviṣayaṃ jīvasya parikalpitam ||
narte tadāgamātsidhyenna ca tenāgamo vinā | dṛṣṭānto 'pi na tasyānyo nṛṣu kaścitpravartate ||
nityāgamāvabodho 'pi pratyākhyeyo 'nayā diśā | na hi tatrāpi visrambho dṛṣṭo 'nena kṛto 'tha vā ||
sarvadā cāpi puruṣāḥ prāyeṇānṛtavādinaḥ | yathādyatve na visrambhastathātītārthakīrtane ||
svapnādijñānavaccāpi pratyayo 'syāgamārthayoḥ | bhavediti saśaṅkānāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ gamyate katham ||
puruṣātiśayaśceṣṭaḥ saiva cāgamanityatā | kalpitaṃ smaraṇaṃ cāsya janmāntaranibandhanam ||
grāhyatve cāgamasyaivaṃ dveṣo 'rthagrahaṇe vṛthā | yo hyanuccāritaṃ śabdaṃ gahṇātyarthe 'sya kā kathā ||
pumāṃstāvatsvatantraḥ syādarthagrahaṇavādinām | āgamapratibhāne tu pāratantryaṃ dvayorapi ||
anekapuruṣasthatvādekatraiva ca janmani | grahaṇasmaraṇādvede na svātantryaṃ vihanyate ||
anyathākaraṇe cāsya bahubhyaḥ syānnivāraṇam | ekasya pratibhānaṃ tu kṛtakānna viśiṣyate ||
ataśca sampradāye ca naikaḥ puruṣa iṣyate | bahavaḥ paratantrāḥ syuḥ sarve hyadyatvavannarāḥ ||
evaṃ ca kalpayantyanye yāvadāgamasiddhaye | tāvanna kalpayatyetatsamatvaṃ jaimineḥ paraiḥ ||
na hi dṛṣṭādhikaṃ kiñcitprāmāṇye tena kalpyate | aprāmāṇyanimitteṣu parasyādṛṣṭakalpanā ||
dṛṣṭaprāmāṇyabādhaśca nāstikasya prasajyate | utpanne sati vijñāne balādbādhaprakalpanā ||
sādhite puruṣābhāve nirdoṣajñānajanmanaḥ | pratyakṣānnāstikairvācyo viśeṣaścodanādhiyaḥ ||
upadeśo 'nyathā na syādatīndriyanidandhanaḥ | tasya kartrā na ceddṛṣṭaḥ so 'rtha ityarthakalpanā ||
yadvānumānamevedamupadeśitvamucyate | dṛṣṭārthapūrvatāvyāptam, vyatireko 'sya nanviti ||
anyathāpyupapannatvaṃ vyāmohāditi kathyate | liṅgasya vyabhicāro vā bālavākyanidarśanāt ||
vedājjñātvopadiṣṭaṃ cedityevaṃ siddhasādhanam | vedādapītyanenoktam, manvādeścaitadiṣyate ||
anyathā saṃvidāno 'pi vivakṣatyanyathā yataḥ | tasmādekāntato nāsti puṃvākyāttaddhiyāṃ gatiḥ ||
bhrāntasyānyavivakṣāyāmanyadvākyaṃ ca dṛśyate | yathāvivakṣamapyetattasmānnaiva pravartate ||
vaktṛdhīrāptavākyeṣu gamyate, nyatra viplutiḥ | tenotsargāpavādābhyāṃ vacasaḥ śaktirucyate ||
padārtharacanāyatto vākyārthapratyayodbhavaḥ | vivakṣāpūrvavijñānavaśācca racanākṛtiḥ ||
vivakṣāntarayuktā hi kurvāṇā racanāntaram | āvāpodvāpabhedena dṛśyante 'rtheṣu mānavāḥ ||
tenārthapratyayotpāde śroturjāte 'pi vākyataḥ | jñāto nūnamaneneti vakturjñāne matirbhavet ||
āptoktikāraṇaṃ kañcidanuyuṅkte naraṃ yadā | tadā ca nirdiśatyāptaṃ sa jānātyetadityasau ||
tajjñānāntaritatvācca śabdāstāvadudāsate | prāmāṇyasthāpanaṃ tu syādvaktṛdhīhetusambhavāt ||
arthe pūrvapratīte 'pi niścayo hi tadāśrayaḥ | tenārthajñānagamyāpi prāmāṇye saiva pūrvabhāk ||
ato 'tra puṃnimittatvādupapannā mṛṣārthatā | na tu syāttatsvabhāvatvaṃ vede vakturabhāvataḥ ||
tadbuddhyantarayornāstītyartho 'rthaiśca pratīyate | ato na jñānapūrvatvamapekṣyaṃ nāyathārthatā ||
apramāṇatvasiddhau vā dṛṣṭānto ya udāhṛtaḥ | buddhādivacanaṃ tasya sādhyenāsaṅgatocyate ||
teṣāmapi hi yatkāryaṃ pūrvatra pratipāditam | tatra samyaktvamarthe tu vyāpāro naiva vidyate ||
svavyāpārātirikte 'rthe vedasyāpi mṛṣārthatā | pūrvapakṣārthavattvena prasaktā siddhasādhyatā ||
ajñātvaivamabhiprāyaṃ kṛtakākṛtakatvayoḥ | satyamithyātvahetūktimātrajñānātparo 'bravīt ||
nanu sāmānyatodṛṣṭam, nānyatvādityadūṣaṇam | anyatvādeva dṛṣṭānto na hi pakṣe sapakṣatā ||
tasmādayamabhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasya varṇyate | abhyupetyārthaviṣayaṃ vākyavyāpāramucyate ||
yadi syādvyavadhāne 'pi vākyārthāpekṣayānṛtam | dṛṣṭānto nṛvaco 'trāpi hetuḥ sādhāraṇo bhavet ||
satyeṣvapi hi dṛṣṭaiva pauruṣeyeṣu vākyatā | atīndriye 'pi kiñciddhi satyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yadṛcchayā ||
nānyatvāditi cānena paroktādanyatocyate | anyo hyeṣa tadābhāsaḥ, vipakṣaṃ vānyamabravīt ||
yadvānyasmādvisaṃvādānmithyātvaṃ tatra na tviha | viṣayasyāpi cānyatvātsādhanāsaṅgataiva sā ||
na hyanyasyeti naikasminmṛṣārthe 'nyamṛṣārthatā | vivakṣāyā mṛṣārthatve na ca vākye mṛṣārthatā ||
śyāmatve puṃstvavaccaitatsādhāraṇye nidarśanam | paroktervāpi duṣṭatvādvikalpasamamucyate ||
yadvā pramāṇamevedaṃ samyaktve 'nyatvamucyate | dhiruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ bādho vāpyanumānataḥ ||
codanājanitā buddhiḥ pramāṇaṃ doṣavarjitaiḥ | kāraṇairjanyamānatvālliṅgāptoktyakṣabuddhivat ||
tathānāptāpraṇītoktijanyatvādbādhavarjanāt | deśakālādibhedādau cāptoktipratyayo yathā ||
akartṛkatvasiddhyā ca hetutvaṃ sādhayiṣyate | evamādyavabudhyāyaṃ nānyatvādityavocata ||
pratyakṣastviti dārḍhyaṃ vā prāthamyaṃ vāpi lakṣayet | svarūpataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ mithyātvaṃ pararūpataḥ ||
jñānābhāvaśca mithyātvaṃ dvayasyāsambhavādyadi | pratyakṣaṃ tatpareṣāṃ ca siddhamasyānumānataḥ ||
yathā ca tava mithyātvaṃ sādhanaṃ sādhayedidam | tathā ca bādhakādhīnaṃ mithyātvamapi sādhayet ||
dharma ityupasaṃhārye yacchreyaskarabhāṣaṇam | taddharmapadavācyārthanirūpaṇavivakṣayā ||
śreyo hi puruṣaprītiḥ sā dravyaguṇakarmabhiḥ | codanālakṣaṇaiḥ sādhyā tasmātteṣveva dharmatā ||
anyatsādhyamadṛṣṭvaiva yāgādīnanuniṣṭhataḥ | dhārmikatvasamākhyānaṃ tadyogāditi gamyate ||
paśvādīni ca dharmasya phalānīti vyavasthitam | citrāgodohanādīnāṃ tānyuktāni phalāni ca ||
tasmātteṣveva dharmatvam, dharmāṇīti ca darśanāt | liṅgasaṃkhyāvinirmukto dharmaśabdo nidarśanam ||
antaḥkaraṇavṛttau vā vāsanāyāṃ ca cetasaḥ | pudgaleṣu ca puṇyeṣu nṛguṇe 'pūrvajanmani ||
prayogo dharmaśabdasya na dṛṣṭaḥ, na ca sādhanam | puruṣārthasya te jñātuṃ śakyante codanādibhiḥ ||
na ca vastvantaraṃ śakyamapūrvaṃ svargayāgayoḥ | jñātuṃ sādhanabhūtaṃ vā sādhyaṃ vā nāpyato 'nyathā ||
śrutasādhanasādhyatvatyāgenāśrutakalpanā | prasajyetāsya tādrūpye vyatireke tvarūpatā ||
tasmātphale pravṛttasya yāgādeḥ śaktimātrakam | utpattau vāpi paśvāderapūrvaṃ na tataḥ pṛthak ||
śaktayaḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ bhāvaśabdairviśeṣataḥ | nopākhyāyanta ityevaṃ nāpūrvaṃ dharmaśabdatā ||
purastāccodanāśabdo vidhāveva vyavasthitaḥ | na ca tallakṣaṇā hiṃsā pratyudāharaṇaṃ katham ||
codanālakṣaṇo yaśca śyenādirhi gamyate | niṣedhābhāvatastasya kathaṃ brūyādanarthatā ||
yadyapi syādvidhispṛṣṭe niṣedho naiva tādṛśaḥ | vijñāyate hyanarthatvaṃ ṣoḍaśigrahaṇādivat ||
codanālakṣaṇaṃ coktvā niṣiddhatvādvirudhyate | śyenādāvupadiṣṭe ca hiṃsā hīti na yujyate ||
hiṃsā hi phalameteṣāṃ bhinnā tebhyaḥ svarūpataḥ | sā hi prāṇaviyogātmā śyenastatrāsivatpṛthak ||
upadeśābhidhānaṃ ca nāvidheye 'vakalpate | śyenāderavidhāne ca kasyānyasya vidheyatā ||
sarvatrāvasthito nyāyo bhāvanāṃśadvaye vidhiḥ | sa bādhyeta, iha ye cāmī jyotiṣṭomādayo matāḥ ||
dharmatvena na te 'pi syurhiṃsāsādhanakā hi te | na cāvidhīyamānasya phalatatsādhanāṅgatā ||
sādhanatvena vihitaṃ na cāvihitamucyate | sādhyatvena vidhānaṃ tu naiveṣṭaṃ lokavedayoḥ ||
tenaivamarthaśabdasya prayojanamihocyate | pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yā śabdaśravaṇena dhīḥ ||
sā codaneti sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hṛdaye sthitam | pravartakagṛhītistu syādudāharaṇārthatā ||
tātparye hyarthaśabdasya neyaṃ vyākhyopapadyate | arthagrahaṇalabhyaṃ vā tatpravartakabhāṣaṇam ||
dharme pramāṇabhūtāyāstadvā lakṣaṇamuktavān | evaṃ sati vidhibhyaḥ syādvidheyārthāvadhāraṇam ||
niṣedhebhyo niṣedhyānāmanarthatvena nirṇayaḥ | tenārthagrahaṇenoktā vidheyasyeha dharmatā ||
niṣedhyānāmanarthatvamarthasiddhaṃ na sūtritam | tasmādubhayamityatra vidheyapratiṣedhyayoḥ ||
yāgādibrahmahatyādivargayoḥ syānnidarśanam | śyenādīnāṃ vidheyatvādiṣṭasyāpi ca sādhanāt ||
upacārādanarthatvaṃ phaladvāreṇa varṇyate | pratiṣiddhā hi setyatra sphuṭametatkariṣyate ||
hiṃsā hīti ca yaccāpi brūte nābhicarediti | śyenādīnāṃ svarūpe tu nottaragranthasaṅgatiḥ ||
vihitatvānniṣedhasya pravṛttisteṣu durlabhā | yadā tu codanāśabdo vidhāveva vyavasthitaḥ ||
tadobhayādiko granthaḥ sadhyasādhanasaṃśritaḥ | sādhyasādhanasambandhe vidhinā pratipādite ||
lakṣyamāṇatvamubhayoḥ, dvividhaṃ ca phalaṃ kratoḥ | svargādi prāpyate tatra pratiṣedhānatikramāt ||
atikrameṇa hiṃsādi, śāstrāntaranirīkṣayā | phalāṃśe bhāvanāyāśca pratyayo na vidhāyakaḥ ||
vakṣyate, jaiminiścāha tasya lipsārthalakṣaṇā | tena sāmānyataḥ prāpto vidhinā na nivāritaḥ ||
phalāṃśopanipātinyā hiṃsāyāḥ pratiṣedhakaḥ | anarthaprāptihetutvaṃ bodhyate tatra yadyapi ||
śyenasvarūpaṃ nānarthastatphalasya tvanarthatā | parastūbhayamityādeḥ phalasyāpi vidheyatām ||
bhāvanāntargatatvādvā matvānarthatvamākṣipat | naivetyetāvatā cāsya vidheyatvanirākriyā ||
kiṃ vidheyamidānīṃ syādāha śyenādayastviti | praśnāpākaraṇe cātra tavyo vidhivivakṣayā ||
prayukto na tu sādhye 'rthe, dvaye 'pyanupayogataḥ | anarthasyāpi sādhyatvamavidheyasya hīṣyate ||
sādhyatvarahite ceṣṭā vidheye nityamarthatā | śatuśca lakṣaṇārthatvaṃ teṣāṃ cāpyupadeśanam ||
bruvan sphuṭīkarotīṣṭamupadeśo hi nānyathā | vidhitvamādiśabdātsyāditikartavyatāsvapi ||
tasmātphalāṃśe yā hiṃsā vaidikī sā niṣidhyate | aṃśadvaye tu yā nāma tanniṣedhābhidhāyinām ||
aviśeṣeṇa yacchāstraṃ śirovaditi cottaram | niṣedhenānavaṣṭabdhe viṣaye na hyanarthatā ||
pratyakṣāderaśakyatvātkalpyate niṣpramāṇikā | na hi hiṃsādyanuṣṭhāne tadānīṃ doṣadarśanam ||
bāhye 'pi vicikitsā tu śāstrādevopajāyate | hiṃsyamānasya duḥkhitvaṃ dṛśyate yanna tāvatā ||
karturduḥkhānumānaṃ syāt, tadānīṃ tadviparyayaḥ | viṣaye 'syāḥ phalaṃ yādṛkpretya kartustathāvidham ||
hiṃsā kriyāviśeṣatvātsūte śāstroktadānavat | ya evamāha, tasyāpi gurustrīgamanādibhiḥ ||
surāpānādibhiścāpi vipakṣairvyabhicāritā | viruddhatā ca, yādṛgdhi dānaistādṛkphalaṃ bhavet ||
vidhigamyaphalāvāptiḥ, aduḥkhātmakatā tathā | na ca yā sampradānasya prītistādṛkphalaṃ śrutam ||
dātustena hi dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhyahīnaḥ pratīyate | sampradānaṃ ca dāne te viṣayaḥ karma hiṃsane ||
vaiṣamyam, sampradāne tu pakṣe tvetadviruddhatā | prīyate sampradānaṃ hi devateti mataṃ tava ||
dṛṣṭānte karma dānaṃ cet, tasya kīdṛkphalaṃ bhavet | japahomādidṛṣṭāntātparapīḍādivarjanāt ||
coditatvasya hetutvādviruddhāvyabhicāritā | vihitapratiṣiddhatve muktvānyanna ca kāraṇam ||
dharmādharmāvabodhasya tenāyuktānumānagīḥ | anugrahācca dharmatvaṃ pīḍātaścāpyadharmatām ||
vadato japasīdhvādipānādau nobhayaṃ bhavet | krośatā hṛdayenāpi gurudārābhigāminām ||
bhūyāndharmaḥ prasajyeta bhūyasī hyupakāritā | anumānapradhānasya pratiṣedhānapekṣiṇaḥ ||
hṛdayakrośanaṃ kasmāddṛṣṭāṃ pīḍāmapaśyataḥ | poḍātaścāpyadharmatvaṃ tathā pīḍāmadharmataḥ ||
anyonyāśrayamāpnoti vinā śāstreṇa sādhayan | evamādāvaśāstrajñomleccho nodvijate kva cit ||
tasya nādharmayogaḥ syātpūrvoktā yadi kalpanā | tasmādanugrahaṃ pīḍāṃ tadabhāvamapāsya ca ||
dharmādharmārthibhirnityaṃ mṛgyau vidhiniṣedhakau | kva cidasyā niṣiddhatvāc chaktiḥ śāstreṇa bodhitā ||
pratyavāyanimittatve vidhinā nāpagacchati | śāstreṇa na hi śaktīnāmāvāpodvāpanakriyāḥ ||
vidyamānā hi kathyante śaktayo dravyakarmaṇām | tadeva cedaṃ karmeti śāstramevānudhāvatā ||
hiṃsādīnāmadharmatvaṃ kathyate nānumānataḥ | evaṃ ye nipuṇaṃ prāhustairapyetatparīkṣyatām ||
surāpānādibhiḥ śūdraḥ kiṃ yāti narakaṃ kṛtaiḥ | vaiśyastomena vā kiṃ syādviprarājanyayoḥ phalam ||
pañcamyāmiṣṭikaraṇānmadhyāhne cāgnihotrataḥ | tasmādyadyādṛśaṃ karma yatphalotpattiśaktikam ||
śāstreṇa gamyate tasya tādṛśasyaiva tatphalam | hiṃsā cāṃśadvayādanyā yā tasyāḥ pratiṣedhajam ||
pratyavāyārthatājñānam, vidhinānyatra vāryate | jñānameva ca śaktīnāṃ nāvāpodvāpanakriyāḥ ||
jñāyante śāstratastāstu kriyābhedavyavasthitāḥ | vyavasthāḥ śaktibhedānāṃ dṛṣṭārtheṣvapi karmasu ||
abhinnatve 'pi dṛśyante bhujeḥ svasthātureṣvapi | rūpābhede 'pi hiṃsāderbhedo 'ṅgānaṅgakāritaḥ ||
tathāpyekaphalatvaṃ cetkriyātvātsarvasaṅkaraḥ | yajitvādyaviśeṣācca citrādiphalatulyatā ||
bhedāttatra vyavasthā cedihāpyevaṃ bhaviṣyati | vidhīnāṃ vāpi sarveṣāṃ sākṣādvyavahito 'pi vā ||
puruṣārthaḥ phalaṃ tena nānartho 'taḥ pratīyate | na caiṣu śrūyate 'narthaḥ, niṣedhānna ca kalpyate ||
na ca prakaraṇasthatvātpuruṣārthaḥ phalaṃ bhavet | karmopakāraḥ kalpyastu dṛṣṭo 'dṛṣṭo 'tha vā punaḥ ||
kalpanāvasarastatra nānarthasyānapekṣaṇāt | kratvarthaścāpi saṃskāraḥ paśornārādupakriyā ||
dṛṣṭaiva tvavadānānāṃ niṣpattiḥ kratvapekṣitā | abhicāre 'pyupāyasthā hiṃsā nādharma ucyate ||
tasmādanaṅgabhūtāyāṃ hiṃsāyāmetaducyate | uddeśācca phalatvena śyenādau na vidhīyate ||
bhāvanāvidhirapyeva phalāṃśādvinivartate | ataḥ svato na dharmatvaṃ śyenādernāpyadharmatā ||
phalānarthānubandhitvāttaddvāreṇopacaryate | nirākāṅkṣasya caikena śyenasya na phaladvayam ||
tasmātkriyāntarādeva hiṃsāto 'nartha ucyate | phalato 'pi ca yatkarma nānarthenānubadhyate ||
kevalaprītihetutvāttaddharmatvena hīṣyate | nanu ceṣṭābhyupāyatvāt śyenāderdharmatā bhavet ||
phalaṃ tāvadadharmo 'sya śyenādeḥ sampradhāryate | yadi yeneṣṭasiddhiḥ syādanuṣṭhānānubandhinī ||
tasya dharmatvamucyeta tataḥ śyenādivarjanam | yadā tu codanāgamyaḥ kāryākāryānapekṣayā ||
dharmaḥ prītinimittaṃ syāttadā śyene 'pi dharmatā | yadi tvaprītiheturyaḥ sākṣādvyavahito 'pi vā ||
so 'dharmaścodanārthaḥ syāttadā śyene 'pyadharmatā | yastu hiṃsātvasādharmyādbāhyavaccodanāsvapi ||
vadedanarthahetutvaṃ tasyāpyāgamabādhanam | tamanādṛtya yo brūyādyāgāderapyasau vadet ||
svargādisādhanāśaktiṃ kriyātvādbhojanādivat | gītāmantrārthavādairyā kalpyate 'narthahetutā ||
pratyakṣaśrutibādhyatvātsānyārthatvena nīyate | śiṣyān pratyaviśiṣṭatvātsūtravaidikavākyayoḥ ||
aśakteścobhayoḥ sāmyānna sūtreṣvityanuttaram | prāguktaparisaṃkhyāyāḥ phalametatprakāśyate ||
sūtreṣu hyanayā yuktyā gatireṣāpi yujyate | tasmādāvartate sūtram, tantraṃ vā śaktibhedataḥ ||
ekadeśānumānādvā dve sūtre parikalpite | itaretarasāmīpyādetāveva parasparam ||
kalpyete vākyaśeṣāya nānyāvayavakalpanā | viśiṣṭārthānuvāditvādatha vetyapi bhāṣite ||
vākyabhedaḥ sa eveti saṃjñātantratvamuttaram | arthaṃ vā pratyupādānātsaṃjñālakṣaṇaśabdayoḥ ||
tantraṃ lakṣaṇaśabdo vā vācyo dharmārthaśabdayoḥ | dharme sāmānyataḥ siddhe pramāṇaṃ kathyate yadā ||
vṛttameva tadārthatvaṃ kimarthaṃ punarucyate | codanālakṣaṇatvasya dharmaṃ prati vidheyatā ||
labhyate 'rthānuvādena saṃśayo hyanyathā bhavet | tathā ca ye 'pyanarthasya sādhanatvena kalpitāḥ ||
niṣedhaiste 'pi dharmāḥ syuścodanālakṣaṇatvataḥ | tasmādarthāparityāgādekārthagrahaṇaṃ yathā ||
labhyate vacanavyaktyā sā syādarthānuvādataḥ | viśeṣaṇādvinā caitadarthasāmarthyakāritam ||
kathyate bhāṣyakāreṇa phalaṃ hiṃsādivarjanam ||

§ 3 nimittasūtra nms

pratijñāvyatirekeṇa bhāṣyakāreṇa yadyapi | vakṣyamāṇā svapakṣasya yuktiḥ pūrvaṃ nidarśitā ||
pratijñāmātramityetajjaiminermatamucyate | vṛttikāro 'dhikaṃ vāpi bhūtādi dvāramabravīt ||

§ 4 pratyakṣasūtra pas

varṇyate sūtrabhedena yena pratyakṣalakṣaṇam | tena sūtrasya sambandho vācyaḥ pūrvapratijñayā ||
lakṣaṇasyābhidhānaṃ tu kenāṃśenopayujyate | kimarthaṃ cānumānāderlakṣaṇaṃ nātra kathyate ||
na tāvadapramāṇatvaṃ teṣāṃ nāpyakṣabuddhiṣu | śakyate 'ntargatirvaktuṃ na ca lakṣaṇatulyatā ||
na cāpi siddhireṣāṃ syādarthātpratyakṣalakṣaṇāt | na hi tatpūrvakaṃ sarvaṃ pramāṇamiti niścitam ||
pratyakṣalakṣaṇoktiśca nānumānādilakṣaṇāt | vinā na sidhyatītyevamarthākṣepo na yujyate ||
tadetatpūrvakatve dhīrna ca tallakṣaṇādbhavet | taduktervānumānādi kiṃ na syāttadapūrvakam ||
na ca lakṣaṇabhedasya svarūpe yattayorapi | pratyakṣalakṣaṇādeṣāṃ kathañcidavadhāraṇā ||
prasiddhatvādavācyatvaṃ pratyakṣe 'pi prasajyate | tenānyaparisaṃkhyārthaṃ sūtraṃ mūḍhena vocyate ||
na tvekaṃ lakṣayedeṣu buddhipūrvaṃ kathañcana | sambhavatyekavākyatve vākyabhedaśca neṣyate ||
na cāpyetena sūtreṇa pratyakṣaṃ lakṣyate sphuṭam | tadābhāse 'pi tulyatvāt, svapnajñānaikavarjanāt ||
taddhīndriyārthasambandhavyāpāreṇa vinā bhavet | kena citsamprayoge tu bhrāntyādi syānniyogataḥ ||
grāhyeṇānyena vetyetatkṛtaṃ naiva viśeṣaṇam | samprayogasya yena syādviśeṣo vakṣyamāṇavat ||
asāmarthya ca matvāsya vṛttikāreṇa lakṣaṇe | tatsamprayoga ityevaṃ pāṭhāntaramṛdāhṛtam ||
tenānyenāpi saṃyoge cakṣurāderyadutthitam | viṣayāntaravijñānaṃ tatpratyakṣaṃ prasajyate ||
satsamprayoganirdeśo vyarthaśced, etadeva hi | pratipādyaṃ parasyāpi lakṣaṇāsiddhireva ca ||
svapnādīnāṃ nivṛttirvā phalaṃ tasya bhaviṣyati | tasmādvidhyanuvāditvaṃ nānukte lakṣaṇe bhavet ||
tena naiṣā vacovyaktiryatsatīndriyasaṅgame | vijñānaṃ jāyate tasya pratyakṣatvaṃ pratīyatām ||
pratyakṣaṃ yajjane siddhaṃ tasyaivandharmakatvataḥ | vidyamānopalambhatvaṃ tena dharme nimittatā ||
evaṃlakṣaṇatvaṃ ca na svarūpavivakṣayā | evaṃliṅgakamityetadbhāṣyakāreṇa varṇyate ||
yato 'sti tatra dharmo 'yaṃ vidyamānopalambhanam | tasmāttena prasiddhena gamyatāmanimittatā ||
pratyakṣatvamado hetuḥ śeṣaṃ hetuprasiddhaye | asmādādau prasiddhatvādyogyarthamabhidhīyate ||
prakṛtena ca sambandhaḥ śeṣāprāmāṇyadarśanāt | tadaprāmāṇyasiddhiśca sambandhāderanīkṣaṇāt ||
śakyamanyāpramāṇatvamiti sūtrairna paṭhyate | na ca paryanuyogo 'tra lakṣaṇānupayogataḥ ||
na ca nyūnātirekādiprasaṅgo lakṣaṇaṃ prati | sarvathā lokasiddhatvāddharmo 'yaṃ tāvadiṣyate ||
tataśca mṛgatṛṣṇādi na pratyakṣaṃ prasajyate | animittaprasaṅgastu tasyāpi na nivāryate ||
atītānāgate 'pyarthe sūkṣme vyavahite 'pi ca | pratyakṣaṃ yogināmiṣṭaṃ kaiścinmuktātmanāmapi ||
vidyamānopalambhatvamasiddhaṃ tatra tān prati | bhaviṣyattvasya vā hetor tadgrāhyairvyabhicāritā ||
mā bhūtāmiti tenāha lokasiddhaṃ sadityayam | na lokavyatiriktaṃ hi pratyakṣaṃ yogināmapi ||
pratyakṣatvena tasyāpi vidyamānopalambhanam | satsamprayogajatvaṃ vāpyasmatpratyakṣavadbhavet ||
teṣāmavartamāne 'rthe vā nāmotpadyate matiḥ | pratyakṣaṃ sā tatastveva nābhilāṣasmṛtādivat ||
loke cāpyaprasiddhatvātpratyakṣatvapramāṇataḥ | pratibhāvaddvayāsattvaṃ sadityetena kathyate ||
laukikī pratibhā yadvatpratyakṣādyanapekṣiṇī | na niścayāya paryāptā tathā syādyogināmapi ||
avidyamānasaṃyogātsyāccetpratyakṣadhīḥ kva cit | bhaviṣyatyapi dharme syāc chaktetyāha sadityayam ||
pratyakṣaḥ prāganuṣṭhānānna dharmo 'nuṣṭhito 'pi vā | phalasādhanarūpeṇa tadānīṃ yena nāstyasau ||
asmatpratyakṣavaccāpi vidyamānopalambhanam | pratyakṣaṃ dhyāyināṃ dharme pratyakṣatvācca neṣyate ||
avidyamānasaṃyogātpratyakṣatvanirākṛtiḥ | yogināṃ kena labhyeta neṣṭaṃ sadgrahaṇaṃ yadi ||
saptamyāpi tu labhyeta sadarthaḥ, kalpanā punaḥ | pareṣāṃ vāraṇīyeti yatno jaimininā kṛtaḥ ||
samyagarthe ca saṃśabdo duṣprayoganivāraṇaḥ | prayoga indriyāṇāṃ ca vyāpāro 'rtheṣu kathyate ||
duṣṭatvāc chuktikāyogo vāryate, rajatekṣaṇāt | evaṃ satyanuvādatvaṃ lakṣaṇasyāpi sambhavet ||
tataścāprāpyakāritvādyadbauddhaiḥ śrotracakṣuṣoḥ | lakṣaṇāvyāptisiddhyarthaṃ saṃyogo neti kīrtyate ||
prāpyagrahaṇapakṣe hi sāntarāgrahaṇaṃ kila | adhiṣṭānādhikaścārtho na gṛhyeta tvagādivat ||
vyāpāramātravācitvādaviruddhaṃ tadatra naḥ | yadi vārthārjavasthānaṃ samprayogo 'tra varṇyate ||
yogyatālakṣaṇo vācyaḥ saṃyogaḥ kāryalakṣitaḥ | sāṃkhyādīnvā vinirjitya prāptipakṣo 'tra dūṣyatām ||
tayośca prāpyakāritvamindriyatvāttvagādivat | ke cittayoḥ śarīrācca bahirvṛttiṃ pracakṣate ||
cikitsādiprayogaśca yo 'dhiṣṭhāne prayujyate | so 'pi tasyaiva saṃskāra ādheyasyopakārakaḥ ||
taddeśaścāpi saṃskāraḥ sarvavyāptyartha ucyate | cakṣurādyupakāraśca pādādāvapi dṛśyate ||
tasmānnaikāntataḥ śakyaṃ saṃskārāttatra vartanam | bahirvṛttistayośceṣṭā pṛthvagrā santatāpi ca ||
adhiṣṭhānādhikaṃ tena gṛhyate yatra yādṛśam | pṛthutvaṃ vṛttibhāge syād, dūre 'pi grahaṇaṃ tathā ||
dīpaprabhā yathā tasminvinaśyati vinaśyati | tathā bahirgatāpyeṣā mūlacchedādvinaśyati ||
adhiṣṭhānapidhāne tu satyapyucchinnayatnayā | tayārtho 'nupanītatvādātmanā nānubhūyate ||
vicchinna iti buddhiḥ syādadhiṣṭhānamapekṣya ca | śabde tvādhikyavicchedau bhrāntyaivoktāvasambhavāt ||
puruṣendriyaśabdau ca vyavadhānena kalpitau | puruṣo laukiko vā syādyo vāsmin sādhayiṣyate ||
vikriyā jñānarūpāsya na nityatve virotsyate | buddhijanmeti cāpyāha jāyamānapramāṇatām ||
vyāpāraḥ kārakāṇāṃ hi dṛṣṭo janmātirekataḥ | pramāṇe 'pi tathā mā bhūditi janma vivakṣyate ||
na hi tatkṣaṇamapyāste, jāyate vāpramātmakam | yenārthagrahaṇe paścādvyāpriyetendriyādivat ||
tena janmaiva viṣaye buddhervyāpāra iṣyate | tadeva ca pramārūpaṃ tadvatī karaṇaṃ ca dhīḥ ||
janma cāvyatirekeṇa bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇitam | tacca bhūtabhaviṣyattvātkṛtaṃ buddherviśeṣaṇam ||
yadāpyaulūkyasiddhāntātsamavāyasya janmatā | buddhistatrendriyādhīnā tena pratyakṣamaśnute ||
pramāṇaphalabhāvaśca yayeṣṭaṃ parikalpyatām | sarvathāpyanimittatvaṃ vidyamānopalambhanāt ||
yadvendriyaṃ pramāṇaṃ syāttasya vārthena saṅgatiḥ | manaso vendriyairyoga ātmanā sarva eva vā ||
tadā jñānaṃ phalam, tatra vyāpārācca pramāṇatā | vyāpāro na yadā teṣāṃ tadā notpadyate phalam ||
na ca sarvātmanākṣeṇa sambandho 'rthasya vidyate | yena sarvārthabodhaḥ syāttatpramāṇābhidhāyinām ||
prāptimātraṃ hi sambandho nendriyasyābhyupeyate | mā bhūtkāraṇamātreṇa tvacā rūpāvadhāraṇam ||
yathā pramāṇaniṣpattau yogyatvādindriyārthayoḥ | niyatā saṅgatirhetuḥ phale 'pyevaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
yogasya dvyāśrayatve 'pi bhavatyanyatarāśrayaḥ | vyapadeśaḥ, atha vāpyakṣaṃ tatrāsādhāraṇaṃ bhavet ||
saṃyoge tvātmamanasoḥ syāccedviṣayabhinnatā | pramāṇaphalayoḥ, nāsau, arthe hi vyāpṛtaṃ dvayam ||
athāpyāśraya iṣṭaste na yogādviṣayāntaram | ātmasthatvena vijñānaṃ na bhinnaviṣayaṃ tataḥ ||
prakṛṣṭasādhanatvācca pratyāsatteḥ sa eva naḥ | karaṇaṃ tena nānyatra kārake syātpramāṇatā ||
pramāṇe sarvasaṃyoge doṣo naiko 'pi vidyate | pramāṇaṃ tvindriyaṃ yasya tasyaiko viṣayaḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
pramāṇaphalate buddhyorviśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ | yadā tadāpi pūrvoktā bhinnārthatvanirākriyā ||
viśeṣaṇe tu boddhavye yadālocanamātrakam | prasūte niścayaṃ paścāttasya prāmāṇyakalpanā ||
niścayastu phalaṃ tatra, nāsāvālocite tadā | tadā naiva pramāṇatvaṃ syādarthānavadhāraṇāt ||
hānādibuddhiphalatā pramāṇaṃ cedviśeṣyadhīḥ | upakārādisaṃsmṛtyā vyavāyaścet, iyaṃ phalam ||
viṣayaikatvamicchaṃstu yaḥ pramāṇaṃ phalaṃ vadet | sādhyasādhanayorbhedo laukikastena bādhitaḥ ||
chedane khadiraprāpte palāśe na cchidā yathā | tathaiva paraśorloke cchidayā saha naikatā ||
bhavate bhedahānena rucitā viṣayaikatā | tattyāgena parebhyastu bhedo rucimupāgataḥ ||
karaṇatvopacārastu phale cetkalpyate tvayā | kathañcidviṣayaikatvaṃ parairvā kiṃ na kalpyate ||
paricchedaphalatvena vṛttasyānantarasya naḥ | pramāṇatvaṃ bhavejjñāne pramāṇe tu paraṃ phalam ||
svasaṃvittiphalatvaṃ tu tanniṣedhānna yujyate | pramāṇe viṣayākāre bhinnārthatvānna yujyate ||
svākāraśca svasaṃvittiṃ muktvā nānyaḥ pratīyate | prāmāṇyaṃ yasya kalpyeta svasaṃvittiphalaṃ prati ||
svākārasya paricchedo na cākārāntarādvinā | tasyāpyevaṃ tathā ca syānnākārāntaḥ kadā cana ||
na cāsañcetitaḥ sattāṃ svākāraḥ pratipadyate | grāhye ca viṣayākāre grāhako 'nyo na labhyate ||
manasastvindriyatvena pratyakṣā dhīḥ sukhādiṣu | manasā samprayukto hi tānyātmā pratipadyate ||
sambaddhaṃ vartamānaṃ ca grahyate cakṣurādinā | sāmānyaṃ vā viśeṣo vā grāhyaṃ nāto 'tra kalpyate ||
lakṣaṇaṃ yacca yairuktaṃ pratyakṣe laukike sati | vidyamānopalambhitvātsarvasyaivānimittatā ||
nirvikalpakapakṣe tu sutarāmanimittatā | sādhyasādhanasambandho nāvikalpya hi gṛhyate ||
kathaṃ pratyakṣapūrvatvamanumānādi no bhavet | yadā smṛtyasamarthatvānnirvikalpendriyasya dhīḥ ||
na cāvikalpya liṅgasya liṅgisambandhayostathā | gṛhītiḥ, upamāne 'pi sādṛśyagrahaṇātsmṛteḥ ||
arthāpattiḥ punaḥ prāyo nānyadṛṣṭe 'rtha iṣyate | pravartate ca yaṃ dṛṣṭvā so 'pyarthaḥ savikalpakaḥ ||
yatra cānumitaṃ liṅgaṃ sūryagatyādi liṅgi ca | tatra pratyakṣapūrvatvaṃ kathamadhyavasīyate ||
pratyakṣāvagate cārthe kutasteṣāṃ pramāṇatā | tairyadā sa pratīyeta tadā nākṣasya gocaraḥ ||
atha kasya cidarthasya jñānāttatpūrvatā bhavet | tadārthasya bhaviṣyattvaṃ na syādajñānakāraṇam ||
vartamāne hi kasmiṃścidvijñāte 'rthe 'kṣabuddhibhiḥ | liṅgādavidyamāno 'pi dharmo gamyeta taistadā ||
pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā ca varṇānvede 'pi gṛhyate | prameyamiti so 'pi syāttatpūrvatvādakāraṇam ||
ke cittatpūrvakatvaṃ tu heturnaiveti manvate | tatpūrvakatvādyattāvatprāmāṇyaṃ tadasambhavaḥ ||
pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā ca, liṅgādyanyatamaṃ dhruvam | pravṛttiranumānāderna ca dharme 'sti tādṛśam ||
anumānānumānāderna cāpyastīha sambhavaḥ | sambandhaliṅgiliṅgānāṃ pūrvasiddherasambhavāt ||
sattā ca nānumānena kasya citpratipadyate | dharmeṇānyadviśeṣyaṃ cet, pakṣo 'siddhaviśeṣaṇaḥ ||
tasmādadṛṣṭapūrvatvātkena cidvastunā saha | dharmasya nānumeyatvamasādhāraṇavastuvat ||
adṛṣṭasadṛśatvācca svayaṃ cānupalambhanāt | dharmasya nopameyatvamasādhāraṇavadbhavet ||
nanvarthāpattirevaṃ syājjagadvaicitryadarśanāt | sukhiduḥkhādibhedo hi nādṛṣṭātkāraṇādṛte ||
dṛṣṭasya vyabhicāritvāttadabhāve 'pi sambhavāt | sevāvyayanatulyatve dṛṣṭā ca phalabhinnatā ||
syādevaṃ yadi śakyeta svābhāvikanivāraṇā | karmaśakteśca vaicitrye heturanyo bhavedyadi ||
yathā ca phalavaicitrye karmaṇāṃ śaktatā svataḥ | tathā ca citratā loke svabhāvādupapatsyate ||
adharme dharmarūpe vā hyavibhakte phalaṃ prati | kimapyastīti vijñānaṃ narāṇāṃ kvopayujyate ||
kiṃ nu yāgādito duḥkhaṃ hiṃsādeḥ kiṃ sukhodbhavaḥ | svargaputrādibhedaśca kīdṛśātkarmabhedataḥ ||
iti yāvadavijñānaṃ tāvannaiva pravartate | pravṛttyaṅgaṃ ca yajjñānaṃ tasya mūlaṃ pratīkṣyate ||
tasmātsiddhe 'pi sāmānye viśeṣo nāgamādṛte | viśeṣasya tu jijñāsā sūtrakāreṇa sūtritā ||
gamyamāne viśeṣe ca tadantarbhāvakāritaḥ | sāmānyapratyayo 'pi syāc chāstrādevetyakāraṇam ||
yathārthāpattirevaṃ ca nānumānopameṣyate | śāstraṃ cettadapekṣeta tasyaiva syātpramāṇatā ||
pratyakṣāgrahaṇaṃ yattu liṅgāderavikalpanāt | tanna, iṣṭatvādvikalpasyāpyartharūpopakāriṇaḥ ||
asti hyālocanā jñānaṃ prathamaṃ nirvikapakam | bālamūkādivijñānasadṛśaṃ śuddhavastujam ||
na viśeṣo na sāmānyaṃ tadānīmanubhūyate | tayorādhārabhūtā tu, vyaktirevāvasīyate ||
mahāsāmānyamanyaistu dravyaṃ saditi cocyate | sāmānyaviṣayatvaṃ ca pratyakṣasyaivamāśritam ||
viśeṣāstu pratīyante savikalpakabuddhibhiḥ | te ca ke citpratidravyaṃ ke cidbahuṣu saṃśritāḥ ||
tānakalpayadutpannaṃ vyāvṛttānugatātmanā | gavyaśve copajātaṃ tu pratyakṣaṃ na viśiṣyate ||
tadayuktam, pratidravyaṃ bhinnarūpopalambhanāt | na hyākhyātumaśakyatvādbhedo nāstīti gamyate ||
nirvikalpakabodhe 'pi dvyātmakasyāpi vastunaḥ | grahaṇam, lakṣaṇākhyeyaṃ jñātrā śuddhaṃ tu gṛhyate ||
na cāsādhāraṇatvena paravyāvṛttyakalpanāt | viśeṣānugamākḷpteḥ sāmānyamiti nāpi tat ||
tataḥ paraṃ punarvastudharmairjātyādibhiryayā | buddhyāvasīyate sāpi pratyakṣatvena sammatā ||
karaṇaṃ cendriyaṃ buddherna tatra jñānamāhitam | tataḥ smṛtyasamarthatvādvikalpo 'to na vāryate ||
ātmanyeva sthitaṃ jñānam, sa hi boddhātra gamyate | smaraṇe cāsya sāmarthyaṃ sandhānādau ca vidyate ||
tenendriyārthasambandhe vicyamāne smarannapi | vikalpayan svadharmeṇa vastu pratyakṣavānnaraḥ ||
taccaitadindriyādhīnamiti tairvyapadiśyate | tadasambandhajātaṃ tu naiva pratyakṣamiṣyate ||
punaḥ punarvikalpe 'pi satī jātiḥ pratīyate | tatsambandhānusāreṇa sarvaṃ pratyakṣamiṣyate ||
na hi praviṣṭamātrāṇāmuṣṇādgarbhagṛhādiṣu | arthā na pratibhāntīti gṛhyante nendriyaiḥ punaḥ ||
yathā tvābhāsamātreṇa pūrvaṃ jñātvā svarūpataḥ | paścāttatrāvabudhyante tathā jātyādidharmataḥ ||
yadi tvālocya saṃmīlya netre kaścidvikalpayet | na syātpratyakṣatā tasya sambandhānanusārataḥ ||
asambaddhavikalpe 'pi tulyamātmādi kāraṇam | tenāsādhāraṇatvaṃ syādatrākṣasyaiva kalpane ||
nirvikalpakabodhe 'pi nākṣaṃ kevalakāraṇam | tatpāramparyajāte vā rūḍhiḥ syātpaṅkajādivat ||
animittaiva vā rūḍhiḥ sutarāṃ savikalpakam | pratyakṣaṃ sammataṃ loke na tathā nirvikalpakam ||
vṛddhaprayogagamyāśca śabdārthāḥ sarva eva naḥ | tena yatra prayukto 'yaṃ na tasmādapanīyate ||
siddhānugamamātraṃ hi kartuṃ yuktaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ | na sarvalokasiddhasya lakṣaṇena nivartanam ||
kalpanāyāḥ svasaṃvittāvindriyādhīnatā katham | manastatrendriyaṃ cetsyādgotvādāvapi tatsamam ||
svasaṃvittau tadiṣṭaṃ cet, loko na hyevamicchati | tasmādrūḍhatvameṣṭavyaṃ pāribhāṣikatāpi vā ||
manasastvindriyatvena sudhaduḥkhādibuddhiṣu | yathā pratyakṣataivaṃ nastadadhīnā bhaviṣyati ||
tadadhīnatvasāmye 'pi kalpanāpoḍhaśabdanāt | pratyakṣaṃ kiñcideveṣṭaṃ yathā tatra tathaiva naḥ ||
liṅgādyabhāvataścāpi nānumānādidhīriyam | bādhakapratyayāsattvānnāprāmāṇyaṃ ca yujyate ||
na ca parvamadṛṣṭatvātsmṛtitvamupapadyate | tasmātpratyakṣamevedam, vyavahārastathaiva ca ||
jātyādyarthāntaraṃ yasmādatadrūpe 'pi vastuni | bhavatyadhyasya dhīstasmānmṛgatṛṣṇādibhiḥ samā ||
naitadaśvādibuddhīnāmadhyāropādyasambhavāt | sthitaṃ naiva hi jātyādeḥ paratvaṃ vyaktito hi naḥ ||
yadi hyekāntato bhinnaṃ viśeṣyātsyādviśeṣaṇam | svānurūpāṃ sadā buddhiṃ viśeṣye janayetkatham ||
sphaṭikādau tu lākṣādisvarūpā yā matirbhavet | avyutpannasya sā mithyā vyutpannānāṃ hi bhedadhīḥ ||
na tu jātyādinirmuktaṃ vastu dṛṣṭaṃ kadā cana | tadvimokena vā tāni lākṣādisphaṭikādivat ||
tatrāpi cenna dṛśyeta bhedaḥ kaiścitkadā cana | raktādibuddhisamyaktvaṃ vinivāryeta kena vā ||
na cāpyayutasiddhānāṃ sambandhitvena kalpanā | nāniṣpannasya sambandhaḥ, niṣpattau yutasiddhatā ||
tathā ca sati sambandhe hetuḥ kaścinna vidyate | tasmāccāpi na sambandhaḥ padārthānāṃ pratīyate ||
samavāyaviyogācca viśleṣaḥ syātparasparam | tatkḷptāvavyavasthā syāttasya tasyānyasaṅgateḥ ||
atha tasyātmarūpatvānnānyasambandhakalpanā | abhedātsamavāyo 'stu svarūpaṃ dharmadharmiṇoḥ ||
na hi sa vyatiriktaḥ san sambandhaṃ pratipadyate | tasmiṃstābhyāmabhinne tu na nānātvaṃ tayorbhavet ||
nanu dharmātirekeṇa dharmiṇo 'nupalambhanāt | tatsaṅghamātra evāyaṃ gavādiḥ syādvanādivat ||
āvirbhāvatirobhāvadharmakeṣvanuyāyi yat | taddharmi yatra vā jñānaṃ prāgdharmagrahaṇādbhavet ||
ato jātyādirūpeṇa dharmi yadgṛhyate naraiḥ | pārarūpyaṃ na tasyāstītyaprāmāṇyaṃ na yujyate ||
yasyāpi vyatirekaḥ syāddharmebhyo dharmiṇaḥ sphuṭaḥ | nityaṃ tasyāpi tādrūpyānna mithyātvaṃ prasajyate ||
yo hyasadrūpasaṃvedyaḥ saṃvedyetānyathā punaḥ | sa mithyā na tu tenaiva yo nityamavagamyate ||
na cānekendriyagrāhyaṃ bhinnatāṃ pratipadyate | mā bhūdbhinnaśarīrasthagrāhyatvādbhinnarūpatā ||
jātyabhedādabhedaścet, indriyatvena tatsamam | tulyabuddherato bhinnā na sattendriyabhedataḥ ||
buddhibhedācca naikatvaṃ rūpādīnāṃ prasajyate | ekānekatvamiṣṭaṃ vā sattārūpādirūpataḥ ||
kva cicca saṅkarānnākṣamekamityavasīyate | dārḍhyadaurbalyabhedena vyavasthāpi yataḥ kva cit ||
yathā hi manasaḥ sārdhaṃ rūpādau cakṣurādinā | pravṛttiḥ sukhaduḥkhādau kevalasyaiva dṛśyate ||
na kva citsaṅkarābhāvātsarvatraiva nivartate | kva cicca saṅkaraṃ dṛṣṭvā saṅkaro 'nyatra kalpyate ||
śrotrāderupaghāte 'pi śabdādismṛtidarśanāt | vartamānasya cājñānādvyavasthā sampratīyate ||
ekaṃ yadi bhavedakṣaṃ sarvairgṛhyeta vā na vā | kalpyate śaktibhedaścet, śaktirevendriyaṃ bhavet ||
śṛṇuyādbadhiraḥ śabdaṃ saṅkare cakṣurādinā | manaso vā svatantratve vartamānārthabuddhiṣu ||
na smaredbadhiraḥ śabdaṃ śrotraṃ cetsmṛtikāraṇam | smṛtivadvā bhavedasya vartamānārthadhīrapi ||
smṛtiśca na bhavetpaścādgṛhṇīyāttanna cenmanaḥ | śrotragrahaṇavelāyām, na cāsarvā smṛtirbhavet ||
bodhātmakatayā puṃsaḥ sarvatra grahaṇaṃ bhavet | yugapadviṣaye 'pyasya karaṇāpekṣitā na cet ||
tasmājjñānānusāreṇa vyavasthāsaṅkarau kva cit | grāhyagrāhakaśaktibhyaḥ kāryadvāreṇa kalpitau ||
cakṣūrūpādibhedastu pañcadhaiva vyavasthitaḥ | tena nīlādibhede 'pi nendriyānantyakalpanā ||
tasmātpañcabhirapyakṣairbodhaḥ sattāguṇatvayoḥ | dravyamūrtau punardvābhyāṃ rūpādāvekaśaḥ sthitaḥ ||
nanu jātyādirūpe 'pi śabdābhedopacārataḥ | pravartamānā mithya syādbuddhī rūpeṣu buddhivat ||
na śabdābhedarūpeṇa buddhirartheṣu jāyate | prākśabdādyādṛśī buddhiḥ śabdādapi hi tādṛśī ||
nanu gotvādirūpeṇa gavākārādibuddhayaḥ | na prākśabdārthasambandhajñānātsanti kadā cana ||
jātyādestatsvarūpaṃ cedaśabdajño 'pi lakṣayet | anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ śabdarūpatvaniścayaḥ ||
yathā rūpādayo bhinnāḥ prākśabdātsvātmanaiva tu | gamyante tadvadevaitatsaṃjñitvaṃ kevalaṃ param ||
na cāvikalpitaḥ śabdāditi vācyo na gṛhyate | tenāgṛhītaśabdo 'pi gotvādīn pratipadyate ||
śrutisaṃsparśabodhe 'pi gotvādīn pratipadyate | vivekādarthaśabdānāṃ cakṣuḥ śrotradhiyā kṛtāt ||
anantadharmake dharmiṇyekadharmāvadhāraṇe | śabdo 'bhyupāyamātraṃ syānnātmādhyāropakāraṇam ||
na copeye 'bhyupāyasya rūpādhyāsaḥ prasajyate | na hi dīpendriyādīnāṃ rūpādhyāropa iṣyate ||
nityaṃ yadi ca gotvādi śabdarūpeṇa gṛhyate | rūpāntaraṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ cedbhedādhyāsau kuto nvimau ||
yadyabhedo na mithyātvam, bhedaścetsyātsvarūpataḥ | nādhyāropaprasaṅgaḥ syādbhrāntyā tvadhyāsakalpanā ||
śabdenaiva ca nirdeśo gṛhīte 'rthe 'vakalpate | gaurityeva ca nirdeśo vācyatadbuddhivādinām ||
nirdeśatulyatāyāṃ ca śrotrā vaktṛsvarūpatā | śabdajñānaprameyeṣu vijñānasyāvasīyate ||
bhrāntihetusamānatve 'pyupāyatvānmatiśrutī | manyate 'rthe samadhyaste nārthādhyāsaṃ tayoḥ punaḥ ||
gotve sāsnādimadrūpāṅgādirūpābhidhāyake | nirākārobhayajñāne saṃvittiḥ paramārthataḥ ||
yadi cābhedarūpeṇa śabdenārthaḥ pratīyate | ekarūpatvamakṣādau devanādeḥ prasajyate ||
syādanakṣanivṛtyā cet, na prākśabdātpratīyate | gavādiṣvapi tulyaṃ cet, nekarūpasya darśanāt ||
traye bibhītakādīnāṃ naikadharmānvayo 'sti hi | śabdaḥ sādhāraṇasteṣāṃ jātiśabdādvilakṣaṇaḥ ||
parasparavibhinnaṃ tu jñāyate 'trākṛtitrayam | tadadhyāse na yujyeta tadrūpasyāvibhāgataḥ ||
bhinnāḥ syurakṣaśabdāścet, nārthe saṃśayadarśanāt | na sāmānyādṛte sa syād, rūpābhedaśca gamyate ||
bhavatyādau ca bhinne 'pi nāmākhyātatvasaṃjñayā | rūpaikatvena cādhyāse tulyārthatvaṃ prasajyate ||
śabdaniṣpattyabhedācca tiṅantārthasya sādhyatā | katham, kathaṃ ca mūrtārtho vācake mūrtivarjite ||
gavāśvaśuklaśabdādervācyarūpānapekṣaṇe | vācakatvavyavasthānaṃ kathaṃ jātiguṇādiṣu ||
vṛkṣaplakṣādiśabdānāṃ tulye bhede ghaṭādibhiḥ | viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ kathamarthānapekṣayā ||
sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca na syadvācakabuddhivat | ekatra copasaṃhāro na buddhyornirvikalpake ||
vastumātre sa cedevaṃ sarveṣāmekavācyatā | bhavedgavādiśabdānāṃ sarvairvastu hi gamyate ||
na cāsādhāraṇe bhede nīlotpalamitīṣyate | na hi śabdapravṛttiḥ syādanyatrānyatra ceṣyate ||
na ca nīlotpalaṃ nāma vastvekaṃ kiñcidiṣyate | śabdārthayoryato bhedo gamyate 'vayavānugaḥ ||
śabdadvayasya cādhyāsaḥ paryāyeṣvapi dṛśyate | ekādhikaraṇāstena syuste nīlotpalādivat ||
na cānavagate pūrvaṃ padamarthe prayujyate | tatra sambandhavelāyāṃ kīdṛśo 'rthaḥ pratīyate ||
tadānīṃ nārtharūpe hi śabdarūpasya sambhavaḥ | na cāsādhāraṇāṃśena sambandhānugamaḥ kva cit ||
tatra pūrvānapekṣatve yadyātmādhyāsaśaktatā | śabdasya prathame 'pi syāc chravaṇe 'dhyastarūpatā ||
mama vācyānabhijñatvānna bhavetsmaraṇaṃ tataḥ | bhavatastvartharūpasya vācakeṣvapi darśanāt ||
yathā tvajñātaśabdānāṃ vācye taddhīrna jāyate | tathaivājñātavācyānāmupalabdhe 'pi vācake ||
tasmānnātīva vācyānāṃ vācakādhīnatā bhavet | smārakatvācca teṣveva pāratantryaṃ pratīyate ||
tena sambandhavelāyāmarthātmā yo 'vasīyate | śabdādapi sa eveti nārtharūpaṃ praṇaśyati ||
pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yāṃ śabdaḥ kurute matim | tādātmyaṃ tasya śabdasya na kathañcitpratīyate ||
karahastādiśabdebhyaḥ śabdarūpasya bhedataḥ | bhinno 'rthaḥ sampratīyeta tadadhyāropakalpane ||
ātmādhyāsastu sādṛśyāduparāgācca dṛśyate | na tāvadarthasādṛśyaṃ śabdasyeha pratīyate ||
na cānurāgaḥ śabdena bhinnadeśasya yujyate | dūrasthapratibimbaṃ ca nārūpasya pratīyate ||
śabdasarvagatatvena yadyarthaprāptirucyate | sarvārthānāṃ bhavec chabdaiḥ sarvairevānurañjanam ||
na ca bhinnendriyagrāhyaṃ kiñcidastyanurāgakṛt | na hi lākṣānurakte 'pi sphaṭike dhīstvagādibhiḥ ||
anumānāgamau mithyā syātāmadhyāsakalpane | nirūpaṇasya mithyātvātsarvābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||
tathāstviti yadi brūyāt, mithyā svavacane sati | kathamevaṃ vadedartho nānṛtāddhi pratīyate ||
śūnyavādottarāccāpi yathārthaṃ buddhiśabdayoḥ | pravṛttirna tu tattantramartharūpaṃ kadā cana ||
tasmātprāgapi ye śabdādbhirnnaikatvādibuddhibhiḥ | gṛhyante sarvadā teṣāṃ paramārthastitā bhavet ||
śabdābhyupāyake 'pyarthe tadabhāve ca yadyapi | arthabuddhirna jāyeta nārthe rūpaṃ praṇaśyati ||
cakṣurāderabhāve hi rūpādyātmā na gṛhyate | svarūpanāśo rūpādestāvanmātreṇa neṣyate ||
sambandhasya ca nityatvānnārthasya syādarūpatā | yugapanna hi sarveṣāmanyākārārthavedanam ||
tadākāre 'pi tadvacced, dvaye sati parīkṣyatām | kiṃ nvarthasyātathābhāvo grahītuḥ kiṃ nvaśaktatā ||
sadasadbhāvayorarthe virodhitvādasambhavaḥ | grahītṛbhedāc chaktatvamaśaktatvaṃ ca yujyate ||
yathāndhānandhayoḥ pārśve rūpasyetyabhidhāsyate | tenārthe dhvanyupāyasya tadhīrnānyasya jāyate ||
devadattādiśabde tu sambandhādyatvadarśanāt | arthasyānityatāyāṃ ca tādrūpyasyāpyanityatā ||
tatrāpyautpattikī śaktistadrūpapratyayaṃ prati | grāhyagrāhakayoriṣṭā niyogasya tvanityatā ||
tatra sarvairatādrūpyaṃ prāṅniyogātpratīyate | teneṣṭameva mithyātvaṃ kaiścidadhyāsakalpane ||
yadā tu yādṛśaḥ piṇḍaḥ pūrvaṃ śabdātpratīyate | tādṛśasmaraṇe hetuḥ śabdastatra yathārthatā ||
niyogātparato vāpi śabdena vyajyatāmiyam | tadgrāhyaśaktirarthasya, pārarūpyaṃ na tāvatā ||
sarvākāraparicchedyaśakte 'rthe vācake 'pi vā | sarvākārārthavijñānasamarthe niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ ||
tatra śabdārthasambandhaṃ pramātuḥ smarato 'pi yā | buddhiḥ pūrvagṛhītārthasandhānādupajāyate ||
cakṣuṣā sannikṛṣṭe 'rthe nāpratyakṣamasau bhavet | viviktā eva te 'pyarthāḥ smṛtipratyakṣagocarāḥ ||
smaryete śabdasambandhau mā bhūtpratyakṣatā tayoḥ | tadapratyakṣabhāvena na tvarthasyāpi vāryate ||
gṛhītamapi gotvādi smṛtispṛṣṭaṃ ca yadyapi | tathāpi vyatirekeṇa pūrvabodhātpratīyate ||
vyaktikālādibhedena tatrāstyavasaro miteḥ | yaḥ pūrvāvagato 'ṃśo 'tra sa na nāma pramīyate ||
idānīn tanamastitvaṃ na hi pūrvadhiyā gatam | na hi smaraṇato yatprāktatpratyakṣamitīdṛśam ||
vacanaṃ rājakīyaṃ vā vaidikaṃ vāpi vidyate | na cāpi smaraṇātpaścādindriyasya pravartanam ||
vāryate kena cinnātastattadānīṃ praduṣyati | tenendriyārthasambandhātprāgūrdhvaṃ vāpi yatsmṛteḥ ||
vijñānaṃ jāyate sarvaṃ pratyakṣamiti gamyatām | vimanaskā yadā ke citsambaddhamapi cendriyaiḥ ||
na budhyante tathā cānye sādṛśyādivimohitāḥ | tatra yo 'rthaṃ vivekena kauśalātsadṛśeṣvapi ||
sūkṣmaṃ vāpi prapadyeta tasya bhrāntirna tāvatā | yathā ṣaḍjādibhedena gāne laukikavaidike ||
vivekenāvagacchanti yeṣāṃ tatsaṃskṛtā matiḥ | gānamātraṃ vijānanti tatrānadhikṛtāstu ye ||
tadajñānānna mithyātvaṃ vaktuṃ śakyaṃ vivekinām | te hi ṣaḍjādiśabdebhyo vināpyeṣaṃ viviktatām ||
yathāvadadhigacchanti, tadvadgotvādivastvapi | saṅkīrṇamarthamātraṃ tu budhyante 'bhyāsavarjitāḥ ||
vivekaṃ pratipadyante ye śabdasmṛtisaṃskṛtāḥ | yathā rūpādimatyarthe yasyaivāsti yadindriyam ||
sa tanmātraṃ gṛhītvānyanna gṛhṇātyanumānataḥ | tathā vivekahetūnāṃ yadā yaṃ pratipadyate ||
tadupeye tadā jñānaṃ vartate tadanugrahāt | tena yāvatpramātāṇāṃ vivekopāyadarśanam ||
na syāttāvadbhavetteṣāṃ vijñānaṃ nirvikalpakam | tasmādyatra prakalpyeta vastu vastvantarātmanā ||
pramāṇābhāsatā tatra na svadharmavikalpane | pratyakṣatvamataḥ siddhaṃ sāmānyasya tathaiva ca ||
sambandhasyeti tatpūrvamanumānādi jāyate | sarvaṃ cāpyanumānādi pratyakṣe nirvikalpake ||
na pravartata ityetadanumāne 'bhidhāsyate | nanvevaṃ sati yāpyagnerdūrādapyauṣṇyakalpanā ||
sāpi pratyakṣameva syādyathā gotvādibuddhayaḥ | pratyāsannataraṃ gotvaṃ pratyakṣatvena sammatam ||
vijñānaṃ nānyadastīti pratyakṣamidameva naḥ | tatrāpyakṣairasambandhaṃ manvānasyopajāyate ||
yadā buddhiḥ, tadā naiva pratyakṣatvena kalpyate | sparśanena tu sambandhe pratyakṣatvena jāyate ||
tasmādyadindriyaṃ yasya grāhakatvena kalpitam | tenaiva sati sambandhe pratyakṣaṃ nānyathā bhavet ||
evaṃ samāne 'pi vikalpamārge yatrākṣasambandhaphalānusāraḥ | pratyakṣatā tasya tathā ca loke vināpyado lakṣaṇataḥ prasiddham ||

§ 5,1 vṛttikāragrantha vkg

pratyakṣādau niṣiddhe 'pi nanu lokaprasiddhitaḥ | dharmādharmau pramāsyete brāhmaṇādivivekavat ||
dhārmikādhārmikatvābhyāṃ pīḍānugrahakāriṇau | prasiddhau hi, tathā cāha pārāśaryo 'tra vastuni ||
idaṃ puṇyamidaṃ pāpamityetasmin padadvaye | ācaṇḍālaṃ manuṣyāṇāmalpaṃ śāstraprayojanam ||
nirmūlāsambhavādatra pramāṇaiḥ saiva mṛgyate | kutaḥ punaḥ pravṛtteti, pratyakṣādi tu vāritam ||
na caitāni parityajya pṛthagloke pramāṇatā | saṃsāramocakādeśca hiṃsā puṇyatvasammatā ||
na paścātpuṇyamicchanti ke cidevaṃ vigānataḥ | mlecchāryāṇāṃ prasiddhatvaṃ na dharmasyopapadyate ||
na cāryāṇāṃ viśeṣo 'sti yāvacchāstramanāśritam | tanmūlārthaprasiddhistu tatprāmāṇye sthite bhavet ||
tasmādabhāvaktrasthau dharmādarmau na śaknuyāt | codanā cetsamuddhartuṃ grastau tenaiva paśyatām ||
upadeśo hi bhavati jñānaṃ tasyeti yojyate | jñāyate yena tajjñānamekādhikaraṇatvataḥ ||
autpattikagirā doṣaḥ kāraṇasya nivāryate | abādho 'nyatirekeṇa, svatastena pramāṇatā ||
sarvasyānupalabdhe 'rthe prāmāṇyaṃ smṛtiranyathā | codanā copadeśaśca vidhiścaikārthavācinaḥ ||
vākyāntare samarthe 'pi kimarthaṃ vidhirāśritaḥ | sādhyasādhanasambandhaḥ sarvākhyāteṣu vidyate ||
sarvavākyeṣu cākhyātaṃ tenākāṅkṣānivartanāt | pravṛttisiddhiricchātaḥ, pratiṣedhāttu varjanam ||
vidhāvanāśrite sādhyaḥ puruṣārtho na labhyate | śrutasvargādibādhena dhātvarthaḥ sādhyatāṃ vrajet ||
vidhau tu tamatikramya svargādeḥ sādhyateṣyate | tatsādhanasya dharmatvamevaṃ sati ca labhyate ||
svapratyayāntarāpekṣā syādanāptanaroktiṣu | āptoktiṣu narāpekṣā nobhayaṃ codanāsu naḥ ||

§ 5.2

ādiśabdo makārāntaḥ, luki kleśena saṅgatiḥ | nañadhyāhriyate sūtre, saṅkarātparicodanā ||
pramāṇalakṣaṇājñānādvyabhicārātparīkṣaṇam | naitatpratyakṣamityevamaparīkṣopasaṃhṛtā ||
tatrānyasyāyathārthatvaṃ pratyakṣe tu yathārthatā | yadābhāsaṃ hi vijñānaṃ tatsaṃyoge tadiṣyate ||
sampūrṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hyetat, tatsatorvyatyayaḥ kṛtaḥ | śobhanārthastu sacchabdaḥ, yadvākhyāhārakalpanā ||
arthāpattyetareṣāṃ ca pratyakṣābhāsalakṣaṇam | bādhakajñānalābho hi pūrvābādhe na sambhavet ||
sa cāstīti, avabodhatve sati nānyonyasaṃśrayam | na cānāgatabādhe ca pūrveṇātmā hi labhyate ||
nimittadoṣabodhena paścādyatrāpyabādhanam | bhavatyeva hi tatrāpi narāntaraviparyayaḥ ||
sarveṣāṃ sarvadā yatra dhīḥ syāttatra na bādhanam | na hi kāraṇaduṣṭatvabuddhistatra balīyasī ||
jātyādiṣu yadā jātā buddhiḥ paścādasambhavāt | nāśyate yuktibhistatra vyaktamanyonyasaṃśrayam ||
svataḥ prāmāṇyataścātra nirṇayo 'stitvabodhanāt | tadrūpapratyayotpattestadasadvādināmapi ||

§ 5,3 nirālambanavāda nav

pramāṇatvāpramāṇatve puṇyapāpādi tatphalam | vidhyarthavādamantrārthanāmadheyādikalpanā ||
sarveṣu lakṣaṇeṣvevaṃ svapramāṇagaṇaiḥ sthitiḥ | vacanavyaktibhedena pūrvasiddhāntapakṣatā ||
karmabhyaḥ phalasambandhaḥ pāralaukyaihalaukike | sarvamityādyayuktaṃ syādarthaśūnyāsu buddhiṣu ||
tasmāddharmārthibhiḥ pūrvaṃ pramāṇairlokasammataiḥ | arthasya sadasadbhāve yatnaḥ kāryaḥ kriyāṃ prati ||
yadā saṃvṛtisatyena sarvametatprakalpyate | jñānamātre 'pi kasmādvo vṛthāgraho 'rthakalpane ||
saṃvṛterna tu satyatvaṃ satyabhedaḥ kuto 'nvayam | satyā cetsaṃvṛtiḥ keyaṃ mṛṣā cetsatyatā katham ||
satyatvaṃ na ca sāmānyaṃ mṛṣārthaparamārthayoḥ | virodhāt, na hi vṛkṣatvaṃ sāmānyaṃ vṛkṣasiṃhayoḥ ||
tulyārthatve 'pi tenaiṣāṃ mithyāsaṃvṛtiśabdayoḥ | vañcanārtha upanyāso lālāvaktrāsavādivat ||
nāstikyaparihārārthaṃ saṃvṛtiḥ, kalpaneti ca | kalpanāpi tvabhinnasya naiva nirvastuke bhavet ||
tasmādyannāsti nāstyeva, yattvasti paramārthataḥ | tatsatyamanyanmithyeti, na satyadvayakalpanā ||
svapnādibhogavaccāpi yopabhogatvakalpanā | tannivṛttyarthameveha paramārthe pravartate ||
na hi svapnasukhādyarthaṃ dharme kaścitpravartate | yādṛcchikatvātsvapnasya tūṣṇīmāsyeta paṇḍitaiḥ ||
paramārthaphalāvāptimicchadbhistena yatnataḥ | pratipattirvidhātavyā yuktibhirbāhyavastuṣu ||
tatrārthaśūnyaṃ vijñānaṃ yogācārāḥ samāśritāḥ | tasyāpyabhāvamicchanti ye mādhyamikavādinaḥ ||
tatra bāhyārthaśūnyatvaṃ tulyaṃ tāvaddvayorapi | nivṛttyāsya tato jñāne tadvatsaṃvṛtikalpanā ||
tasmātsādhāraṇatvena tanmūlatvena cāpyayam | bāhyārthasadasadbhāve yatno bhāṣyakṛtā kṛtāḥ ||
bāhyārthāpahnave 'dvaitamekārthasya parīkṣaṇāt | pramāṇamāśritaścaikastatrāstāṃ yaḥ prameyataḥ ||
pramāṇasthastu mūlatvādihedānīṃ parīkṣyate | prastutaḥ sa dvidhā cātra prathamaṃ tvanumānataḥ ||
pratyakṣabādhane cokte paścāttacchaktyavekṣaṇāt | tatrānumānamāhedaṃ nanviti, asya ca saṅgatiḥ ||
tatsamprayogajaṃ nāma pratyakṣamiti bhāṣitam | tatrendriyārthasambandhabhedo na paramārthataḥ ||
kalpitaḥ samprayogastu svapnādāvapi vidyate | tadatadyogajanyasya vibhāgastena durlabhaḥ ||
mithyātvaṃ yaddvidhaivoktaṃ nāyathetyatra cocyate | sarvasyaiva ca mithyātve kiṃ viśiṣyābhidhīyate ||
stambhādipratyayo mithyā pratyayatvāttathā hi yaḥ | pratyayaḥ sa mṛṣā dṛṣṭaḥ svapnādipratyayo yathā ||
siddhasādhanabhāvo 'ṃśe dṛṣṭāntābhāva eva ca | mā bhūtāmevaśabdaśca vyartho 'śeṣaprasādhane ||
sarva eveti tenātra jāgradbuddhiparigrahaḥ | svāṃśābhyupagamāccāpi bāhyagrāhyanivāraṇam ||
pratyayasyeti sādhyāṃśavyāptahetunidarśanam | hetuścopanayenātra jāgrato 'pīti darśataḥ ||
vipakṣābhāvataścātra vyatireko na kathyate | sāmānyasya ca hetutvātkasmātpakṣaikadeśatā ||
jāgrajjñāne viśeṣo 'yaṃ yataḥ supariniścayaḥ | bāhyālambanasambandho na prasiddhaḥ paraṃ prati ||
tasmādyadbhāṣyakāreṇa dattamuttaramatra tu | vikalpasamatā vā syādvaidharmyasamatāpi vā ||
dṛṣṭatvātpūrvapakṣasya jātyuktiḥ kaiścidāśritā | pratijñādoṣamevāhuḥ ke citpratyakṣabādhanam ||
śakṣyāmo yadi vispaṣṭaṃ svāṃśagrāhyanivāraṇam | tadā te śuddha eva syātpakṣo grāhyanivāraṇaḥ ||
pratyakṣādeśca viṣayo bāhya evāvatiṣṭhate | tanniṣedhakṛtastasya tairbhavetpakṣabādhanam ||
suniścayena caiteṣāṃ bādhakapratyayādṛte | pramāṇābhāsatā nāstītyetasmātkatyate balam ||
duṣṭajñānagṛhītārthapratiṣedho hi yujyate | gṛhītamātrabādhe tu svapakṣo 'pi na sidhyati ||
agrāhyatvācca bhedena viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ | aprasiddhobhayatvaṃ vā vācyamanyatarasya vā ||
vaktṛśrotrośca yajjñānaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ | tannirālambanatvena svavāgbādho dvayorapi ||
sambhavo na ca bhedasya viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ | tasmānnirūpaṇaṃ nāsti pratijñārthasya śobhanam ||
nirālambanatā nāma na kiñcidvastu gamyate | tena yadvyatirekādau praśno naivopapadyate ||
yadyavastu kathaṃ tvasmāṃstvaṃ bodhayitumicchasi | budhyase vā svabuddhyā tvam, kalpitā tvatha sādhyate ||
asataḥ kalpanā kīdṛk, kḷptau vastu prasajyate | kathamiṣṭamabhāve ced, vastu so 'pīti vakṣyate ||
tathā pratyaya ityeṣa karma bhāvādi vā bhavet | bhāvādiṣu virodhaḥ syātkarma cetsiddhasādhanam ||
pratyāyyasya hi rūpādernirālambanateṣyate | avijñānātmakatvena kiñcinnālambate hyasau ||
kartṛtve karaṇatve vā pakṣatvaṃ śabdayorapi | tannirālambanatvena pakṣābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||
pratyāyyena ca bhinnena vinā kartrādyasambhavaḥ | pratyaye tannimitte vā bādhaḥ svavacanena te ||
athāpi rūḍhirūpeṇa pratyayaḥ syāttathāpi tu | grāhakaṃ vastu siddhaṃ naḥ pratyayo 'nyasya vastunaḥ ||
tamabhyupetya pakṣaścedabhyupetaṃ virudhyate | viśeṣyasyāprasiddhaśca tava, asmākamatādṛśe ||
ātmadharmasvatantratvakalpane 'pi tathā bhavet | na ca pratyayamātratvaṃ kiñcidastyanirūpaṇāt ||
śabdārthamātrarūpeṇa yathānyeṣāṃ nirūpaṇam | tathā ca bhavato na syādvācyabhedamanicchataḥ ||
nirālambanatā cāpi sarvathā yadi sādhyate | viśeṣaṇāprasiddhiśca dṛṣṭāntaśca na vidyate ||
kena ciccetprakāreṇa nirālambanatocyate | rasajñānasya rūpādiśūnyatvātsiddhasādhanam ||
atha buddhiryadākārā tadālambanavāraṇam | svākārasyābhyupetatvāttadabhāvo virudhyate ||
bāhyānālambanatve 'pi bāhya ityagraho yadi | stambhādau naiva tadbuddhirityevaṃ siddhasādhanam ||
atha stambhādirūpeṇa nirālambanatocyate | saṃvedanasya dṛṣṭatvāttadvirodhaḥ prasajyate ||
dvicandrādiṣu tulyaścet, nendriyāprāptito hi naḥ | tatrānālambanoktiḥ syānnārthasaṃvittyabhāvataḥ ||
sarvatrārthendriyāṇāṃ naḥ saṃyogasadasattayā | saṃvittau vidyamānāyāṃ sadasadgrāhikā sthitiḥ ||
bhavatastvindriyādīnāmabhāvādgrahaṇādṛte | nālambanasya hetuḥ syānniṣedho 'to na yujyate ||
bahirbhāvāprasiddhatvāttenānālambanā matiḥ | kathañcitsādhyate naiṣa pakṣo hi jñāyate tadā ||
yathānyabodhanāśakternāprasiddhe viśeṣaṇe | pakṣasiddhistathaiva syādviśeṣaṇaviśeṣaṇe ||
nāprasiddhe padārthe hi vākyārthaḥ sampratīyate | tatpūrvakatvātpakṣaśca vākyārthaḥ sthāpayiṣyate ||
paryudāse niṣedhe vā vyatiriktasya vastunaḥ | prameyatvādyabhedena jagataḥ siddhasādhanam ||
yadi cātyantabhedena nirālambanatocyate | kathañciccedvirudhyeta prākpakṣaḥ kalpitena ||
vastvādyākārataścāpi dhīrnirālambaneṣyate | grāhakāccedabhinnatvaṃ śaktibhedo virudhyate ||
nirālambanabuddheśca yadyutpattiḥ prasādhyate | dṛṣṭatvātseṣyate 'smābhirbāhyagrāhyavivarjitā ||
samyaktvaṃ punaretasyāstvaṃ necchasi kathañcana | ātmāṃśe 'vasitā hyeṣā mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhivat ||
caitrādipratyayānāṃ ca nirālambanatā yadi | dharmabhūtā na gṛhyeta sādhanotthitayā dhiyā ||
tato viṣayanānātvātpratiyogyanirākṛtā | rūpātsālambanaprāptiḥ satī kena nivāryate ||
yadi pratyayaśabdo 'pi pratyayatvena gṛhyate | saṃvittyālambanatvaṃ ca vāryate, siddhasādhanam ||
buddhyutpādanaśaktiścedvāryā, sādhyaṃ na sidhyati | sādhanasya prayogo 'tra bodhakatvādvinā na te ||
na cābhidhāstyasambandhādṛte bhedācca nāstyasau | na cāsau tadgataṃ bhedaṃ bodhayantya dhiyā vinā ||
prāśnikairagṛhīte ca vākyasyāvayave pṛthak | pakṣe hetau ca dṛṣṭānte vādini prativādini ||
sādhanasyāprayogaḥ syādabhyupetyocyate yadi | pūrvābhyupagamenaiva pratijñā bādhyate tataḥ ||
dharmādharmādibhede ca nāsiddhe paramārthataḥ | śiṣyātmanośca dharmāderupadeśo 'vakalpate ||
tadanuṣṭhānato buddheriṣṭo bhedaḥ, sphuṭaṃ ca taiḥ | sūtrāntare 'bhyupetatvādbhavedāgamabādhanam ||
sarvalokaprasiddhyā ca pakṣabādho 'tra te dhruvam | kṛtsnasādhanabuddhiśca yadi mithyeṣyate tataḥ ||
sarvābhāvo yatheṣṭaṃ vā nyūnatā vābhidhīyate | teṣāṃ sālambanatve vā tairanaikāntiko bhavet ||
tadanyasya pratijñā cet, tadanyapratyayo mṛṣā | tanmithyātvaprasaṅge ca sarvaṃ pūrva na sidhyati ||
stambhādisādhanajñānabhedo na hi tathā bhavet | yāvadyāvatpratijñeyaṃ tadaṅgasya pratīyate ||
tāvattāvatpareṣāṃ syānmithyātvādanyabādhanam | viruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ bādho vāpyanumānataḥ ||
itthaṃ sarveṣu pakṣeṣu vaktavyaṃ pratisādhanam | bāhyārthālambanā buddhiriti samyakca dhīriyam ||
bādhakāpetabuddhitvādyathā svapnādibādhadhīḥ | sāpi mithyeti cedbrūyāt, svapnādīnāmabādhanāt ||
tasmātsādharmyadṛṣṭānto bhavataḥ sādhane na hi | vijñānāstitvabhinnatvakṣaṇikatvādidhīstathā ||
samyakcedabhyupeyeta tadānaikāntiko bhavet | tanmithyābhyupapattau ca pakṣabādhaḥ prasajyate ||
tathā ca baddhamuktādivyavasthā na prakalpate | tataśca mokṣayatnasya vaiphalyaṃ vaḥ prasajyate ||
vikalpotpadyamānā ca jñānāstitvādidhīryadi | mṛṣeṣṭā, na ca dṛṣṭātra pramāṇāntarato gatiḥ ||
pramāṇābhāvatastena jñānāstitvādi durlabham | sarvaṃ cāpyasmadādīnāṃ mithyā jñānaṃ vikalpanāt ||
sānnidhyaviprakṛṣṭatve sattvāsattve ca durlabhe | mithyājñānāviśeṣe 'pi sāṃkhyādiparivarjanāt ||
bauddhadarśana ekasmin pakṣapāto na yujyate | mṛṣātvaṃ yadi buddheḥ syādbādhaḥ kiṃ nopalabhyate ||
bādhādvināpi taccetsyādvyavasthā na prakalpate | pratiyogini dṛṣṭe ca jāgrajjñāne mṛṣā bhavet ||
svapnādibuddhirasmākaṃ tava bhedo 'pi kiṅkṛtaḥ | na cānyatpratiyogyasti jāgrajjñānasya śobhanam ||
yaddarśanena mithyātvaṃ stambhādipratyayo vrajet | svapnādipratiyogitvaṃ sarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ ||
tadīyadharmavaidharmyādbādhakapratyayo yathā | yogināṃ jāyate buddhirbādhikā pratiyoginī ||
jāgratstambhādibuddhīnāṃ tataḥ svapnāditulyatā | prāptānāṃ tāmavasthāṃ ca sarvaprāṇabhṛtāmapi ||
bādho 'yaṃ bhavitā tena siddhā sapratiyogitā | iha janmani keṣāñcinna tāvadupalabhyate ||
yogyavasthāgatānāṃ tu na vidmaḥ kiṃ bhaviṣyati | yogināṃ cāsmadīyānāṃ tvaduktapratiyoginī ||
tvaduktiviparītā vā bādhabuddhirbhaviṣyati | īdṛktve yogibuddhīnāṃ dṛṣṭānto na tavāsti ca ||
dṛṣṭāntastvasmadādīnāṃ yo gṛhītaḥ sa vidyate | atha stambhādibuddhīnāṃ vadetsapratiyogitām ||
bādhyatvaṃ cāpi buddhitvānmṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhivat | iṣṭaṃ sapratiyogitvaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhibhiḥ ||
tadātmanā ca bādhyatvaṃ grāhyāntaratayāpi ca | bādhakaiścāpyanekāntaḥ, tadanyatve ca pūrvavat ||
mithyādhīpratiyogitvaṃ svapnādāviva te bhavet | rāgādikṣayayogitvanimittādhigatistathā ||
yāvānviśeṣa iṣṭaścetsarvābhāvādviruddhatā | mahājanasya vā bādhādivānīmbādhabuddhivat ||
vācyo 'numānabādho vā yadi vā pratisādhanam | pūrvasādhanadoṣāśca sandheyāḥ, tasya cādhunā ||
sādhyābhedādavācyatvādhetornobhayasiddhatā | pratyayatvaṃ ca, sāmānyaṃ bhinnābhinnaṃ na vidyate ||
bhavato 'tyantabhinnaṃ ca matpakṣe 'pi kathañcana | sārūpyānyanivṛttī ca netyetatsādhayiṣyate ||
tasmāddheturna sāmānyamasti siddhaṃ dvayorapi | viśeṣayośca hetutvaṃ pakṣatattulyasaṃsthayoḥ ||
na syādanvayahīnatvādataddharmatayāpi ca | na cārthahīnā tadbuddhirhetutvena bhaviṣyati ||
āśrayāsiddhitā coktā viśeṣyasyāprasiddhitaḥ | tathā hetorviruddhatvaṃ dṛṣṭānte sādhyahīnatā ||
viśeṣaṇāprasiddhatvavikalpenaiva bodhite | svapnādipratyaye bāhyaṃ sarvathā na hi neṣyate ||
sarvatrālambanaṃ bāhyaṃ deśakālānyathātmakam | janmanyekatra bhinne vā tathā kālāntare 'pi vā ||
taddeśo vānyadeśo vā svapnajñānasya gocaraḥ | alātacakre 'lātaṃ syāc chīghrabhramaṇasaṃskṛtam ||
gandharvanagare 'bhrāṇi pūrvadṛṣṭaṃ gṛhādi ca | pūrvānubhūtatoyaṃ ca raśmitaptoṣaraṃ tathā ||
mṛgatoyasya vijñāne kāraṇatvena kalpyate | dravyāntare viṣāṇaṃ ca śaśasyātmā ca kāraṇam ||
śaśaśṛṅgadhiyaḥ, mauṇḍyaṃ niṣedhe śiraso 'sya ca | vastvantarairasaṃsṛṣṭaḥ padārthaḥ śūnyatādhiyaḥ ||
kāraṇatvaṃ padārthānāmasadvākyārthakalpane | atyantānanubhūto 'pi baddhyā yo 'rthaḥ prakalpyate ||
tasyotpattau kathañcitsyuḥ pṛthivyādīni kāraṇam | eṣa pratyakṣadharmaśca vartamānārthataiva yā ||
sannikṛṣṭārthavṛttiśca na tu jñānāntareṣviyam | kathamutpādayejjñānaṃ tatrāsaṃścet, kuto nviyam ||
arthasyāvidyamānasya vijñānotpattyaśaktatā | bāhyālambanatāyāṃ nau vivādo 'rthasya saṃnidhiḥ ||
yadi nāsti, kimevaṃ syādasmatpakṣanivartanam | tasmādyadanyathāsantamanyathā pratipadyate ||
tannirālambanaṃ jñānam, abhāvālambanaṃ ca tat | bhāvāntaramabhāvo 'nyo na kaścidanirūpaṇāt ||
bhavatā dvayamatyetaddurnirūpaṃ sahetukam | pratijñādoṣavaccāpi yojyā hetorviruddhatā ||
samastavyastadharmādisvarūpādiviparyayāt | dṛṣṭāntadoṣāḥ sarve ca yojyāḥ, na hyekavastuni ||
tava sādhyāṃśahetvaṃśavyāptadharmādisambhavaḥ | ke cidvaidharmyadṛṣṭānto nāstītyapyanuyuñjate ||
tadabhāvādavṛtteśca nāstyatrāvasarastava | vidhirūpapratijñāyāmetadvaktuṃ hi śakyate ||
tatrāvastuvipakṣe 'pi prayogasya hi sambhavaḥ | yasminnanityatā nāsti kāryatāpi na vidyate ||
tasmin, yathā khapuṣpādāviti śakyaṃ hi bhāṣitum | atra tvavastusādhyatvaṃ vastunaśca vipakṣatā ||
tena syādvyatireko 'sya vācyaḥ, yaścāpi darśayet | pratiṣedhadvayāttena vidhireva pradarśitaḥ ||
na ca śakyo vidhirvaktuṃ vastunyasati kena cit | evaṃ sthite ca sarvajñaniṣedhādāviyaṃ gatiḥ ||
pratyakṣāderasāmarthyaṃ tadīyasyāsmadādivat | vaidharmyāsambhave 'pyetadanye tvāhuradūṣaṇam ||
vinaiva tatprayogeṇa heturaikāntiko yataḥ | sarvathā sadupāyānāṃ vādamārgaḥ pravartate ||
adhikāro 'nupāyatvānna vāde śūnyavādinaḥ | nanu sarvaṃ bhavatsiddhaṃ mayedaṃ sādhanaṃ kṛtam ||
kimarthaṃ tadasiddhyā tvaṃ vikalpyātrātthadūṣaṇam | vipralipsurivāhaivaṃ kimarthaṃ nyāyavidbhavān ||
nāśrauṣīḥ sādhanatvaṃ kiṃ prasiddhasya dvayorapi | yo 'pi tāvatparāsiddhaḥ svayaṃ siddho 'bhidhīyate ||
bhavettatra pratīkāraḥ svato 'siddhe tu kā kriyā | taṃ sādhayanvirundhyāddhi pūrvābhyupagataṃ naraḥ ||
asādhite tu sādhyo 'rtho na tena pratipadyate | parāsiddho na paryāptaḥ pareṣāṃ pratipattaye ||
tenāsādhanatā yuktā, svato 'siddhe tu kiṅkṛtā | dvayoḥ siddhasya hetutvaṃ nādṛṣṭāyopadiśyate ||
pratyeṣyanti svasiddhena sādhanena svayaṃ yataḥ | vadetkathamasiddhaṃ cet, ityanenāpi kiṃ tava ||
gṛhītamagṛhītaṃ vā sādhyaṃ vā sādhanāpi vā | mayocyate cettvasiddhaṃ kiṃ tvaṃ na pratipadyase ||
yatra syātpuruṣādhīnā buddhistatredamucyate | kuto 'sya pūrvavijñānamityatretanna yujyate ||
yadi caivaṃ bhavedatra pratijñāmātra eva hi | maddoṣājñānamātreṇa pratipattirbhavettava ||
yatastu sādhanāpekṣā tenāsyaiva pramāṇatā | tatsmṛtyutpattimātre tu vākyavyāpāra iṣyate ||
tasmādyathaiva sādhyāṃśavyāptahetunidarśanāt | sādhyaṃ gṛhṇanna vaktāramapekṣeta tathā bhavān ||
yaccāpi bhavato jñānaṃ pratyakādiḥ kimatra te | matprasiddhāsti yuktirvā sādhyaṃ vātra yathecchasi ||
tasmānna viduṣāmetaduttaraṃ yujyate yataḥ | tava heturasiddho 'yaṃ mama tena na sādhanam ||
satyaṃ yadi mamaivātra pratipattiḥ phalaṃ bhavet | tadā tvadaprasiddhe 'pi hetau māṃ prati hetutā ||
yadā tu jñānamātratvapratipattau bhavānmayā | pṛṣṭaḥ ko heturatreti tadaivaṃ nopapadyate ||
