svayaṃ na hyagṛhītena matprasiddhena vā bhavān | hetunā sādhyametattu pratipannaḥ kathañcana ||
na ca vyāpriyate 'nyatra vacanaṃ prāśnikān prati | svaniścayāya yo hetustasyaiva pratipādanāt ||
matprasiddhatvametasya kutaścāvagataṃ tvayā | kathaṃ cetthaṃ vivakṣā te svayamarthamajānataḥ ||
mayi jijñāsamāne 'pi buddhipūrvābhidhāyinaḥ | iti jñātvā ca vo vṛddhairbhāṣitobhayasiddhatā ||
tena yadvanmamaitena tvamadhitsasi hetunā | sādhyajñānam, tathaivāhamajñānaṃ tava dūṣaṇaiḥ ||
yathaiva ca bhavānīdṛksādhyamuktvāsya sādhanam | sādhyānurūpamajñātvā vihataḥ pratipādanāt ||
tathaiva pratipādyo 'pi tādṛksādhyabubhutsayā | manvānaḥ sādhanaṃ duṣṭaṃ tataḥ sādhyaṃ na budhyate ||
saṃvittyā sādhanaṃ matvā tatsadbhāve dṛḍhe sthite | sādhyasyāsambhavādeva tvaduktaṃ nāvabudhyate ||
tenāśeyaṃ na kartavyā mohādapi mayerite | sādhane sādhanaṃ jñātvā para evāvabhotsyate ||
vispaṣṭaścākṣapādokto virodho hetusādhyayoḥ | yamadṛṣṭvā parairuktamadūṣaṇamidaṃ kila ||
nanu lokaprasiddhena pūrvametena hetunā | sādhyasiddhirmamāpyāsītparamārtho 'sya nāstitā ||
yo 'dhunā paramārthena nāstītyevaṃ prakāśate | kathaṃ pūrvamasāvāsīdasaṃścetsādhanaṃ katham ||
sādhanaṃ cedavaśyaṃ ca paramārthāstitā bhavet | siddhirnāparamārthena paramārthasya yujyate ||
na dṛṣṭā śaśaśṛṅgādeḥ samyagjñānādihetutā | bāṣpādināpyadhūmena mithyā vahnyādibodhanam ||
tasmādasatyahetoryā paramārthe matistava | sāpyasatyā na satyaṃ hi satyābhāsena gamyate ||
ye 'pi rekhādayo dṛṣṭā varṇānāṃ pratipādakāḥ | na te svenāpi rūpeṇa paramārthatvavarjitāḥ ||
varṇātmanā na satyāścet, sarvabhāveṣvayaṃ vidhiḥ | padārthāntararūpeṇa na satyaṃ kiñcidiṣyate ||
svarūpe vidyamāne tu yadapyevaṃ prakāśate | svarūpābhāvakḷptau tu na satyaṃ nāpyasatyatā ||
hetvādīnāṃ tu bhavataḥ svarūpeṇāpyasatyatā | tena bāṣpādivatteṣāmupāyatvam, na lekhyavat ||
upāyānāṃ svarūpaṃ hi saṃvṛttyātmakameva naḥ | tathā ca satyateṣṭaiva svarūpāsatyatā katham ||
saṃvṛtyā yatsvarūpaṃ hi tadvāṅmātranibandhanam | hetutvaṃ paramārthasya pratipattuṃ na śaknuyāt ||
paramāthācca lokasya na bhede heturasti te | laukikopāyagamyasya kena syātparamārthatā ||
nanvasatyapi bāhye 'rthe buddhyārūḍhena sidhyati | vāsanāśabdabhedotthavikalpapravibhāgataḥ ||
nyāyavidbhiridaṃ coktaṃ dharmādau buddhimāśrite | vyavahāro 'numānādeḥ kalpyate na bahiḥsthite ||
astīdaṃ vacanaṃ teṣāmidaṃ tatra parīkṣyatām | bhedo 'sataḥ kathaṃ hi syādbuddhiśabdaprakalpanāt ||
nirvastuke kathañcinnu prasavo buddhiśabdayoḥ | śabdabhedo 'pi bhavatastadabhāvānna sidhyati ||
yadi vā vidyamāno 'pi bhedo buddhiprakalpitaḥ | sādhyasādhanadharmādervyavahārāya kalpyate ||
tato bhavatprayukte 'smin sādhane yāvaducyate | sarvatrotpadyate buddhiriti dūṣaṇatā bhavet ||
yaśca mantrastvayokto 'yaṃ dharmyādau buddhimāśrite | na bāhyāpekṣayā sa syādasiddhyādau mayerite ||
buddhiprakḷptisiddhiśca bhavatāṃ vyavahāriṇām | maduktaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ siddhaṃ tvaduktaṃ tu na sādhanam ||
bāhyārthavyavahāritvājjñānotpāde sthite 'pi naḥ | kathañcinna hi kalpyeta vyavahāro 'rthavarjitaḥ ||
nanu yadvanmayā heturneṣyate dūṣaṇaṃ tathā | tena me dūṣaṇābhāvādaduṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ bhavet ||
nedānīṃ dūṣaṇaiḥ kāryam, sādhanābhāvato yadi | tvayaivāsmadabhipretā svapakṣāsiddhirāśritā ||
na cāsti vāsanābhedo nimittāsambhavāttava | jñānabhedo nimittaṃ cet, tasya bhedaḥ kathaṃ punaḥ ||
vāsanābhedataścetsyāt, prāptamanyonyasaṃśrayam | svacchasya jñānarūpasya na hi bhedaḥ svato 'sti te ||
pramāṇaṃ vāsanāstitve bhede vāpi na vidyate | kuryādgrāhakabhedaṃ sā grāhyabhedastu kiṅkutaḥ ||
saṃvittyā jāyamānā hi smṛtimātraṃ karotyasau | kṣaṇikeṣu ca citteṣu vināśe ca niranvaye ||
vāsyavāsakayoścaivamasāhityānna vāsanā | pūrvakṣaṇairanutpanno vāsyate nottaraḥ kṣaṇaḥ ||
uttareṇa vinaṣṭatvānna ca pūrvasya vāsanā | sāhitye 'pi tayornaiva sambandho 'stītyavāsanā ||
kṣaṇikatvāddvayasyāpi vyāpāro na parasparam | vinaśyacca kathaṃ vastu vāsyate 'nyena naśyatā ||
avasthitā hi vāsyante bhāvābhāvairavasthitaiḥ | avasthito hi pūrvasmādbhidyate nottaro yadi ||
pūrvavadvāsanā tatra na syādevāviśeṣataḥ | bhaṅgure pūrvasādṛśyādbhinnatvāccāsti vāsanā ||
naitadastyanurūpaṃ tu kṣaṇikatve dhiyāṃ tava | pūrvajñānaṃ tvanutpannaṃ kāryaṃ nārabhate kvacit ||
na vinaṣṭaṃ, na tasyāsti niṣpannasya kṣaṇaṃ sthitiḥ | tenotpannavinaṣṭatvānnāstyārambhakṣaṇo 'pi hi ||
niranvayavinaṣṭatvādānurūpyaṃ kutaḥ punaḥ | na tadīyosti kaścicca dharma uttarabuddhiṣu ||
samānadharmatāṃ muktvā nānurūpyaṃ ca vidyate | yadi syādānurūpyācca vāsanā godhiyo yadā ||
hastibuddhirbhavettatra vailakṣaṇyānna vāsanā | tataḥ paraṃ ca gojñānaṃ nirmūlatvānna sambhavet ||
sarvaṃ vilakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ na syādeva vilakṣaṇāt | bāhyārthānugrahābhāvātpārārthyenāvaśīkṛtāḥ ||
niranvayavināśinyaḥ kuryuḥ kāryaṃ kathaṃ kramāt | vināśe kāraṇasyeṣṭaḥ kāryārambhaśca nānyathā ||
tataiva jñānanāśena vinaṣṭāḥ sarvavāsanāḥ | tena sarvābhya etābhyaḥ sarvākāraṃ yadutthitam ||
jñānamekakṣaṇenaiva vināśaṃ gantumarhati | yadyāśrayavināśe 'pi śaktyanāśo 'bhyupeyate ||
kṣaṇikatvaṃ ca hīyeta na cārambho 'nyathā bhavet | vāsanānāṃ pravāho 'pi yadi jñānapravāhavat ||
vāsanātastato jñānaṃ na syāttasmācca vāsanā | kuryātāṃ tulyamevaite nānyonyaṃ tu kadā cana ||
nānyo vilakṣaṇo heturyenānyādṛkphalaṃ bhavet | tasmātsaṃvṛtisatyaiṣā kalpitā nāsti tattvataḥ ||
na cedṛśena bhāvena kāryamutpadyate kva cit | yasya tvavasthito jñātā jñānābhyāsena yujyate ||
sa tasya vāsanādhāro vāsanāpi sa eva vā | kusume bījapūrāderyallākṣādyupasicyate | tadrūpasyaiva saṃkrāntiḥ phale tasya, ityavāsanā ||
yuktyānupetāmasatīṃ prakalpya yadvāsanāmarthanirākriyeyam | āsthānivṛttyarthamavādi bauddhairgrāhaṃ gatāstatra kathañcidanye ||

§ 5,4 śunyavāda snv

evamukte 'numānasya jñānamāśritya dūṣaṇe | jñānapravṛttyaśaktyā tu paraḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate ||
yattāvanmanyamānena pratyakṣaṃ bhavatocyate | dūṣaṇaṃ tadvirodhādi tadidānīṃ parīkṣyatām ||
pravartituṃ hi kiṃ śaktaṃ stambhādyarthe bahiḥ sthite | atha vātmāṃśa evaitat grāhye kṣīṇaṃ na vastuni ||
tadyadyetena bāhyo 'rtho gṛhyate dūṣaṇaṃ tataḥ | tvaduktaṃ sarvamātmāṃśe grāhye tannopapadyate ||
tatra tāvadidaṃ siddhaṃ sarvaprāṇabhṛtāmapi | grāhyataṃ nīlapītādidīrghādyākāravastunaḥ ||
na cāpyākārabhedena jñānajñeyāvadhāraṇā | na cānyataradharmatvaṃ vispaṣṭaṃ tatra gṛhyate ||
gṛhyamāṇasya cāstitvaṃ nāgrāhyasyāpramāṇakam | tasmādākāravadvastu grāhyatvādvidyate dhruvam ||
ataḥ parīkṣamāṇānāṃ jñānamākāravadyadi | tanmātre ca pramā kṣīṇā tato nāstyarthakalpanā ||
yadi vākāravattā syādbāhyasyaiveha vastunaḥ | tadasti gṛhyamāṇatvāttatsiddhaivāsti dhīrapi ||
kiṃ tāvadatra yuktaṃ syājjñānamākāravat, kutaḥ | ekamākāravadvastu grāhyamityadhyagīṣmahi ||
tadyadyākāravānartho bāhyaḥ kalpyeta tasya ca | grāhyatvamanyathā na syāditi grāhakakalpanā ||
tenākāravataḥ kḷptādgrāhyādākāravarjitam | vastvantaraṃ prakalpyaṃ syādgrāhakaṃ niṣpramāṇakam ||
tasyākalpanamicchaṃścedarthe grāhakatāṃ vadeḥ | saṃjñāmātre visaṃvādaḥ siddhā tvekārthakalpanā ||
grāhyagrāhakayoraikyaṃ sarvathā pratipādyate | bāhyābhyantararūpaśca parikalpyo mṛṣeṣyate ||
matpakṣe yadyapi svaccho jñānātmā paramārthataḥ | tathāpyanādau saṃsāre pūrvajñānaprasūtibhiḥ ||
citrābhiścitrahetutvādvāsanābhirupaplavāt | svānurūpyeṇa nīlādi grāhyagrāhakarūṣitam ||
pravibhaktamivotpannaṃ nānyamarthamapekṣate | anyonyahetutā caiva jñānaśaktyoranādikā ||
anekakalpanāyāśca jyāyasī hyekakalpanā | śaktimātrasya bhedaśca vastubhedādviśiṣyate ||
tasmādubhayasiddhatvājjñānasyākārakalpanā | jyāyasī, bhavatastvarthaṃ kalpayitvā bhavediyam ||
tadasiddhāvaśaktatvāt, tenaivaṃ viprakṛṣṭatā | pratyāsannaṃ ca, sambaddhaṃ grāhyaṃ mama bhaviṣyati ||
itaścākāravajjñānam, yasmāttadvatprakāśakam | svayamprakāśahīnasya bāhyasyopāsanaṃ matam ||
na cāgṛhīte jñānākhye prakāśyo 'rtho 'vadhāryate | tadadhīnaprakāśatvāddīpābhāse yathā ghaṭaḥ ||
utpanneṣvapi cārtheṣu prakāśābhāvataḥ kva cit | pratibandhakayogādvā saṃvittirnopajāyate ||
jñānasyotpadyamānasya pratibandho na kaścana | na cāprakāśarūpatvaṃ yenāsyāgrahaṇaṃ bhavet ||
prākcārthagrahaṇādiṣṭā tasyotpattistadaiva ca | saṃvedanaṃ bhavedasya, na cetkālāntare 'pi na ||
kiṃ hi tasya bhavedūrdhvaṃ prākca nāsīnna yena tat | pūrvaṃ gṛhītaṃ paścāt ca gṛhītamiti bhāṣyate ||
jñānāntarasya cotpattiṃ prakāśo na pratīkṣate | tasya tasyāpi cānyena saṃvittāvasthitirbhavet ||
jñānapṛṣṭena yo 'pyūrdhvamarthābhāve 'pi dṛśyate | parāmarśo 'rtharūpasya sa kathaṃ vopapadyate ||
tadrūpamārthamālikhya yadi dhīrnopajāyate | bhūtakāle ca yadyarthastatpūrvaṃ nopalakṣitaḥ ||
vaktāraścāpi dṛśyante varttamānārthabuddhiṣu | nīlo 'rtho 'yaṃ yato me 'tra tadrūpā jāyate matiḥ ||
tasmātpūrvagṛhītāsu buddhiṣvarthopalambhanam | na copalabdhirastīhi nirākārāsu buddhiṣu ||
vivekabuddhyabhāvācca, sākārasya ca darśanāt | ākāravattayā bodho jñānasyaiva prasajyate ||
na hyevaṃ kalpanā śakyā nirākārādito matiḥ | gṛhyate 'rthastataḥ paścātsākāraḥ sampratīyate ||
ākāravattvabhedo hi jñātvā śakyeta bhāṣitum | prāgbuddhigrahaṇādarthe saṃvittirneti sādhitam ||
na cārthākāra evāyaṃ jñānārūḍhaḥ pratīyate | na hi so 'ntaḥpraveśāya paryāpto nārthahānaye ||
itthambhāve pramāṇaṃ ca tasya vaktuṃ na śakyate | tadīyapratibimbatvametasmādeva neṣyate ||
niścandre bimbarūpaṃ hi dṛṣṭaṃ yena divā jalam | sa rātrau khe ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā jānāti pratibimbatām ||
vijñāne na kadā cittu prāṅ nirākāradarśanam | bāhye vākāravattādhīryenaivaṃ kalpanā bhavet ||
śabdagandharasānāṃ ca kīdṛśī pratibimbatā | jñāne ca gṛhyamāṇasya kathaṃ syādarthadharmatā ||
bāhyābhyantaradeśatvānna cārthajñānayormithaḥ | samparko 'sti yato mohādavivekamatirbhavet ||
asammūḍhasya cādṛṣṭe na sammohaprakalpanā | kalpyamāne 'tha vāpyevaṃ taddvayoravatiṣṭhate ||
saṃsargadhama ākārastasmādeva na yujyate | deśabhedādasaṃsargaḥ, mūrāmūrtatayā tathā ||
tailokyena prasaṅgācca saṃsargo naikakālatā | na cāpyārjavataḥ sthānaṃ jñāne nārthasya vidyate ||
sarvathā kalpanāyāṃ ca cakṣuṣāpi rasādayaḥ | gṛhyeran sarvabhāvānāmaṇvākārāśca tadgatāḥ ||
na cāpi viṣayatvena sthāne saṃsargakalpanā | viṣayatvaṃ hi kīdṛksyātprāgākāropalambhanāt ||
na hyasañcetito bhāvo viṣayatvena kalpyate | viṣayatvāttadākāra ākārādviṣayaśca saḥ ||
dvayorākāranirmuktaṃ sattvaṃ saṃsṛṣṭatā tathā | svarūpataḥ paricchidya vaktumityādi yujyate ||
na cāpyasyeha sadbhāvaḥ prāggṛhīto na copari | na hyākāravinirmuktaṃ grāhyamastīti bhāṣitam ||
tasmādarthena saṃsargo niṣpramāṇaka eva te | jñānavaicitryasiddhyarthaṃ na cāstyarthasya kalpanā ||
tadadhīnaṃ hi vaicitryaṃ kva dṛṣṭaṃ yena kalpyate | nirākāreṇa cotpattirvaicitryākārayoḥ katham ||
nirākārācca viṣayādbuddhyākāro 'tivismayaḥ | smṛtisvapnādibodhe ca syādanākāratā tava ||
na hi tatrārthasaṃsargaḥ kevalā vāsanaiva tu | hetutvenopapanneti saiva jāgraddhiyāmapi ||
anvayavyatirekābhyāmevaṃ jñānasya gamyate | ākāraḥ, na hi bāhyasya jñānāpeto nidarśyate ||
bāhyāpeto mayā yadvat, tasmātsaṃsargavāgiyam | nirākāre 'pi vijñāne vāsanāsveva yujyate ||
dvayorapyeka ākāra ityetasyāpramāṇatā | deśabhedādasaṃsargaḥ, dvayoścānavadhāraṇāt ||
evamevārthabuddhyoḥ syātsādṛśyānnāvibhaktatā | bhede jñāte hi sādṛśyaṃ nājñāte syātkhapuṣpavat ||
tathā dvicandramāyādāvanyathārthe vyavasthite | yā syādākārasaṃvittirnāsāvarthanibandhanā ||
nakṣatraṃ tārakā tiṣyo dārā ityevamādiṣu | naikatrārthe viruddhatvālliṅgānekatvasambhavaḥ ||
parivrāṭkāmukaśunāṃ kuṇapādimatistathā | dīrghahrasvatvabuddhiśca hyekasminnapyapekṣayā ||
ghaṭatvātpārthavadravyaprameyādimatistathā | yugapadgrāhakāṇāṃ ca na syādaikātmyavattayā ||
nārthe hyekatra yugapadviruddhākārasambhavaḥ | pratyayānāṃ tu bhinnatvādbhavec chaktyanusārataḥ ||
nirapekṣaṃ svarūpeṇa tasmājjñānaṃ yadākṛti | tathārtho na yathārthaṃ tu jñānamutpadyate kva cit ||
itthaṃ vijñānatantratve ko nvarthaṃ kalpayiṣyati | dhīranāropitākārā svātmanyevopayokṣyate ||
naitadasti, tvayaikaṃ hi grāhyaṃ grāhakamiṣyate | na caikasyaivamātmatve dṛṣṭāntaḥ kaścidasti te ||
agnyādayo ghaṭādīnāṃ prasiddhā ye prakāśakāḥ | na te prakāśyarūpā hi prakāśasya, anapekṣaṇāt ||
grāhyatvaṃ tu yadā teṣāṃ tadākṣaṃ grāhakaṃ matam | akṣagrahaṇakāle tu grāhikā dhīrbhaviṣyati ||
tasyāṃ tu gṛhyamāṇāyāmanyā dhīrgrāhikeṣyate | nanvātmā grāhako grāhyo bhavatābhyupagamyate ||
kathañciddharmarūpeṇa bhinnatvātpratyayasya tat | grāhakatvaṃ bhavettatra grāhyaṃ dravyādi cātmanaḥ ||
yastu nātyantabhedo 'tra kva vāsāviṣyate mayā | pratyāsattinimittā tu pratyagātmapravarttitā ||
asmatprayogasambhinnā jñānasyaiva tu kartari | bhavantī tatra saṃvittiryujyetāpyātmakartṛkā ||
na cātra karaṇajñānagrāhakākāravedanam | grāhyatvaṃ yena buddheḥ syādabhinnatve 'pi pūrvavat ||
anyarūpāpi saṃvittiryadyanyaviṣayeṣyate | jñānākārāpi saṃvittiḥ kasmānnārthasya kalpyate ||
abhinnatvaṃ yadā ceṣṭaṃ grāhyagrāhakavastunoḥ | tadānyatarasaṃvittau dvyākāraṃ grahaṇaṃ bhavet ||
yadā tu grāhyamākāraṃ nīlādi pratipadyate | na tadā grāhakākārā saṃvittirdṛśyate kva cit ||
tasmādabhinnatā cetsyāttasyāpyanubhavo bhavet | grāhyo vā nānubhūyeta grāhakānanubhūtivat ||
grāhakagrahaṇe 'pyevaṃ grāhyasaṃvedanaṃ bhavet | śuddhameva nirākāraṃ grāhakaṃ saṃvidasti hi ||
grāhyādabhinnatāyā ca sā saṃvittirna yujyate | grāhako vā na gṛhyeta tadgrāhyānanubhūtivat ||
yathāvadgrāhyasaṃvittau grāhakagrahaṇe 'pi vā | grāhyagrāhakasaṃvittirnāstyeva syāddvayorapi ||
sa bahirdeśasambaddhaḥ ityanena nirūpyate | grāhyākārasya saṃvittirgrāhakānubhavādṛte ||
paraṃ prati hi sādhyatvadarthasyākārasiddhaye | bahirdeśena sambandho na hetutvāya kalpate ||
tasmādbahiritīhedaṃ niṣkṛṣṭaṃ grāhakāṃśataḥ | saṃvedyaṃ nīlapītādi pratyakṣāderudāhṛtam ||
na pūrvaṃ jñāyate buddhirityatraitadvadiṣyate | grāhakasyaiva saṃvittirlakṣyate grahaṇe kva cit ||
na smarāmi mayā ko 'pi gṛhīto 'rthastadeti hi | smaranti grāhakotpādagrāhyarūpavivarjitam ||
tasmādabhinnatāyāṃ ca grāhye 'pi smaraṇaṃ bhavet | grāhakasmṛtinirbhāsāttatrāpyeṣaiva gṛhyate ||
tadatyantāvinābhāvānnaikākāraṃ hi jāyate | anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ siddhaivaṃ bhinnatā tayoḥ ||
grāhyāṃśo grāhakāṃśena gṛhyate, grāhakaḥ punaḥ | gṛhyeteti na vaktavyam, grāhakāntaravarjanāt ||
grāhyāṃśenāpyaśaktatvānna tasya grahaṇaṃ bhavet | grāhakatvena caitasya hīyetaiva dvirūpatā ||
grāhake gṛhyamāṇe ca grāhyamātraprasañjanam | na syādākāra ekaśceditarasyāpi nāstitā ||
udbhavābhibhavābhyāṃ ca grāhyāgrāhyatvadarśanam | yathā dīpaprabhādīnāṃ rūpamātropalambhanam ||
divā cāgneḥ samīpasthaiḥ sparśa evopalabhyate | gandhavaddravyavṛttau ca gandhasyaivopalambhanam ||
na guṇāntarasaṃvittiryathātrābhibhavāt, tathā | nākārāntarasaṃvittirgrāhyagrāhakabuddhiṣu ||
grāhyādananyabhūto 'pi kaścinnaivopalabhyate | nityānityādayo dharmāḥ śabdādigrahaṇe yathā ||
abhedaṃ vābhyupetyāyaṃ prasaṅgo yadi gīyate | ekasmingṛhyamāṇe 'śe na gṛhyetāparaḥ katham ||
tasmādyatsyādyadā yogyaṃ tasyaiva grahaṇaṃ tadā | dvayaṃ ca tvadupanyastaṃ śaktyabhāvānna gṛhyate ||
kuto 'yamekavastutve yogyāyogyatvasambhavaḥ | udbhavābhibhavātmatvaṃ kathaṃ caikasya kalpitam ||
ekāṃśābhibhave ca syāditarābhibhavo 'pi te | tathā tasyābhibhūtatvādgrāhyatvaṃ na ca yujyate ||
ayogyatā vikalpyaivam, dṛṣṭāntā ye 'tra kīrtitāḥ | rūpādibhedāttatra syādudbhavābhibhavādyapi ||
yadāpyekāntato bhedo rūpāderna parasparam | tadāpi dravyarūpasya pariṇāmastathā tathā ||
abhinnatve 'pi na grāhyamiti yaccābravīdbhavān | kṛtakatvādidharmāṇāṃ dhībhede 'nanyatā katham ||
na hyanyatpratyayādasti bhinnādgrāhyasya bhedakam | na ceyattaiva bhedasya deśato mūrtito 'pi vā ||
kāraṇānāṃ hi sambandhaḥ kāryaiḥ kṛtakatocyate | vibhāgo 'vayavānāṃ ca bhavetkva cidanityatā ||
buddhyāderātmarūpādisthānaṃ nāśitvamucyate | nityatvaṃ sarvadā sattā, vastutvaṃ saiva kīrtyate ||
pramāṇajñānasambandhaḥ prameyajñeyatocyate | sarvatra cātra bhinnatvamasti kena cidātmanā ||
tasmādyathaiva rūpāderdeśabhedādibhirvinā | buddhibhedena bhedo 'sti tathaivātra pratīyatām ||
atyantabhinnatāsmābhirnaiva kasya cidiṣyate | sarvaṃ hi vasturūpeṇa bhidyate na parasparam ||
sarvaṃ ca kṛtakatvādi kriyāhetvādyapekṣayā | gṛhyate tadasaṃvittāvabhede 'pi na gṛhyate ||
jñāne naivaṃvidho bhedo nāpekṣānyatra vidyate | paraspareṇa cāpekṣā syāccet, sannihitaśca saḥ ||
nanu grāhakamityevaṃ grāhyamityapi vā matiḥ | nīlādigrahaṇe nāstītyapekṣā kathamucyate ||
mā bhūdevaṃ tathāpyatra dvyākāre grahaṇaṃ bhavet | evaṃ cāgṛhyamāṇe vā jñāne dvyākāratā katham ||
uttarottaravijñānaviśeṣādyā prakalpyate | grāhakākārasaṃvittiḥ smaraṇāccānumānikī ||
ekākāraṃ kila jñānaṃ prathamaṃ yadi kalpyate | tatastadviṣayāpyanyā tadrūpaiva matirbhavet ||
ghaṭavijñānatajjñānaviśeṣo 'to na sidhyati | grāhakākārasaṃvittau tvākārapracayo bhavet ||
jāyate pūrvavijñānaṃ dvyākāraṃ yatra tatpunaḥ | tasyātmīyaśca pūrvau ca viṣayasthāvupaplutau ||
pareṣvākāravṛddhyaivaṃ pūrvebhyo bhinnatā, tathā | grāhyavatsmaraṇātpaścātsaṃvittau grāhakaḥ purā ||
na tāvadevamākārān paśyāmaḥ pracayānvitān | viṣayavyapadeśācca narte jñānanirūpaṇam ||
tasmājjñānātmanaikatve grāhyabhedanibandhanaḥ | saṃvittibhedaḥ siddho 'tra kimākārāntareṇa naḥ ||
nirākāratasāmye 'pi yathākāravatāṃ dhruvam | bhedaḥ svābhāvikastadvajjñānānāṃ kiṃ na sidhyati ||
smṛteruttarakālaṃ cetyetanmithyaiva gīyate | tadaiva hyasya saṃvittirarthāpattyopajāyate ||
gṛhītameva yaccoktaṃ tadabhedāt, na tad, yataḥ | nāsmabhirvākyavṛttestvaṃ nimittamanuyujyase ||
grāhyagrāhakataivāsya kena cinnopalabhyate | pratyakṣajñānapakṣe ca naiṣā syādānumānikī ||
ekākāre ca vijñāne yadyanyo 'pyatra kalpyate | sahasrākārataikasya kasmānna parikalpyate ||
grāhyagrāhakayorbhedo nanvastyeva parasparam | siddho naḥ pakṣa evaṃ syāt, na, jñānatvādabhedataḥ ||
bhinnābhinnatvamekasya kuto 'tra parikalpitam | tvayā sāṃkhyamatenaivamuktvā buddhasya śāsanam ||
ekaṃ cedgrāhakaṃ grāhyaṃ kuto bhinnatvavāgiyam | bhinnaṃ cetkathamucyeta tasyaikatvaṃ punastvayā ||
ekajñānādananyatvādgrāhyagrāhakayormithaḥ | ekatvena bhavejjñānaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakameva vā ||
tatra cānyatarāpāye dvitīyāpāyataḥ punaḥ | jñānasyāṃśadvayāsattvānnaiḥsvābhāvyādabhāvatā ||
bhinnābhyāṃ vāpyabhinnatvādbhedo jñānātmano bhavet | tatsvātmanaḥ, tataścaivaṃ siddhaṃ vastudvayaṃ hi naḥ ||
tayośca yadi saṃjñeyaṃ jñānamityastvathāpi vā | jñānaṃ jñāyata ityartho dhīrbhāve karaṇe 'pi vā ||
sarvathā vastubhedo naḥ siddhaḥ śabdo yathāruci | pravartatāṃ na nastatra kācidvipratipannatā ||
atha satyapi bhinnatve grāhyaṃ jñānāntaraṃ bhavet | jñānatve tasya kā yuktiḥ, pūrvoktā yadi seṣyate ||
jñānaṃ jñānamitīdaṃ tu na dvayoranuvartate | vyatiriktaṃ ca sāmānyaṃ tvayā nābhyupagamyate ||
vyatireke tayorjñānānna jñānātmakatā bhavet | tadrūparahitatve ca jñānābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||
tābhyāṃ ca tasya sambandhe pratyekaṃ vyatiṣajya ca | bhedasāvayavatvādi doṣo vaiśeṣikādivat ||
yathā hi teṣāṃ jātyādau doṣā hyuktāḥ parairamī | tathaivaiṣāṃ prasajyante bhinnābhinnārthasaṅgatau ||
tābhyāmavyatireke vā bhedaḥ pūrvokta eva te | sādṛśyāpohasāmānyakalpanā vārayiṣyate ||
vastvantarasya cābhāvāttvayāpoho 'pi duṣkaraḥ | nājñānaṃ nāma kiñcitsyādapohyaṃ jñānavādinaḥ ||
apoho na hyabhāvasya kathañcidupapadyate | vastvantaramabhāvaḥ syād, apohyatvācca vastutā ||
tenājñānanivṛttau hi jñāne 'nyārtha prasajyate | kalpitaṃ syādapohyaṃ cet, nātyantāsatyakalpanā ||
buddhirajñānanirbhāsā tavājñānaṃ prakalpitam | tataśca jñānamevaikamapohyatvena sammatam ||
na cātmāpoha evāsti kva citsāmānyakalpane | vṛkṣasya na hyapohyatvaṃ vṛkṣeṇaiva kadā cana ||
apohye caiva vijñāne jñānatvaṃ na bhavettava | vṛkṣatvaṃ na hyapohyeṣu kalaśādiṣu yujyate ||
tataścājñānamevārtha ityabhinnārthatā bhavet | ajñānapratyayaścāyaṃ kimālambana iṣyate ||
na tāvajjñānanirmuktamajñānaṃ grāhyamasti te | na ca vastu niṣiddhaṃ tadabhāvaḥ kiṃ na gṛhyate ||
bhāvo na gṛhyate yena tasyābhāveṣu kā kathā | svāṃśaparyavasānaṃ ca tulyamatrāpi kāraṇam ||
tena jñānāntaraṃ vā syādgrāhyamātmāṃśa eva vā | svarūpaviparītaṃ ca kathaṃ grāhyaṃ pratīyate ||
yathoṣṇe 'nuṣṇadhīrnāsti, jñāne 'pyajñānadhīstathā | tena na jñānamātratve syādapohyaṃ kathañcana ||
grāhyagrāhakayoścāto na jñānātmasamānatā | tasmādanyataratredaṃ jñānatvaṃ sampratīyate ||
tatrāpyubhayasiddhatvādgrāhakasyeti gamyate | vastubhede prasiddhe ca vyapadeśo yathāruci ||
jñānamastūbhayaṃ vārtho grāhako vārtha ucyatām | buddhyorayugapadbhāvānna dvayormayamānatā ||
kṣaṇikā hītyanenoktam, artho hyekaḥ prasajyate | anyonyanirapekṣatvādyugapaccāpi janmani ||
mānameyatvanāstitvam, kriyākārakavarjanāt | arthavijñānayoratra yā mitiṃ prati saṅgatiḥ ||
kāryakāraṇabhāvo 'yam, nānyatraivaṃ ca dṛśyate | niyamaśca na labhyeta savyadakṣiṇaśṛṅgavat ||
idaṃ kāryamayaṃ hetuḥ, dvayaṃ na, anyonyasaṃśrayāt | tadbhāvabhāvitāmātraṃ hetuḥ kairnaiva varṇyate ||
paurvāparyavinirmuktaṃ kāryakāraṇalakṣaṇam | gavāśvasya yathā nāsti paurvāparye 'pi tattathā ||
yugapajjāyamāne 'pi santatyantaraje kṣaṇe | rūpādiṣu ghaṭe yadvat, tasmātpūrvamavasthite ||
yo yasmājjāyate paścātsa tatkāryamitīṣyate | hetuhetumatāṃ siddhaṃ yaugapadyanidarśanam ||
yatpradīpaprabhādyuktaṃ sūkṣmaḥ kālo 'sti tatra naḥ | durlakṣastu yathā vedhaḥ padmapattraśate tathā ||
bhāgayoryaugapadyena tathaiva syānnirākriyā | na ca śaktyarpaṇadvāraṃ krameṇālambanaṃ bhavet ||
grāhyaṃ tadā hyatītaṃ syāt, tadrūpyaṃ cāpramāṇakam | atītatvānuviddho hi smṛtyā grāhyo 'nubhūyate ||
tadvadeva bhavedatra, svapne na syāt, viparyayāt | tatra hyavartamāno 'pi gṛhyate vartamānavat ||
bādhajñānādidaṃ bhrāntam, na tvatraivaṃ viparyayaḥ | tasmātpratyakṣabuddhīnāṃ nātito viṣayo bhavet ||
atītatvādyathaivāsāṃ vṛtto janmāntareṣu yaḥ | tadrūpatvena vā jñānaṃ heturbhāvivaducyate ||
atītatve 'pi nārtho 'yaṃ dhīreṣetyatra kā pramā | atītaṃ yacca vijñānaṃ grāhyatvena prakalpitam ||
tasmādgrāhakarūpaṃ vā grāhyaṃ vobhayathāpi vā | grāhyākāratvamātre syādarthaḥ śabdāntareṇa te ||
svakāle cāpyasaṃvitterna syāc chaktyarpaṇaṃ tataḥ | yathaivānāgatājjñānātsantatyantarajādapi ||
dṛḍhatvenāpyavijñātāttathotpannādvinaśyataḥ | kevalagrāhakatve tu viṣayatvaṃ na yujyate ||
kimapekṣya ca tasyedaṃ grāhakatvaṃ prakalpyate | dvyākāratā nirastaiva, saṃvedyeta tadaiva ca ||
tataścottaravijñānaṃ na pratīkṣeta bodhakam | dvyākārakalpanāyāṃ ca parasyātmāṃśa eva te ||
pramāparyavasānena nātīto viṣayo bhavet | pūrvagrāhyasarūpatve grāhakatvaṃ prahīyate ||
grāhakākāramātre syādviṣayo nāsarūpataḥ | na ca śaktyarpaṇasyātra vyāpāra upalabhyate ||
śaktyarpaṇasya cābhāvo yuṣmatpakṣe prasādhitaḥ | santānāntaravaccaiṣāṃ niṣedhyā hetusādhyatā ||
vāsyavāsakabhāvaśca jñānatvādekasantatau | tasmādyadbhāsakaṃ rūpaṃ tadgrāhyāttasya bhinnatā ||
tatsaṃvittāvasaṃvitte rasādigrāhakaṃ yathā | grāhyaṃ tadgrāhakāccaiva tatparāmṛśatā yataḥ ||
na parāmṛśyate 'vaśyaṃ rasādigrāhakaṃ yathā | dvayaṃ paraspareṇaivaṃ bhinnaṃ sādhyaṃ rasādivat ||
aikarūpyeṇa cājñānātsantānāntarabuddhivat | jñānaṃ svāṃśaṃ na gṛhṇāti jñānotpatteḥ svaśaktivat ||
grāhyatvapratiṣedhaśca dvayahīnā hi vāsate | caitrajñānaṃ tadudbhūtajñānāṃśagrāhyabodhakam ||
jñānatvānna bhavedyadvattasya dehāntarodbhavam | etayaiva diśā vācyā śaktidvayanirākriyā ||
pramāṇāntarasiddhatvādanyatrānekaśaktitā | na tvatra kāraṇaṃ tādṛkśaktibhedakṛdasti te ||
tasmādubhayasiddhatvāllāghavādyaḥ parigrahaḥ | upāyatvācca yattasya pūrvagrahaṇakalpanam ||
cakṣurādīndriyairatra tadanaikāntikaṃ bhavet | yadapyapratibaddhatvādutpattau gṛhyatāmiti ||
tatrātmanā na śaktyaṃ tannānyotpattistadasti vā | tenaitatkāraṇābhāvāttadānīṃ nānubhūyate ||
nānyathā hyarthasadbhāvo dṛṣṭaḥ sannupapadyate | jñānaṃ cennetyataḥ paścātpramāṇamupajāyate ||
na cāpyapratibandhena kevalena graho bhavet | viśiṣṭakāraṇābhāve 'pyartho naivānubhūyate ||
vyāpṛtaṃ cārthasaṃvittau jñānaṃ nātmānamṛcchati | tena prakāśakatve 'pi bodhāyānyatpratīkṣyate ||
īdṛśaṃ vā prakāśatvaṃ tasyārthānubhavātmakam | na cātmānubhavo 'styasyetyātmano na prakāśakam ||
sati prakāśakatve ca vyavasthā dṛśyate yathā | rūpādau cakṣurādīnāṃ tathātrāpi bhaviṣyati ||
prakāśakatvaṃ bāhye 'rthe śaktyabhāvāttu nātmani | anyena vānubhāve 'sāvanavasthā prasajyate ||
tatra tatra smṛtiṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvānubhavakalpanā | ekena tvanubhūtatve sarvaṃ tatraiva sambhavet ||
tatrāpi smṛtirityetanna lokānumataṃ vacaḥ | na hi vijñānasantānaṃ kaścitsmarati laukikaḥ ||
ghaṭādāvagṛhīte 'rthe yadi tāvadanantaram | arthāpattyāvabudhyante vijñānāni punaḥ punaḥ ||
yāvacchramaṃ tataḥ paścāttāvatyeva smariṣyati | tadā tvakalpite 'pyevaṃ smṛtivarndhyāsutādivat ||
smṛtibhrāntaśca yāpyatra paścājjñāneṣu jāyate | tadaivārthasmṛtereṣāṃ tajñānādipramāṇatā ||
yāvacchramaṃ ca tadbuddhistatprabandhe mahatyapi | śramādrucyānyasamparkādvicchedo viṣayeṣviva ||
tatrāpi smṛtirityeṣāṃ prathame pratyaye yadi | tanmātragrahaṇādevaṃ nānavasthā prasajyate ||
smaraṇaṃ tvatha sarveṣu tatsiddhyai grahaṇaṃ tathā | pramāṇavattvādāyātaḥ pravāhaḥ kena vāryate ||
atha tānyādyavijñānaviṣayāṇīti kalpyate | nottarottarabuddhīnāṃ viśeṣa upapadyate ||
vijñānaviṣayatvaṃ ca yasya sarvāsu buddhiṣu | ghaṭavijñāna tajñānaviśeṣastena durlabhaḥ ||
smaranyathaiva vijñānaṃ nirākāraṃ smaratyayam | tathā smarangṛhītārthaṃ nirākāratayā smaret ||
jñānapṛṣṭena yo 'pyūrdhvaṃ parāmarśo bhavatyasau | tasyārtheṣvabhyupāyatvānna tu grāhyatvakāritaḥ ||
pratyāsannatvasambandhau grāhyatvāsambhavāccyutau | viṣayatvena vāpyetau staḥ kiṃ deśāvibhāgataḥ ||
arthākārasya yo 'pyukto mithyājñāneṣvasambhavaḥ | dośakālānyathāmātrasambhavaḥ keṣu citkṛtaḥ ||
pratyakṣādanyavijñānamatītānāgatairapi | janyate 'rthe bhavantīṣu vāsanāsvasatīṣu vā ||
yaḥ punarnānubhūto 'rtho na vāpyanubhaviṣyate | vāsanābhāvatastatra tavāpyanubhavaḥ katham ||
vināpi vāsanātaścedbuddhirutpadyate tataḥ | vāsanāyā nimittatvamabhyupetaṃ virudhyate ||
vāsanā cedbhavettatra sā ca saṃvittipūrvikā | tathā sati ca pūrvatra gṛhītaḥ kvāpyasau dhruvam ||
evaṃ ca naiva vaktavyamatyantābhavanaṃ kva cit | anyathānupapatyā hi siddhā janmāntare 'stitā ||
duṣṭatvena ca vijñānamanyathāpi vyavasthitam | pṛthivyādiṣu gṛhṇīyādākāraṃ tannibandhanam ||
tānyapāsya tu naivārthe kva cidākārakalpanā | na jñānaṃ hyanavaṣṭambhamātmānaṃ labdhumarhati ||
vijñānasyaiva vā kāryaṃ yadyeṣo 'nye ca kalpitāḥ | viśeṣaḥ ko 'tra yenāyamatyantāsannitīṣyate ||
tasmādbhrāntirapi tveṣāṃ kalpayantyarthameva naḥ | kalpayatyanyathā santaṃ na tvātmānaṃ vyavasyati ||
tataśca bādhakajñānādvācoyuktiriyaṃ bhavet | arthe 'nyathāpi satyeṣa dhiyākāraḥ pratīyate ||
dvicandrādimatiṣvevam, tārakādimatau tathā | strītvādyanyatra dṛṣṭaṃ syāt, kathañcidveha sambhavet ||
śabdamātrapratīyā vā, dṛṣṭairvā kaiścidiṅganāt | saṃstyānaprasavasthānairyathā pātañjale mate ||
tena liṅgatrayasyātra sadbhāvaḥ syātpramāṇavān | apekṣābhedataścātra virodho 'pi na vidyate ||
kuṇapādimatau caivaṃ sārvarūpye vyavasthite | vāsanāḥ sahakāriṇyo vyavasthākāradarśane ||
svapratyayānukāro hi bahvākāreṣu vastuṣu | nirdhāraṇe bhaveddheturnāpūrvākārakalpane ||
tathā dīrghaghaṭatvādau bhinnāpekṣānibandhanā | ākārabhedasampattiraviruddhā bhaviṣyati ||
nānekākārasaṃvitternirākāratvakalpanā | yuktā, pratītibhedāttu bahvākāratvasambhavaḥ ||
saṃvitteśca viruddhānāmekasminnapi sambhavaḥ | ekākāraṃ bhavedekamiti neśvarabhāṣitam ||
tathaiva tadupetavyaṃ yadyathaivopalabhyate | na cāpyaikāntikaṃ tasya syādekatvaṃ ca vastunaḥ ||
tasmāddeśādisadbhāvanimittaiḥ pratyayaiḥ pṛthak | vastvākārāḥ pratīyerannudbhavābhibhavātmakāḥ ||
yugapadgrāhakāṇāṃ ca yo yadākāravācinam | śabdaṃ smarati tenāsāvākāraḥ sampratīyate ||
nityaṃ satsu tathā loke rūpādiṣu ghaṭe pṛthak | cakṣurādyanurodhena saṃvittirvyavatiṣṭhate ||
evameva ghaṭatvādau sarvān prati bhavatyapi | vācakasmṛtibhedena saṃvittirvyavatiṣṭhate ||
tasmādbahiḥ sthito 'pyātmā narāṇāṃ cakṣurādibhiḥ | prāpya vāprāpya vā buddherviṣayatvena kalpyate ||
vadanti laukikā yacca yādṛgjñānaṃ tathā bahiḥ | te punarjñānasaṃvittyā tathārthaṃ prati jānate ||
grāhakatvena vijñānaṃ yathārthaṃ naḥ samarpayet | tādṛgarthaḥ sa ityevaṃ teṣāṃ vā tadupāyataḥ ||
laiṅgikāsattvamaprāptairetairbāhyārthavādibhiḥ | jñānānubhavamutkramya bāhya eva pratīyate ||
yathā loke ca tadbuddhirvācyamevaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ | na yādṛgantarākārastādṛgbāhyo 'vakalpate ||
utpadyamānā gṛhyeta dhīrarthagrahaṇe yadi | pūrvapakṣasya kiṃ siddham, kathaṃ cārthāntaraṃ vadet ||
bāhyārthavādinaṃ brūte bhavān kiṃ naivamicchati | pratibandho na tasyāsti gṛhṇātyarthāntaraṃ yadā ||
uttaraṃ grahakābhāvālliṅgābhāvācca nāsti naḥ | tadā grahaṇamityetat, anyatarkeṣu cocyate ||
teṣu tarkeṣu vijñānamarthakāle 'vagamyate | tathā satyarthanāśaḥ syādityetadupadiśyate ||
nanvityetadasambaddhaṃ pareṣṭasyaiva codanāt | paurvāparyavibhāgo 'pi prāguktena virudhyate ||
kṣaṇikatvena yuktaṃ syājjñātatvamatha cettadā | bhūtakālāśrayādbrūyād, pṛthoktasya punarvacaḥ ||
atrāpi na svasiddhāntamūce vyājātparasya tu | bhrāntatvādanyathā pakṣaṃ gṛhītveti sma pṛcchati ||
sahotpattyupalabdhā hi jñānasyaikāntataḥ sthitiḥ | prāgūrdhvaṃ vārthasaṃvitteryugapadveti cintyate ||
evaṃ cārthasya saṃvitteḥ paścājjñānāvabodhanam | bravītu nūnametasya paścādutpadyate 'pi tat ||
na caitac chaktyate tasmādutpatterapakarṣaṇam | karomi tāvattatkālā saṃvittirapi setsyati ||
prākca tadgrahaṇe siddhe bāhyābhyantarayordhruvam | vivekādarśanam, tasmādidam, pūrvaṃ ca coditam ||
yugapadgṛhyamāṇe 'pi nākāro 'rthasya lakṣyate | tasmādarthasya saṃvittiḥ pūrvaṃ yatnena sādhyate ||
yastvetasyottaro granthaḥ prāgevāsau nirūpitaḥ | na tvetatsādhanaṃ sākṣātpūrvaṃ buddherabodhane ||
na parāmṛśyate 'rthātmā jñāto 'pyajñātavadyataḥ | tasānna grahaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ buddheḥ kiṃ kena saṅgatam ||
ataḥ pūrvopalabdhyā yo buddhyākāro 'tra vāñchitaḥ | tannirākaraṇenaiva phalatvādgranthavarṇanā ||
kāmaṃ buddheriti tvetadarthādhīnatvamucyate | na cārtharūpādbhedena dhiyāmasti nirūpaṇam ||
pararūpanirūpyaṃ ca na meyaṃ mṛgatoyavat | asadgrāhyānusāreṇa jñānasaṃvedyatā tava ||
svacchatvāttu svarūpasya kalpitā grāhyatā dhiyām | vāsanopaplavāttena na meyaṃ pāramārthikam ||
nimittaniyatatvaṃ tu samānamubhayorapi | nijaśaktyanusāritvājjñānabāhyārthavādinoḥ ||
tantvarthairapi kasmādvaḥ kriyate kevalaḥ paṭaḥ | nārabhyate ghaṭaḥ kiṃ tairmṛtpiṇḍārthena vā paṭaḥ ||
tantumṛtpiṇḍavijñāne hyanuyojye mate yadi | arthaparyanuyogo 'pi tadvadeva prasajyate ||
arthārambhavyavasthā cetsāmarthyaniyamāśrayā | jñānārambhavyavasthāyāṃ sāmarthyaṃ kena vāryate ||
tasmādyatrobhayordoṣaḥ parihāro 'pi vā samaḥ | naikaḥ paryanuyoktavyastādṛgarthavicāraṇe ||
deśakālanimittāni vyañjakānyarthavādinaḥ | śaktīnāṃ kāraṇasthānāṃ svakāryaniyamaṃ prati ||
śaktayo 'pi ca bhāvānāṃ kāryārthāpattikalpitāḥ | prasiddhāḥ pāramārthikyaḥ pratikāryaṃ vyavasthitāḥ ||
bhavatastu na vijñānādbhinnābhinnā nirūpyate | śaktiḥ saṃvṛtisadbhāvamutsṛjya paramārthataḥ ||
vāsanaiva ca yuṣmābhiḥ śaktiśabdena gīyate | nimittaniyatatvaṃ ca vāsanāyā yaducyate ||
tasyāścāsambhavenaitadapārārthyācca durlabham | deśakālanimittādi na ca te 'sti niyāmakam ||
matvaitadapi cetyāha bhāṣyakāraḥ paraṃ prati | tasmādaparihāro 'yaṃ tantubhyaste yathā paṭaḥ ||
tathā me tantubuddhibhyaḥ paṭabuddhiritīdṛśaḥ | evamādyapramāṇābhyāṃ na tāvadbāhyaśūnyatā ||
āgamasya tu naiveha vyāpāraḥ, ato 'nyathāpi vā | nopamā sadṛśābhāvāt, nārthāpattirviparyayāt ||
tasmādabhāvagamyatvaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ sthitaṃ hi naḥ | evaṃ pramāṇato 'siddhā yaiḥ prameyāśrayocyate ||
bāhyasyāṇusamūhādergrāhyasyāsambhavekṣaṇāt ||
tairāntarāsambhavato yathoktādjñeyatvamanyasya balādupeyam | grāhyā na ceṣṭāḥ paramāṇavo 'taḥ satyaḥ samūhaḥ pratipādanīyaḥ ||
iti bahirviṣayapratipādanād tadabhāvakṛtā matisaṃvṛtiḥ | ubhayatattvavidāṃ paramārthataḥ, kṣamamidaṃ dhuri dharmavicāraṇe ||

§ 5,5 anumānapariccheda amp

pratyakṣāvyabhicāritvādevaṃlakṣaṇakaṃ ca yat | prasiddhamanumānādi na parīkṣyaṃ tadapyataḥ ||
pramātā jñātasambandhaḥ, ekadeśyatha vocyate | karmadhārayapakṣo vā sambandhinyekadeśatā ||
dvayaṃ vā jñātasambandhamupalabdhaṃ parasparam | tasyaikadeśaśabdābhyāmucyete samudāyinau ||
sambandho vyāptiriṣṭātra liṅgādharmasya liṅginā | vyāpyasya gamakatvaṃ ca vyāpakaṃ gamyamiṣyate ||
yo yasya deśakālābhyāṃ samo nyūno 'pi vā bhavet | sa vyāpyo vyāpakastasya samo vābhyadhiko 'pi vā ||
tena vyāpye gṛhīte 'rthe vyāpakastasya gṛhyate | na hyanyathā bhavatyeṣā vyāpyavyāpakatā tayoḥ ||
vyāpakatvagṛhītastu vyāpyo yadyapi vastutaḥ | ādhikye 'pyaviruddhatvādvyāpyaṃ na pratipādayet ||
vispaṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭametacca goviṣāṇitvayormitau | vyāpyatvādgamikā gāvo vyāpikā na viṣāṇitā ||
tena yatrāpyubhau dharmau vyāpyavyāpakasammatau | tatrāpi vyāpyataiva syādaṅgaṃ na vyāpitā miteḥ ||
tena dharmyantareṣveṣā yasya yenaiva yādṛśī | deśe yāvati kāle vā vyāpyatā prāṅ nirūpitā ||
tasya tāvati tādṛksa dṛṣṭo dharmyantare punaḥ | vyāpyāṃśo vyāpakāṃśasya tathaiva pratipādakaḥ ||
bhūyodarśanagamyā ca vyāptiḥ, sāmānyadharmayoḥ | jñāyate bhedahānena, kva ciccāpi viśeṣayoḥ ||
kṛttikodayamālakṣya rohiṇyāsattikḷptivat | vyāpteśca dṛśyamānāyāḥ kaściddharmaḥ prayojakaḥ ||
asmin satyamunā bhāvyamiti śaktyā nirūpyate | anye paraprayuktānāṃ vyāptīnāmupajīvakāḥ ||
tairdṛṣṭairapi naiveṣṭā vyāpakāṃśāvadhāraṇā | ye tu tānapi visrabdhaṃ sādhyasiddhyau prayuñjate ||
sulabhaiḥ pratihetvādidoṣairbhrāmyanti te ciram | teṣvāgamaviruddhatvaṃ svayaṃ ceṣṭavighātitā ||
alaukikavivādāśca varṇyaste haitukaistataḥ | niṣiddhitvena hiṃsānāmadharmatvaṃ prayujyate ||
tadabhāve na tatsiddhirhiṃsātvādaprayojakāt | hetudvayaprayukte ca mithyātve sarvabuddhiṣu ||
jñānatvotpattimattvādisādhako naprayojakaḥ | traivarṇikaprayuktā ca yāgādeḥ svargahetutā ||
na manuṣyatvamātreṇa śūdrasthena prayujyate | kṛtasāvayavatvādiprayuktā ca vināśitā ||
prayatnānantarajñānasadṛśairna prayujyate | jātimattvendriyatvādi vastusanmātrabandhanam ||
śadānityatvasiddhyarthaṃ ko vadedyo na tārkikaḥ | tasmādya eva yasyārtho dṛṣṭaḥ sādhanaśaktitaḥ ||
sa eva gamakastasya na prasaṅgānvito 'pi yaḥ | upāttaścaikadeśābhyāṃ dharmyapyatraikadeśatā ||
apārārthye hi dhūmādeḥ svarūpairnaikadeśatā | sa eva cobhayātmāyaṃ gamyo gamaka eva vā ||
asiddhenaikadeśena gamyaḥ siddhena bodhakaḥ | ataḥ pṛthagabhinno vāprayoktāṇāṃ vivakṣaya ||
anityaḥ kṛtako yasmāddhūmavānagnimāniti | dharmyabhinnamupādānam, bhedo 'trāgniritīdṛśe ||
ekadeśaviśiṣṭaśca dharmyevātrānumīyate | na hi tannirapekṣatve sambhavatyanumeyatā ||
na dharmamātraṃ siddhatvāt, tathā dharmī, tathobhayam | vyastaṃ vāpi samastaṃ vā svātantryeṇānumīyate ||
ekadeśasya liṅgatvaṃ sādhyenānugamo 'sya ca | dvayaṃ ca na syādiṣṭaṃ satpakṣeṣveṣu yathākramam ||
anityatvādayo dharmāḥ kṛtakatvādayo na hi | dhvaninānugamo naiṣāṃ nobhayasyobhayena vā ||
sambandho 'pyanupādānānnāmnā ṣaṣṭhyāpi vā mitau | na cāpyanugamastena liṅgasyeha nidarśyate ||
na cākāradvayaṃ tasya sādhyasādhanabhāgbhavet | tasmadarthagṛhītatvānmatubarthasya gamyatā ||
na svāntantryeṇa mantavyā, yathā daṇḍyādiśabdataḥ | viśīṣṭārthapratītau syātsambandho nāntarīyakaḥ ||
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvamāpannau dvāvimāvataḥ | gamyau, aṅgāṅgibhāvastu kaiścidiṣṭo vikalpataḥ ||
sarvathā dharmiṇo dharmo dharmeṇa tvavagamyate | viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatve na viśeṣo 'vadhāryate ||
tatrotaraṃ vadantyanye yadi dharmī viśeṣaṇam | hetudharmeṇa sambandhastasyāprādhānyataḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
pradhānatvāddhi dharmeṇa sambandho vākyato bhavet | tatrāsambhavataḥ paścātkalpyo 'sau dharminā saha ||
dhvanerityatha vā vācyam, anvayasya tu darśane | bhedopāttasya dharmasya guṇābhāvo na duṣyati ||
agnerdeśaviśiṣṭatve na caitatpakṣalakṣaṇam | viśiṣṭatāsya deśena bhavedevamprakārikā ||
yo 'gniḥ so 'sti kva ciddeśe yo dṛṣṭo yatra tatra vā | agniḥ pūrvānubhūto vā deśamātreṇa saṅgataḥ ||
yo 'gniḥ so 'nena yukto vā, yo dṛṣṭo 'nena so 'tha vā | yo 'yaṃ sa deśamātreṇa yuktaḥ, pūrveṇa vāpyayam ||
etaddeśaviśiṣṭo vā yo 'yamagniriti, iha tu | pūrvayoḥ siddhasādhyatvaṃ pareṣu syādviruddhatā ||
vyāptiretena deśena sarvāgnīnāṃ na yujyate | nāpi pūrvasya, nāpyeṣa vahniḥ sarvairviśiṣyate ||
deśaiḥ, pūrveṇa vāpyasya na deśena viśeṣyatā | etaddeśaviśiṣṭo 'yamityetatkathyate katham ||
yadā deśānapekṣo 'gnirnāyamityavadhāryate | agneḥ pūrvataraṃ cātra deśa evāvadhāryate ||
tajjñānakālabuddhaśca na deśaḥ syādviśeṣaṇam | deśasya parvatādestu svarūpe pāvakādṛte ||
gṛhīte 'gniviśiṣṭasya punarjñānaṃ na duṣyati | tasmāddharmaviśiṣṭasya dharmiṇaḥ syātprameyatā ||
sā deśasyāgniyuktasya, dhūmasyānyaiśca kalpitā | nanu śabdavadeva syālliṅgagamyaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||
naivam, na hyatra liṅgasya śaktyanekatvakalpanā | na ca tasyānumeyatvam, viśeṣyaścāvadhāritaḥ ||
viśiṣṭatvena cājñānāttanmātrasyānumeyatā | nanu dhūmaviśeṣyatve hetoḥ pakṣaikadeśatā ||
naitadasti, viśeṣe hi sādhye sāmānyahetutā | dhūmatajjānasambandhasmṛtiprāmāṇyakalpane ||
phalena viṣayaikatvaṃ tadvyāpārātpuroditam | prameyadhīpramāṇatvaṃ bhāṣyakārastu manyate ||
pratyakṣāniyamoktaśca sarvatraivānuṣajyate | anumānagṛhītasya tenaiva pratipādanam ||
parebhyo vāñchatā vācyaḥ pūrvapakṣo yathoditaḥ | tatra dharmiṇamuddiśya sādhyadharmo vidhīyate ||
niyamastadvipakṣācca kalpyate nāvirodhinaḥ | asannikṛṣṭavācā ca dvayamatra jihāsitam ||
tādrūpyeṇa paricchittistadviparyayato 'pi ca | pramitasya pramāṇe hi nāpekṣā jāyate punaḥ ||
tādrūpyeṇa paricchinne pramāṇaṃ niṣphalaṃ param | vaiparītyaparicchinne nāvakāśaḥ parasya tu ||
mūle tasya hyanutpanne pūrveṇa viṣayo hṛtaḥ | pratyakṣādeśca ṣaṭkasya yenaivārtho 'vadhāritaḥ ||
tenaivottarabādhaḥ syād, vikalpāderasambhavāt | agrāhyatā tu śabdādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virudhyate ||
teṣāmaśrāvaṇatvādi viruddhamanumānataḥ | na hi śrāvaṇatā nāma pratyakṣeṇāvagamyate ||
sānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ gamyate badhirādiṣu | tridhā śabdavirodhaḥ syātpratijñādivibhāgataḥ ||
pratijñāpūrvasañjalpasarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ | yāvajjīvamahaṃ maunītyuktimātreṇa bādhyate ||
sarvavākyamṛṣātve tu dharmoktyaivātmabādhanam | dharmyuktyāhaṃ yato jātaḥ sā vandhyā jananī mama ||
bauddhasya śabdanityatvaṃ pūrvopetena bādhyate | candraśabdābhidheyatvaṃ śaśino yo niṣedhati ||
sa sarvalokasiddhena candrajñānena bādhyate | jñātagogavayākāraṃ prati yaḥ sādhayedidam ||
na gorgavayasādṛśyaṃ tasya bādhopamānataḥ | gehāvagatanāstitvo jīvaṃścaitro yadā bahiḥ ||
nāstīti sādhyate bādhastatrārthāpattito bhavet | agnāvadāhake sādhye śabde cānabhidhāyake ||
śrotrādināstitāyāṃ ca śabdānityatvasādhane | śrutārthāpattibādho 'tra yadāptoktinivārite ||
divābhujau niṣidhyeta hetunā rātribhojanam | śaśaśṛṅgādisadbhāvavirodho 'nupalabdhitaḥ ||
evaṃ ca dharmasambandhabādhastāvadudāhṛtaḥ | dharmadharmyubhayeṣāṃ ca svarūpasvaviśeṣayoḥ ||
śrutyarthākṣiptayorvākye vācyaḥ sarvapramāṇakaḥ | tṛṇādivikriyāhetoragnimaddhimasādhane ||
pratyakṣāvagatāc chaityāttadviśeṣotthabādhanam | adharmo vihito duḥkhaṃ karotyalpamitīha tu ||
vihitatvādadharmasya svarūpasyaiva bādhanam | tathā duḥkhanimittatvaṃ viśeṣastasya bādhyate ||
ayathārthā dhiyaḥ sarvāḥ ityukte dvayabādhanam | svarūpasvaviśeṣābhyām, taddhīmithyātvasādhanāt ||
kṣaṇikātyantamithyātve viśeṣau ca dvayoriha | darśanādekadeśasyetyanenaitadvyudasyate ||
yatraikasyobhayorvāpi saṃśayādhīviparyayāḥ | śaityānna dāhako bahniścākṣuṣatvādanityatā ||
śabdasyetyevamādau tu dvayoḥ siddho viparyayaḥ | kṛtakatvaguṇatvādau parokte yājñikaṃ prati ||
svokte caivamprakāre syādasiddho 'nyatarasya tu | bāṣpādibhāvasandigdho dvayoranyatarasya vā ||
dhūmastridhāpyasiddhaḥ syāt, evaṃ tāvatsvarūpataḥ | eta eva prakārāḥ syurāśrayāsiddhikalpane ||
jñāte 'pi hi svarūpeṇa nātaddharme 'sti hetutā | sarvatra dṛṣṭakāryatvādātmā sarvagatastviti ||
bauddhaṃ pratyāśrayāsiddhaḥ, laukikādestu saṃśayaḥ | bāṅmātrāsiddhimātreṇa vyavahārāprakalpanāt ||
dvābhyāṃ yo 'sattvato jñātastadvaco dūṣaṇaṃ matam | itaratsādhanaṃ tu syādvādinā yadi sādhyate ||
nirākaraṇasiddhau vā dūṣaṇaṃ prativādinaḥ | sandehaviparītatvahetū cātra nirākṛtau ||
jñātasambandhavacanāt, trayaḥ saṃśayahetavaḥ | san sādhye tadabhāve vā dvābhyāṃ vyāvṛtta eva ca ||
dvau viruddhārthasambaddhau yāvekatraikadeśini | prameyānityatāmūrtidharmāḥ sādhāraṇā dvayoḥ ||
nityāyatnotthayatnotthānityeṣu dviranityataḥ | nityā bhūrgandhavattvena syādasādhāraṇastvayam ||
niścayaikāṅgavaikalyādeṣa saṃśayakāraṇam | sādhāraṇo yathā dṛṣṭo buddhidvayanimittakaḥ ||
viruddhaikānavāpteśca saṃśaye kāraṇaṃ matam | atrāsādhāraṇo nāsti tadabhāvamukhena tu ||
dvayāsattvavirodhācca mataḥ saṃśayakāraṇam | sandigdhahetutā caiṣāṃ viṣayāpekṣayocyate ||
nirṇayasyāpi hetutvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sādhyāntare yataḥ | vyavacchedānvayau labdhvā, niṣkriyādāvamūrtivat ||
kṣityekadeśasiddhatve gandhavattvasya hetutā | yatrāpratyakṣatā vāyorarūpatvena sādhyate ||
sparśātpratyakṣatā vāsau viruddhāvyabhicāritā | ke cijjātyantaraṃ caināṃ varṇayantyapare punaḥ ||
sādhāraṇatvamaṃśena samastaṃ vāpyananvayam | pratijñā yatra bādhyeta pūrvoktairyasya sādhanaiḥ ||
tatparājayataḥ kāryo nirṇayo bādhavarjanāt | kva citsaṃśayahetū yau pratyekatvena lakṣitau ||
saṅghāte nirṇayastābhyāmūrdhvatākākavattvavat | pratyekaṃ saṃhatau vāpi gamakāvavirodhinau ||
tasmādbhinnau viruddhārthau hetū cātra nidarśitau | ṣoḍhā viruddhatāmāhuścaturddhā vaikadhāpi vā ||
śrutyarthoktasya bādhāyāṃ pratijñārthasya hetunā | nityatve kṛtakatvasya dharmabādhādviruddhatā ||
bādho dharmaviśeṣasya yadā tvevaṃ prayujyate | arthavacchabdarūpaṃ syātprāksambandhāvadhāraṇāt ||
vibhaktimattvātpaścādvatsvarūpeṇeti cāśrite | asvarūpārthayogastu paścāc chabdasya dṛśyate ||
tena prāgapi sambandhādasvarūpārthatā bhavet | ihapratyayahetutvāddravyādervyatiricyate ||
samavāyo yathehāyaṃ ghaṭa ityādisaṅgatiḥ | atrāpyasamavāyatvaṃ saṃyogasyeva sidhyati ||
tena dharmisvarūpasya vaiparītyādviruddhatā | yacca sattāvadekatvaṃ samavāyasya kalpitam ||
tatra saṃyogavadbhedātsyādviśeṣaviruddhatā | nityamātmāstitā kaiścidyadā sautrāntikaṃ prati ||
sādhyate 'vayavābhāvādvyomavaddvayabādhanam | tadobhayaviśeṣasya bādho 'yaṃ sādhyate yadā ||
pārārthyaṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ saṅghātāc chayanādivat | śayane saṅghapārārthyaṃ bhautikavyāptahetuke ||
ātmānaṃ prati pārārthyamasiddhamiti bādhanam | asaṃhataparārthatve dṛṣṭe saṃhatatāpi ca ||
anahaṅkārikatvaṃ ca cakṣurādeḥ prasajyate | gamakasyaikadeśasya vyāptirgamyeti bhāṣitum ||
sādhyasādharmyavaidharmyadṛṣṭāntaḥ pratipādyate | tatra hetvarthamuddiśya sādhyopādānamiṣyate ||
uddeśyo vyāpyate dharmo vyāpakaścetaro mataḥ | yadvṛttayogaḥ prāthamyamityādyuddeśalakṣaṇam ||
tadvṛttameva kāraśca syādupādeyalakṣaṇam | vadatyarthaṃ svaśaktyā ca śabdo vaktranapekṣayā ||
sādhyahetutvamarthānāṃ vyāptiśaktyanurodhataḥ | tatrājñānādyadā vakta sahacāravivakṣayā ||
viparyayeṇa vā hetau na vyāptatvaṃ vivakṣati | vivakṣannapi vā śabdaṃ tadyogyaṃ na vadedyadi ||
ghaṭe kṛtakanāśitve nāśivyāptaṃ kṛtena vā | na tadeṣṭasya hetutvam, syādaniṣṭasya caiva tat ||
tasmādvyāpyatvarūpeṇa vācyo hetutvasammataḥ | yadā samyakprayukte 'pi vākye 'rtho na tathā bhavet ||
sādhyahetūbhayavyāptiśūnyatvātparamārthataḥ | nityo dhvaniramūrttatvātkarmavatparamāṇuvat ||
ghaṭavadvyomavaccāpi, tadasadvādinaṃ prati | dharmyasiddhāvapi hyevaṃ dṛṣṭāntābhāsatā bhavet ||
tatsadbhāve 'pi ca vyomni dvayayukte 'pi kīrtite | karmādyālocanādvyāptirhetornāstīti varjanam ||
vyāptyā sādharmya ukte ca na vaidharmyamapekṣyate | sahabhāvitvadṛṣṭyā tu yadā vyāptiṃ na lakṣayet ||
paraḥ sādharmyadṛṣṭāntāttacca nāpekṣate yadā | vaktā vā sahabhāvitvaṃ śuddhaṃ tena vadedyadā ||
viparītānvayaṃ vāpi tatsamādhitsayā tadā | pūrvajñānopamardena vaidharmyeṇeṣṭasādhanam ||
sāhityamātraṃ pūrvoktaṃ hetostatropayujyate | vyāpyavyāpakabhāvo hi bhāvayoryādṛgiṣyate ||
tayorabhāvayostasmādviparītaḥ pratīyate | dhūmabhāve 'gnibhāvena vyāpte 'nagnistataścyutaḥ ||
adhūma eva vidyetetyevaṃ vyāpyatvamaśnute | tathānagnāvadhūmena vyāpte dhūmastatacyutaḥ ||
anyatrānavakāśatvādvyāpyate dhruvamagninā | vyāpakau tu yadocyete bhāvābhāvau tadā tataḥ ||
naiva vyāpyādvipakṣasya pracyutiḥ kathitā bhavet | tasmāddhūmena sādhyatvamagneḥ prārthayate yadā ||
tadānagniradhūmena vyāpto vācyaḥ, na cānyathā | anagnyadhūmasāhitye vyāptervāpi viparyaye ||
na prastutopakāraḥ syādanyadvāpi prasādhyate | yatrāpyarthasya śūnyatvaṃ dvābhyāmekena vā bhavet ||
yadanityaṃ tu tanmūrtamaṇuvadbuddhivatkhavat | sādhyena vyāptisiddhyaiva vyatireko 'tra kathyate ||
yasyāyaṃ nāstyasau hetustena sādhyena nāpyate | tena dṛṣṭe 'pi sāhitye na sarvo gamya iṣyate ||
sahadṛṣṭirna sambandho vyāptirnaiva ca tāvatā | mūrtānityatvayukte 'pi tasmādaṅgīkṛte ghaṭe ||
karmādau vyāptyabhāvena na dṛṣṭāntatvamiṣyate | aśeṣāpekṣitatvācca saukaryāccāpyadarśanāt ||
sādhane yadyapīṣṭo 'tra vyatireko 'numāṃ prati | tāvatā na hyanaṅgatvaṃ yuktiḥ śābde hi vakṣyate ||
bodhaprasaṅgo bhedānāṃ na cāvyāpterbhaviṣyati | astisāmānyavastveṣu vyāpitā tatra gamyatām ||
ke citsādharmyadṛṣṭānte vyāptyāpi kathite punaḥ | vaidharmyoktimapīcchanti, vyāvṛttiniyamecchayā ||
hetau sādharmyadṛṣṭāntātsādhyenaivāvadhārite | vyāvṛttiḥ sarvataḥ prāptā sādhyābhāve niyamyate ||
tattu mandaphalaṃ yasmātpakṣe 'pyevaṃ nirūpitam | vyāpakābhāvamātraṃ hi vyāpyānnityaṃ nivartate ||
tasmādyathaiva śuklatve paṭasyokte virodhinām | nivṛttirna tu dairdhyādestathātrāpi bhaviṣyati ||
dvaividhyaṃ nopapannaṃ tu yathaiva hyagnidhūmayoḥ | pratyakṣadṛṣṭaḥ sambandho gatiprāptyostathaiva hi ||
āditye 'nupalabdhiścenna deśe 'pyadhunātane | kva cittatropalabdhiśceddevadatte 'pi dṛśyatām ||
yadi dharmyantarāpekṣā tatra sāmānyadṛṣṭatā | syādagnidhūmayoḥ saiva, tasmādevaṃ pracakṣate ||
pratyakṣadṛṣṭasambandhaṃ yayoreva viśeṣayoḥ | gomayendhanatajjanyaviśeṣādimatiḥ kṛtā ||
taddeśasthena tenaiva gatvā kālāntare 'pi tam | yadāgnirbudhyate, tasya pūrvabodhātpunaḥ punaḥ ||
sandihyamānasadbhāvavastubodhātpramāṇatā | viśeṣadṛṣṭametacca likhitaṃ vindhyavāsinā ||
ākṛtyoreva caiṣeṣṭā vyavacchedena kena cit | hetusādhyavyavastheti viśeṣo nopadarśitaḥ ||
agnidhūmāntaratve ca vācye sāmānyato mitau | sāmānyadṛṣṭamekāntādatretyāditya ucyate ||
pratyakṣaviṣayatvaṃ ca sāmānyasya prasādhitam | vastutvaṃ ca, atra heturvā dvayasyāpyabhidhīyate ||
dhūmādagnyanumānasya vastvālambanatā bhavet | abhāvānyapramāṇatvātsvārthe śrotrādibuddhivat ||
sāmānyasya ca vastutvaṃ pratyakṣagrāhyatāpi ca | abhāvānyaprameyatvādasādhāraṇavastuvat ||
sāmānyaṃ nānumānena vinā yasya pratīyate | na ca liṅgavinirmuktamanumānaṃ pravartate ||
asāmānyasya liṅgatvaṃ na ca kena cidiṣyate | na cānavagataṃ liṅgaṃ kiñcidasti prakāśakam ||
tasya vāpyanumānena syādanyena gatiḥ punaḥ | tadutpattiśca liṅgātsyātsāmānyajñānasaṃhitāt ||
tasya cāpyanumānatvāt bhavelliṅgena codbhavaḥ | anumānāntarādeva jñānenaivaṃ ca kalpane ||
liṅgaliṅgyanumānānāmānantyādekaliṅgini | gatiryugasahasreṣu bahuṣvapi na vidyate ||
atha sāmānyabhūte 'pi liṅge 'nyasmādgatirbhavet | pramāṇādapramāṇādvā, tathā liṅgigatirbhavet ||
evamapyanumānasya nityocchedaḥ prasajyate | pramāṇāntarameva syātsāmānyasyāvabodhakam ||
apramāṇāvabuddhādvā liṅgālliṅgini yā matiḥ | sāpi mithyā bhavennityaṃ bāṣpajātāgnibuddhivat ||
nanvapramāṇabhūtāpi sambandhasmṛtiriṣyate | yathā liṅgigatau hetustathā liṅgagatirbhavet ||
tatra yatpūrvavijñānaṃ tasya prāmāṇyamiṣyate | tadupasthānamātreṇa smṛteḥ syāccaritārthatā ||
na tu liṅgagatau kiñcitpramāṇamupapadyate | tadabhāvāsmṛtiścātra na kathañcitpravartate ||
smārtametadabhedena vijñānamiti yo vadet | tasya vandhyāsute 'pyasti nūnaṃ smaraṇaśaktatā ||
na cāsādhāraṇo 'rthātmā sāmānyajñānakāraṇam | yasmānnāsyāvinābhāvastena dṛṣṭaḥ kathañcana ||
syādvā sambandhadṛṣṭyāsau sāmānyaṃ kṛtakatvavat | na hyasādhāraṇaṃ vastu pūrvatreha ca vidyate ||
na cāpyavyapadeśasya vikalparahitasya ca | vinā pūrvānusandhānālliṅgatvamupapadyate ||
kalpyante ca viśeṣā ye te 'pyaliṅgamananvayāt | etasmādeva hetoḥ syāttajñānasyāpyaliṅgatā ||
sāmānyarūpatāyāṃ vā tathaivānavadhāraṇam | kva cidvā dṛṣṭasambandhe sarvaḥ pratyāyako bhavet ||
sambandhānubhavo 'vaśyameṣitavyaśca liṅganaḥ | anumānapravṛttestu prāgjñānaṃ tatra nāsti te ||
na cāpi vāsanāmātrālliṅgajñānasya sambhavaḥ | liṅgijñānaṃ ca tadvatsyāttrirūpālliṅgato na tat ||
tatrābhāvasya liṅgatvaṃ na cāsāvānumānikaḥ | pramāṇāntaragamyatvāttatra doṣo na jāyate ||
pratyakṣāvagatālliṅgādyasya liṅgigatirbhavet | tasya nāto 'dhikaṃ kiñcitprārthanīyaṃ prasajyate ||
yatrāpyanumitālliṅgālliṅgini grahaṇaṃ bhavet | tatrāpi maulikaṃ liṅgaṃ pratyakṣādeva gamyate ||
liṅgatvaṃ kṛtakatvādau kriyāyāḥ kārakasya vā | pratyakṣatvaṃ ca tasyeṣṭamiti dūraṃ na gamyate ||
evaṃ śabdopamānādau sāmānyāśrayatā yataḥ | taddaussthityena daussthityaṃ sarvatrātaḥ prasajyate ||
tasmātpratyakṣapūrvatvaṃ pramāṇāntara iṣyate | pratyakṣatvaṃ ca sāmānye nānyathā hi gatirbhavet ||
pratyakṣālambanatvaṃ ca viśeṣasya kathaṃ bhavet | yadā vastvantarāpekṣaḥ sāmānyāṃśaḥ sa kīrtyate ||
rūpādayo hi sāmānyaṃ sarve nīlādyapekṣayā | svaviśeṣānapekṣyātha nīlādīnāṃ samānatā ||
te cāpi tāvatsāmānyaṃ yāvatsyuḥ paramāṇavaḥ | dvyaṇukasyāpi yadrūpaṃ taddhi sādhāraṇaṃ dvayoḥ ||
na cāntyena viśeṣeṇa vyavahāro 'sti kasya cit | na ca pratyakṣatā tasya saṅghāte kevalasya vā ||
bhedenāgṛhyamāṇasya nābhedo grāhyatāṃ vrajet | na ca bhinneṣvabhinnatvabuddhergrāhyatvasambhavaḥ ||
samudāyo na vāpyasti bhavatāṃ na ca sarvadā | sarveṣāmasatārthena pratyayotpattisambhavaḥ ||
na caikajātiyogena vināsti samudāyatā | samudāye 'pi cāṇutvaṃ naiteṣāmapagacchati ||
sāmānyamityadṛśye 'pi tena sāmānya eva naḥ | vyāsaṅginī bhavatyeṣā dhīrvināpyekakalpanāt ||
vyāsajya vartamānasya sāmānyasya yathendriyaiḥ | grahaṇaṃ tadvadeva syātprativyaktiniveśinaḥ ||
mīmāṃsakaiśca nāvaśyamiṣyante paramāṇavaḥ | yadbalenopalabdhasya mithyātvaṃ kalpayedbhavān ||
samūharūpaṃ pratyakṣamadṛśyaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ | yo 'pahnute śaśasyāpi so 'bhāvaṃ śṛṅgato vadet ||
samūhaparamārthatve sthite tatsiddhihetukā | yadi nāmāvagamyeta paramāṇvastitā punaḥ ||
tasmādyadgṛhyate vastu yena rūpeṇa sarvadā | tattathaivābhyupetavyaṃ sāmānyamatha vetarat ||
sattādisāmānyamapekṣya sarvaṃ gotvādi sādhāraṇatāmupaiti | tasmādasādhāraṇamakṣagamyaṃ vadanna sāmānyamapahnuvīta ||
sāmānyarūpeṇa na gṛhyate cet, kiṃ vāstyasādhāraṇabuddhiratra | yadvastu lokaḥ pratipadyate 'smindvidhāpi tacchaktyata eva vaktum ||

§ 5,6 śabdapariccheda sbp

pratyakṣādiṣu vaktavyaṃ śabdamātrasya lakṣaṇam | adatitvariteneha kiṃ śāstrādabhidhīyate ||
sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ tyaktvā viśeṣasyaiva lakṣaṇam | na śakyaṃ kevalaṃ vaktumito 'pyasya na vācyatā ||
yaccoktaṃ śabdavijñānādarthe jñānamitīdṛśam | aviśiṣṭaṃ viśiṣṭasya na tacchāstrasya lakṣaṇam ||
pravṛttirvā nivṛttirvā nityena kṛtakena vā | puṃsāṃ yenopadiśyeta tacchāstramabhidhīyate ||
svarūpakathanaṃ yattu kasya cittatra dṛśyate | tadaṅgatvena tasyāpi śāstratvamavagamyate ||
bhāvanāyāṃ samastāyāṃ vākyādevopajāyate | pravṛttirvā nivṛttirvā tacchāstraṃ na padādyataḥ ||
aparīkṣāmiṣeṇāpi lakṣaṇāni vadannayam | na svatantropayogitvanirapekṣāṇi jalpati ||
tatra yallokavākyasthaṃ kathayecchabdalakṣaṇam | vedaṃ vyākhyātukāmasya tannātīvopayujyate ||
pratyakṣādyupayogaṃ tu varṇamātrāditaḥ puraḥ | śāstrārthajñānavelāyāṃ matvā tallakṣaṇaṃ kṛtam ||
yattu gāmānayetyādivākyasthaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam | tasya nehopayogo 'sti tasmāc chāstragataṃ kṛtam ||
veśeṣaśca na sāmānyamantareṇāsti kaścana | tasmāttamapyudāhṛtya sāmānyaṃ lakṣayetsukham ||
sāmānyarūpamapyetadadhikārādviśiṣyate | codanā copadeśaśca śāstramevetyudāhṛtam ||
yathā ca codanāśabdo vaidikyāmeva vartate | śabdajñānārthavijñānaśabdau śāstre tathā sthitau ||
pratyakṣādyaparīkṣyatve tadantarbhāvahetukam | śāstrasyāpyaparīkṣyatvamanayaiva dhiyoditam ||
tatrānumānamevedaṃ bauddhairvaiśeṣikaiḥ śritam | bhedaḥ sāṃkhyādibhistviṣṭo na tūktaṃ bhedakāraṇam ||
pūrvasaṃskārayuktāntyavarṇavākyādikalpanā | vivakṣādi ca dhūmādau nāstītyetena bhinnatā ||
yairuktā tatra vaidharmyavikalpasamajātitā | dhūmānityaviṣāṇyādiviśeṣānna hi bhinnatā ||
tailakṣaṇyaparityāgo yāvanna pratipādyate | tāvadviśeṣamātreṇa vadato jātitā bhavet ||
yatheṣṭaviniyogena pratītiryāpi śabdataḥ | na dhūmāderitīhāpi vyabhicāro 'ṅgavṛttibhiḥ ||
hastasaṃjñādayo ye 'pi yadarthapratipādane | bhaveyuḥ kṛtasaṅketāste na liṅgamiti sthitiḥ ||
puruṣākṣiptatāyāṃ ca tathaiva vyabhicāritā | padavaidikavākyānāṃ na satyavyāpitā bhavet ||
sambandhātubhavaścāyaṃ so 'nyatrāpi vilakṣaṇaḥ | etasmin puruṣāpekṣā deśāpekṣāgnidhūmayoḥ ||
kālādyapekṣayā cānyaḥ, uktā cānyairabhinnatā | āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyādanumānataḥ ||
na cāpūrvādiśabdānāṃ bhedātsarvatra bhinnatā | na cehāśvādiśabdebhyo bhedasteṣāṃ pratīyate ||
na cāpyajñātasambandhaṃ padaṃ kiñcitprakāśakam | sambandhānanubhūtyāto na syādananumānatā ||
tulyākāratayāpyatra śabdajñānārthataddhiyām | agnidhūmeṣvadṛṣṭatvānna bhedastannivāraṇāt ||
pratibimbeṣvanaikānto bimbaṃ yādṛgghi darpaṇe | tādṛṅ mukhādi budhyante, na cātrānanumānatā ||
pratyakṣatā tadāpyatra tadānyairvyabhicāritā | yatra pādādi bambena gatānāmanumīyate ||
ekavākyātsakṛccoktānnāpyanekasya tatkṣaṇam | syādviruddhāviruddhasya bodhādetasya bhinnatā ||
liṅgasyāpi hi tādrūpyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hetuviruddhayoḥ | virodhānnānumānaṃ cet, syādanāgamatāpi te ||
yatra caikārthatā vākye tatra syādanumānatā | sakṛduccarite cāsminvivakṣaikaiva dṛśyate ||
yastvanirdhāritārthānāmanekapratibhodbhavaḥ | sa liṅge 'pyasphuṭe dṛṣṭastasmānnaitena bhidyate ||
dṛṣṭāntānabhidhānaṃ ca dhūmādau vyabhicāritam | prasiddhatvāddhi tatrāpi na dṛṣṭānto 'bhidhīyate ||
anabhyaste tvapekṣante śabde sambandhinaḥ smṛtim | atra pratyukta ityevaṃ budhyante hi cirātkva cit ||
paroktā hetavaścātra nābhedasya nivāritāḥ | śabdānumānayoraikyaṃ dhūmādagnyanumānavat ||
anvayavyatirekābhyāmekapratyakṣadarśanāt | sambandhapūrvakatvācca pratipattirito yataḥ ||
pratyakṣānyapramāṇatvāttadadṛṣṭārthabodhanāt | sāmānyaviṣayatvācca traikālyaviṣayāśrayāt ||
kaiścinmīmāṃsakairukto bhedo 'tra viṣayāntarāt | pūrvābhyāṃ hyaparicchinne śāstramarthe pravartate ||
tatrāpi nāgamatvaṃ syātpuruṣokte, tathāstu cet | pratyayaḥ kinnimitto 'rthe, vaktṛbuddheḥ, kuto nvasau ||
na śabdārthasya sāliṅgaṃ na śabdo 'syāḥ kathañcana | viśeṣo gamyate tābhyāṃ na caitasyānumeyatā ||
tena vakturabhiprāye pratyakṣādyanirūpite | puruṣoktirapi śroturāgamatvaṃ prapadyate ||
na cāpyananumeyatvamāgamārthasya śakyate | liṅgaṃ hi śabda evāsya dhūmo 'gneriva kalpyate ||
na cāpyananumeyatvātpramāṇāntaragamyatā | rūpasyāśrāvaṇatvena na hyapratyakṣateṣyate ||
evaṃ sati svayūthyā na ke cinnātiprapañcinaḥ | anumānaviśeṣo 'yamīdṛgdharmasya bodhakaḥ ||
bhaviṣyatyartharūpaṃ tu liṅgaṃ dharme nirākṛtam | saṃjñānumānatecchā tu na duṣyedāgame 'pi naḥ ||
lakṣaṇena tvabhinnatvaṃ yadi śabdānumānayoḥ | vedajñānāpramāṇatvaṃ syādatallakṣaṇatvataḥ ||
āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyānnṛvacassu hi | lakṣaṇenānumānatvātprāmāṇyaṃ siddhimṛcchati ||
vede tvāptanarābhāvātsambandhānubhavādṛte | lakṣaṇaṃ nānumānasyetyaprāmāṇyaṃ prasajyate ||
nanvekadeśasatyatve tasya syādanumānatā | vedatvādagnihotrādau vāyukṣepiṣṭhavākyavat ||
nādityayūpe 'naikāntāt, tadvadvā gauṇatā bhavet | nātaḥ pratyanumānānāmevaṃ pūrvoktayā viśā ||
tasmāllakṣaṇabhedena yadi śabdapramāṇatā | samā loke ca vede ca siddhā vedapramāṇatā ||
tena cāptopadeśatvaṃ na syādāgamalakṣaṇam | nāptasya sambhavo vede, loke nāsmātpramāṇatā ||
purastādvarṇitaṃ hyetat, tasmāc chabdena yā matiḥ | tasyāḥ svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ na cetsyāddoṣadarśanam ||
anumānena caitasya prāmāṇyaṃ kevalaṃ samam | pade tāvatkṛto yatnaḥ parairityatra varṇyate ||
viṣayo 'nyādṛśastāvaddṛśyate liṅgaśabdayoḥ | sāmānyaviṣayatvaṃ ca padasya sthāpayiṣyati ||
dharmādharmaviśiṣṭaśca liṅgītyetacca sādhitam | na tāvadanumānaṃ hi yāvattadviṣayaṃ na tat ||
sāmānyādatiriktaṃ tu śābde vākyasya gocaraḥ | sāmarthyādanumeyatvādaśrute 'pi padāntare ||
saṃkhyādimān padārthaścet, na tāvatso 'vyayādiṣu | yatrāpi te pratīyante tatra vyakterviśeṣaṇam ||
padāntarābhidheyasya tādarthyācca kriyātmanaḥ | vākyārthe 'pi padaṃ yatra gomadādi prayujyate ||
satyapyatra viśeṣṭatve siddhatvānnaiva pakṣatā | tāvāneva hi tatrārtho yaḥ pūrvamavadhāritaḥ ||
bhedabuddheśca vaiṣamyaṃ prakṛtipratyayārthayoḥ | viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyārthasvātantryagrahaṇaṃ na ca ||
viśeṣyapūrvikā tatra buddhiścātra viparyayaḥ | atha śabdo 'rthavattvena pakṣaḥ kasmānna kalpyate ||
pratijñārthaikadeśo hi hetustatra prasajyate | pakṣe dhūmaviśeṣe ca sāmānyaṃ heturiṣyate ||
śabdatvaṃ gamakaṃ nātra gośabdatvaṃ niṣetsyate | vyaktireva viśiṣyāto hetuścaikā prasajyate ||
bhavedvyañjakabhedāccet, na tvevaṃ pratyayo 'sti naḥ | kathaṃ cāsya viśiṣṭatvaṃ na tāvaddeśakālataḥ ||
tatpratītiviśiṣṭaścet, paraṃ kimanumīyate | na pratyāyanaśaktiśca viśeṣasyānumīyate ||
viśeṣāṇāṃ na śaktirhi saikadeśe 'gnijātivat | sāmānyasyaiva śaktatvaṃ pakṣo hetustadeva ca ||
tasmādarthaviśiṣṭasya na śabdasyānumeyatā | kathaṃ ca pakṣadharmatvaṃ śabdasyeha nirūpyate ||
na kriyākartṛsambandhādṛte sambandhanaṃ kva cit | rājā bharttā manuṣyasya tena rājñaḥ sa ucyate ||
vṛkṣastiṣṭhati śākhāsu tā vā tatreti tasya tāḥ | deśe 'gnimati dhūmasya kartṛtvaṃ bhavanaṃ prati ||
kāryakāraṇabhāvādau kriyā sarvatra vidyate | na cānavagatākāraḥ sambandho 'stīti gamyate ||
na cāstyasati sambandhe ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣo 'pi vā | tasmānna pakṣadharmo 'yamiti śakyā nirūpaṇā ||
nivṛtte 'nyatra sambandhe ye 'pi tadviṣayātmanā | vadeyuḥ pakṣadharmatvaṃ śabdasyānupalabdhivat ||
tairapyetannirūpyaṃ tu śabdastadviṣayaḥ katham | na taddeśādisadbhāvo nābhimukhyādi tasya vā ||
tasmādutpādayatyeṣa yato 'rthaviṣayā matim | tena tadviṣayaḥ śabda iti dharmatvakalpanā ||
tatra vācakatāyāṃ ca siddhāyāṃ pakṣadharmatā | na pratītyaṅgatāṃ gacchenna caivamanumānatā ||
gamakatvācca dharmatvaṃ dharmatvādgamako yadi | syādanyonyāśrayatvaṃ hi tasmānnaiṣāpi kalpanā ||
na cāgṛhītasambandhāḥ svarūpavyatirekataḥ | śabdaṃ jānanti yenātra pakṣadharmamatirbhavet ||
na ca svarūpamātreṇa dhūmādeḥ pakṣadharmatā | na cāpi pūrvasambandhamapekṣyaiṣā prasajyate ||
dhūmavānayamityevamapūrvasyāpi jāyate | pakṣadharmamatiḥ, tena bhidyetottaralakṣaṇāt ||
na tvatra pūrvasambandhādadhikā pakṣadharmatā | na cārthapratyayātpūrvamityanaṅgamiyaṃ bhavet ||
na ca dharmī gṛhīto 'tra yena taddharmatā bhavet | parvatādiryathā deśaḥ prāgdharmatvāvadhāraṇāt ||
yaścātra kathyate dharmī prameyo 'sya sa eva naḥ | na cānavadhṛte tasmiṃstaddharmatvāvadhāraṇam ||
prāksa cetpakṣadharmatvādgṛhītaḥ kiṃ tataḥ param | paṣadharmādibhirjñātairyena syādanumānitā ||
anvayo na ca śabdasya prameyeṇa nirūpyate | vyāpāreṇa hi sarveṣāmanvitatvaṃ pratīyate ||
yatra dhūmo 'sti tatrāgnerastitvenānvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ | na tvevaṃ yatra śabdo 'sti tatrārtho 'stīti niścayaḥ ||
na tāvattatra deśe 'sau tatkāle vāvagamyate | bhavennityavibhutvāccet, sarvārtheṣu ca tatsamam ||
tena sarvatra dṛṣṭatvādvyatirekasya cāgateḥ | sarvaśabdairaśeṣārthapratipattiḥ prasajyate ||
athaivaṃ deśakālābhyāmasatyatvaprakalpane | vācakapratyayaṃ kaścidbrūyādarthadhiyānvitam ||
naivamapyasti dṛṣṭo hi vināpyarthadhiyā kva cit | vācakapratyayo 'smābhiravyutpannanarān prati ||
dvitīyādiprayoge ca bhavedanvayakalpanā | śatakṛtvaḥ prayukte 'pi na ca dṛṣṭārthadhīḥ kva cit ||
nanu ye jñātasambandhāsteṣāṃ dṛṣṭo 'nvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ | yadyevamanvayātpūrvaṃ sambandhaḥ ko 'pi kalpitaḥ ||
nāṅgamarthadhiyāmeṣā bhavedanvayakalpanā | anvayādhīnajanmatvamanumānasya ca sthitam ||
jñāte pratītisāmarthye tadvaśādeva jāyate | paścādanvaya ityeṣa kāraṇaṃ kathamucyate ||
tasmāttannirapekṣaiva śabdaśaktiḥ pratīyate | na ca dhūmānvayātpūrvaṃ śaktatvamavagamyate ||
vyatireko 'pyavijñātādarthāc chabdadhiyau yadi | so 'pi paścātsthitatvena nārthapratyayasādhanam ||
sambandhaṃ yaṃ tu vakṣyāmastasya nirṇayakāraṇam | syādanvayo 'tirekaśca na tvarthādhigamasya tau ||
tasmādananumānatvaṃ cābde pratyakṣavadbhavet | trairūpyarahitatvena tādṛgviṣayavarjanāt ||
sati cāsya pramāṇatve bhedābhedanirūpanā | yuktā na tu padajñānātpadārtho 'tra pramīyate ||
padaṃ prayujyamānaṃ hi caturddhārthe prayujyate | pratyakṣe ca parokṣe ca jñāte 'jñāte 'pi vā purā ||
tatra yatpūrvavijñāte pratyakṣe ca prayujyate | pramite ca prayuktatvādanuvādo 'dhikādvinā ||
adṛṣṭapūrve tvajñānaṃ sambandhapratyayo 'pi vā | sambandho na ca tasyārthaḥ, yo 'rthaḥ sa tvanyagocaraḥ ||
parokṣe 'nanubhūte ca nābhidheye matirbhavet | parokṣaścānubhūtaśca yastatra smṛtiriṣyate ||
pramite ca pravṛttatvātsmṛternāsti pramāṇatā | paricchedaphalatvāddhi prāmāṇyamupajāyate ||
tādātvikaparicchedaphalatvena pramāṇatā | pratyabhijñānavatkasmātsmṛterapi na kalpyate ||
yāvān pūrvaparicchinnastāvānevāvadhāryate | smṛtyā tadanusāreṇa tadāsattve 'sya naiva dhīḥ ||
padamabhyadhikābhāvātsmārakānna viśiṣyate | padādhikyaṃ bhavetkiñcittatpadasya na gocaraḥ ||
pramāṇamanumānaṃ vā yadyapi syātpadānmitiḥ | vākyārthasyāgamārthatvāddoṣo nāgamavādinām ||
vākyārthe tu padārthebhyaḥ sambandhānubhavādṛte | buddhirutpadyate tena bhinnā 'sāvakṣabuddhivat ||
vākyādhikaraṇe cāsya hetoḥ siddhirbhaviṣyati | sarveṣāṃ ca paroktānāṃ vākyabuddhāvasiddhatā ||
vākyeṣvadṛṣṭeṣvapi sārthakeṣu padārthavinmātratayā pratītim | dṛṣṭvānumānavyatirekabhītāḥ kliṣṭāḥ padābhedavicāraṇāyām ||

§ 5,7 upamānapariccheda ump

kīdṛggavaya ityevaṃ pṛṣṭo nāgarikairyadi | bravītyāraṇyako vākyaṃ yathā gaurgavayastathā ||
etasminnupamānatvaṃ prasiddhaṃ śabare punaḥ | tasyāgamābahirbhāvādanyathaivopavarṇitam ||
puruṣapratyayenaiva tatrārthaḥ sampratīyate | tadīyavacanatvena tasmādāgama eva saḥ ||
sadṛśādupajāyeta yā matiḥ sadṛśāntare | dhyānādismṛtitulyatvātsā pramāṇaṃ kathaṃ bhavet ||
deśakālādibhedena yathānyatra viśiṣyate | prameyaṃ naivamastyatra nagarasthānusārataḥ ||
śrutātideśavākyānāmāraṇye gavaye matiḥ | yā sopamānaṃ keṣāñcidgosādṛśyānurañjitā ||
pratyakṣo gavayastāvatsādṛśyasmṛtiratra tu | nanu sādṛśyayukte 'rthe na smṛtirnendriyādgatiḥ ||
pūrvavākyārthavijñānānnādhikyaṃ gavaye yadi | smaraṇādaviśiṣṭatvātsaṅgaterna pramāṇatā ||
atha tvadhikatā kā citpratyakṣādivaśādbhavet | yāvaddhīndriyasambandhastatpratyakṣamiti sthitam ||
syaryamāṇasya cāṃśasya vivedenāpramāṇatā | śrutātideśavākyatvaṃ na cātīvopayujyate ||
ye 'pi hyaśrutatadvākyāsteṣāmapi bhavatyayam | pratyakṣadṛṣṭagotvānāṃ vane gavayadarśinām ||
atha saṃjñānusandhānaṃ teṣāṃ nāstīti varṇyate | na nāma vastu tattāvatsarvathā taiḥ pratīyate ||
na ca śabdārthasambandhaḥ prameyo 'tra tadeṣyate | sādṛśyāvadhṛte vākye vākyādavagato hyasau ||
na cāsya pratyabhijñānaṃ punarutpadyate vane | śaktyoratīndriyatvena smṛtireva hi seṣyate ||
śabdānuviddhabodhe 'pi pratyakṣamupapāditam | tasmātsādṛśyayuktārthaḥ prameyo 'pūrva ucyatām ||
vyavasāyātmakatvaṃ tu pratyakṣasya yadeṣyate | jātyādivattadā tena sādṛśyaṃ kiṃ na mīyate ||
pratyakṣābhāsametattu nirvikalpakavādinām | prameyavastvabhāvācca nābhipretā pramāṇatā ||
sādṛśyasyāpi vastutvaṃ na śakyamapabādhitum | bhūyo 'vayavasāmānyayogo jātyantarasya tat ||
sadṛśāvayavatvaṃ tu yatra padmadalākṣivat | tatsvāvayavasāmānyabhūmnā teṣā bhaviṣyati ||
evaṃ jātiguṇadravyakriyāśaktisvadharmataḥ | ekaikadvitrisāmastyabhedādetasya citratā ||
na dharmā eva sādṛśyaṃ bhūyastā vā tadāśrayā | bhūyastvavaddhi jātyādi sadṛśatvena dṛśyate ||
yamayoḥ kathametacced, dṛṣṭatvātkimihocyate | kva ciddhi bhūyasāmetatkva cidalpīyasāmapi ||
naitāvatā viśeṣeṇa vastutvaṃ tasya hīyate | sāmānyānyapi caitāni nāśīnyāśrayanāśataḥ ||
anantāśrayayogācca na nāśo 'nyatra vidyate | tena sarvaṃ na sāmānyaṃ nityatvena prakalpyate ||
sāmānyānāṃ na vā nāśaḥ kva cidabhyupagamyate | sarvasya hyāśrayaḥ kaścidasti deśāntarādiṣu ||
teṣāṃ bhūyastayā cedaṃ sādṛśyamatiricyate | tāni vyastāni santyevaṃ pratyakṣe 'pi kva citkva cit ||
sadṛśāvayavatvaṃ tu yatra nāma pratīyate | tadapyavayavānāṃ syātsamānavayavāntaraiḥ ||
evaṃ tāvadyato nāsti parābhedaprakalpanā | tataḥ paraṃ tu sāmānyaṃ bhavetsādṛśyavarjitam ||
pradhānānāṃ tu sāmānyaṃ yatraikaṃ sampratīyate | sa eveti bhavettatra tadbhede sadṛśatvadhīḥ ||
citrādau yatra sādṛśyaṃ sāmānyaṃ tatra kiṃ bhavet | tatrāpi pṛthivīvarṇaviśeṣādisamānatā ||
rūpagandharasānāṃ ca kasya cittulyatā kva cit | nāvaśyaṃ sarvasāmānyātsādṛśyamupajāyate ||
pṛthivyādiṣu caiteṣāṃ satāmeva svabhāvataḥ | pariṇāmādibhirvyaktiryathādṛṣṭyavadhāryate ||
na hi śaktyātmanā kiñcidasajjanma prapadyate | dharmāṇāṃ na ca nānātvam, asti cāvāntarasthitiḥ ||
vastutve sati cāsyaivaṃ sambandhasya ca cakṣuṣā | dvayorekatra vā dṛṣṭeḥ pratyakṣatvaṃ na vāryate ||
sāmānyavacca sādṛśyamekaikatra samāpyate | pratiyoginyadṛṣṭe 'pi tasmāttadupapadyate ||
tatra yadyapi gāṃ smṛtvā tadbhānamupajāyate | sannidhergavayasthatvādbhavedindriyagocaraḥ ||
tasmādyatsmaryate tatsyātsādṛśyena viśeṣitam | prameyamupamānasya sādṛśyaṃ vā tadanvatam ||
pratyakṣeṇāvabuddhe 'pi sādṛśye gavi ca smṛteḥ | viśiṣṭasyānyato 'siddherupamānapramāṇatā ||
pratyakṣe 'pi yathā deśe smaryamāṇe ca pāvake | viśiṣṭaviṣayatvena nānumānāpramāṇatā ||
yatra tvasadṛśādeva kalpayitvopajāyate | sādṛśyapratyayastatra tadābhāsatvakalpanā ||
bādhakapratyayāccaiṣā sādṛśyābhāsatā matā | yathā palālakūṭasya sādṛśyaṃ kuñjarādinā ||
samīpastho 'pi jānāti sādṛśyaṃ neti tatra hi | na bādhyate samīpādau yattu sādṛśyameva tat ||
na caitasyānumānatvaṃ pakṣadharmādyasambhavāt | prākprameyasya sādṛśyaṃ na dharmatvena gṛhyate ||
gavaye gṛhyamāṇaṃ ca na gavāmanumāpakam | pratijñārthaikadeśatvādgogatasya na liṅgatā ||
gavayaścāpyasambandhānna gorliṅgatvamṛcchati | sādṛśyaṃ na ca sarveṇa pūrvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tadanvayi ||
ekasminnapi dṛṣṭe 'rthe dvitīyaṃ paśyato vane | sādṛśyena sahaivāsmiṃstadaivotpadyate matiḥ ||
śṛṅgitvāderathocyeta sambandhālliṅgatā gavi | na, teṣāṃ gavayajñānavyāpāraṃ pratyupakṣayāt ||
yadi tebhyaḥ pratītiḥ syānniḥsādṛśyaiva sā bhavet | na gauḥ śṛṅgādisadṛśī sadṛśī gavayena tu ||
sadṛśapratyayaṃ dṛṣṭvā śṛṅgādipratyayātparam | gavayapratyayādeva gojñānamupajāyate ||
sadṛśāvayavatve tu teṣāmevopamā bhavet | na ca śṛṅgādayo yatra tatra gauranumīyate ||
itthaṃ cānumimānasya bhrāntajñānaṃ prasajyate | nagarasthe tu gojñānaṃ smaraṇānnātivartate ||
bhinnānumānādupameyamuktam, sauryādivākyairasahāyi dṛṣṭam | sādṛśyato 'gnyādiyutaṃ kathaṃ nu, pratyāyayedityupayujyate naḥ ||
pratinidhirapi caivaṃ vrīhisādṛśyayogādbhavati tadapacāre yatra nīvārajātau | tadapi phalamabhīṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇasyopamāyāḥ pratikṛtirapi gauṇairbodhyate yatra cānyaiḥ ||
yadi susadṛśamanyallabhyate tatra mithyā bhavati visadṛśatvānmandasādṛśyayuktam | matirapi ca tathaiva drāgivotpadyate 'sminnitaraviṣayabodhe 'satyapītthaṃ ca bādhaḥ ||

§ 5,8 arthāpattipariccheda aap

pramāṇaṣaṭkavijñāto yatrārtho nānyathā bhavet | adṛṣṭaṃ kalpayedanyaṃ sārthāpattirudāhṛtā ||
dṛṣṭaḥ pañcabhirapyasmādbhedenoktā śrutodbhavā | pramāṇagrāhiṇītvena yasmātpūrvavilakṣaṇā ||
tatra pratyakṣato jñānāddāhāddahanaśaktatā | vahneranumitātsūrye yānāttacchaktiyogyatā ||
śrutārthāpattiratraiva parastādabhidhāsyate | gavayopamitā yā gaustajjñānagrāhyatā matā ||
abhidhānaprasiddhyarthamarthāpattyāvabodhitāt | śabde bodhakasāmarthyāttannityatvaprakalpanam ||
abhidhā nānyathā sidhyediti vācakaśaktatām | arthāpattyāvagamyaivaṃ tadananyagateḥ punaḥ ||
arthāpattyantareṇaiva śabdanityatvaniścayaḥ | darśanasya parārthatvādityasminnabhidhāsyate ||
pramāṇābhāvanirṇītacaitrābhāvaviśeṣitāt | gehāccaitrabahirbhāvasiddhiryā tviha darśitā ||
tāmabhāvotthitāmanyāmarthāpattimudāharet | pakṣadoṣeṣu cānyāsāmudāharaṇavistaraḥ ||
abhāvāvagatāccaitrādbahirbhāvasya sūcanam | pakṣadharmādyanaṅgatvādbhinnaivāpyanumānataḥ ||
bahirdeśaviśiṣṭe 'rthe deśe vā tadviśeṣite | prameye yo gṛhābhāvaḥ pakṣadharmastvasau katham ||
tadabhāvaviśiṣṭaṃ tu gṛhaṃ dharmo na kasyacit | gṛhābhāvaviśiṣṭastu tadāsau na pratīyate ||
gamyate tu gṛhaṃ tatra na ca caitraḥ pratīyate | na cātrādarśanaṃ heturyathābhāve 'bhidhāsyate ||
tena veśmanyadṛṣṭatvāditi heturna kalpyate | adarśanādabhāve ca prameyasyāvadhārite ||
bahirbhāvamatirnāsau tenādarśanahetukā | caitrābhāvasya hetutvaṃ gehe 'bhāvaśca saṃsthitaḥ ||
pūrvaṃ na cāgṛhītasya dharmiṇaḥ syātprameyatā | na cātra bāhyadeśo vā caitro vā gṛhyate purā ||
nadīpūreṇa yā vṛṣṭirupariṣṭātpratīyate | deśe kathamadṛṣṭe tu pakṣadharmatvasambhavaḥ ||
vṛṣṭimatparadeśatvaṃ nadīpuravato 'tra tu | deśasya pratipadyante yadvārthāpattireva sā ||
jīvataśca gṛhābhāvaḥ pakṣadharmo 'tra kalpyate | tatsaṃvittirbahirbhāvaṃ na cābuddhvopajāyate ||
agnimattānapekṣā tu dhūmavattā pratīyate | na tadgrahaṇavelāyāmagnyadhīnaṃ hi kiñcana ||
gehābhāvastu yaḥ śuddho vidyamānatvavarjitaḥ | sa mṛteṣvapi dṛṣṭatvādbahirvṛtterna sādhakaḥ ||
vidyamānatvasaṃsṛṣṭagṛhābhāvadhiyānayā | gehādutkālitaścaitro vidyate bahireva hi ||
gehābhāvatvamātraṃ tu yatsvatantraṃ pratīyate | na tāvatā bahirbhāvaścaitrasyaivāvadhāryate ||
siddhe sadbhāvavijñāne gehābhāvadhiyātra tu | gehādutkālitā sattā bahirevāvatiṣṭhate ||
tenāsya nirapekṣasya vyabhicāro mṛtādinā | yasya tvavyabhicāritvaṃ na tato 'nyatpratīyate ||
tasmātpratyakṣato gehe caitrābhāve hyabhāvataḥ | jñāte yatsattvavijñānaṃ tadevedaṃ bahiḥ sthitam ||
pakṣadharmātmalābhāya bahirbhāvaḥ praveśitaḥ | tadviśiṣṭo 'numeyaḥ syātpakṣadharmānvayādibhiḥ ||
pakṣadharmādivijñānaṃ bahiḥ sambodhato yadi | taiśca tadbodhato 'vaśyamanyonyāśrayatā bhavet ||
anyathānupapattau tu prameyānupraveśitā | tādrūpyeṇaiva vijñānānna doṣaḥ pratibhāti naḥ ||
avinābhāvitā cātra tadaiva parikalpyate | na prāgavadhṛtetyevaṃ satyapyeṣā na kāraṇam ||
gṛhābhāvabahirbhāvau na ca dṛṣṭau niyogataḥ | sāhitye 'pi pramāṇaṃ ca tayoranyanna vidyate ||
anyathānupapattyaiva hyekenānyatpratīyate | tathā na kalpyate taccetsāhityaṃ na pratīyate ||
tena sambandhavelāyāṃ sambandhyanyataro dhruvam | arthāpattyāvagantavyaḥ paścādastyanumānatā ||
gṛhadvāri sthito yastu bahirbhāvaṃ prakalpayet | yadaikasminnayaṃ deśe na tadānyatra vidyate ||
tadāpyavidyamānatvaṃ na sarvatra pratīyate | na caikadeśe nāstitvādvyāptirhetorbhaviṣyati ||
nanvatrāvidyamānatvaṃ gamyate 'nupalabdhitaḥ | sā cāprayatnasādhyatvādekasthasyaiva sidhyati ||
naitayānupalabdhyātra vastvabhāvaḥ pratīyate | taddeśāgamanātsā hi dūrastheṣvasti satsvapi ||
gatvā gatvā tu tāndeśānyadyartho nopalabhyate | tato 'nyakāraṇābhāvādasannityavagamyate ||
nanu cāgnyādyabhāve 'pi dhūmādivyatirekiṇām | taddeśāgamanātspaṣṭo vyatireko na sidhyati ||
yasya vastvantarābhāvaḥ prameyastasya duṣyati | mama tvadṛṣṭamātreṇa gamakaḥ sahacāriṇaḥ ||
nanvevamitaratrāpi sambandho 'nupalabdhitaḥ | caitrābhāvasya bhāvena dṛṣṭatvādupapadyate ||
sāhitye mitadeśatvātprasiddhe cāgnidhūmayoḥ | vyatirekasya cādṛṣṭergamakatvaṃ prakalpyate ||
iha sāhityamevedamekasya sahabhāvinaḥ | anantadeśavarttitvānna tāvadupapadyate ||
nanu deśāntaraṃ śūnyaṃ caitreṇaivaṃ pratīyate | taddeśavyatiriktatvātsamīpasthitadeśavat ||
viruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ tadvadeva hi gamyate | samīpadeśabhinnatvāt caitrādhiṣṭhitadeśavat ||
puruṣasya tu kārtsnyena yadekatropalambhanam | tasyānyathā na siddhiḥ syādityanyeṣvasya nāstitā ||
tenārthāpattipūrvatvamatra yatra ca kāraṇe | kāryādarśanataḥ śakterastitvaṃ sampratīyate ||
kāryasya nanu liṅgatvaṃ na sambandhānapekṣaṇāt | dṛṣṭvā sambandhitāṃ caiṣā śaktirgamyeta nānyathā ||
taddarśane tadānīṃ ca pratyakṣāderasambhavāt | arthāpatteḥ pramāṇatvaṃ trailakṣaṇyādvinā bhavet ||
anumānādabhinnatvānnoktau jayaparājayau | vadhyaghātakabhāvena yau sarpanakulādiṣu ||
pīno divā na bhuṅkte cetyevamādivacaḥ śrutau | rātribhojanavijñānaṃ śrutārthāpattirucyate ||
tāmarthagocarāṃ kecidapare śabdagocarām | kalpayantyāgamāccaināmabhinnāṃ pratijānate ||
prāyaśaścānayā vede vyavahāro vyavasthitaḥ | so 'vaidikaḥ prasajyeta yadyeṣā bhidyate tataḥ ||
vacanasya śrutasyaiva so 'pyarthaḥ kaiścidāśritaḥ | tadarthopaplutasyānyairiṣṭo vākyāntarasya tu ||
na tāvac chrūyamāṇasya vacaso 'rtho 'yamiṣyate | na hyanekārthatā yuktā vākye vācakatā tathā ||
padārthānvayarūpeṇa vākyārtho hi pratīyate | na rātryādipadārthaśca divāvākyena gamyate ||
na divādipadārthānāṃ saṃsargo rātribhojanam | na bhedo yena tadvākyaṃ tasya syātpratipādakam ||
anyārthavyāpṛtatvācca na dvitīyārthakalpanā | tasmādvākyāntareṇāyaṃ buddhisthena pratīyate ||
tasya cāgamikatve 'pi yattadvākyaṃ pratīyate | pramāṇaṃ tasya vaktavyaṃ pratyakṣādiṣu yadbhavet ||
na hyanuccārite vākye pratyakṣaṃ tāvadiṣyate | nānumānaṃ na cedaṃ hi dṛṣṭaṃ tena saha kvacit ||
yadi tvanupalabdhe 'pi sambandhe liṅgateṣyate | taduccāraṇamātreṇa sarvavākyamatirbhavet ||
na cārthāpattigamyāni sarvaiḥ sarvavacāṃsi hi | sambaddhānyupalabdhāni yena teṣvanumā bhavet ||
na ca sattānumānena viśeṣo vānumīyate | iha vākyaviśeṣasya sattaiva tvavagamyate ||
pūrvasiddhaḥ svatantro 'rthaḥ svatantreṇa viśeṣitaḥ | dharmādharmaviśiṣṭo 'tra nānumeyaḥ pratīyate ||
atha śrutasya vākyasya mīyate tadviśiṣṭatā | tataḥ pakṣo 'bhyupetaḥ syādaprasiddhaviśeṣaṇaḥ ||
kiñca liṅgāntarābhāvādetasya yadi liṅgatā | pratijñārthaikadeśatvaṃ padavatte prasajyate ||
tadvadeva nirākāryā vacaso dharmadharmitā | nāgṛhīte hi taddharmo gṛhīte nānumeyatā ||
kriyākārakasambandhādṛte nāsti tu dharmatā | avācakatayā caitanna dharmo viṣayātmanā ||
pratītervācakatvaṃ cetprasaktānekaśaktitā | anumāviṣayotthaṃ tu dharmatvaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet ||
padārthairapi tadvākyaṃ nāsambandhātpratīyate | sāmānyānyanyathāsiddherviśeṣaṃ gamayanti hi ||
na tu vākyāntareṇaiṣāṃ vinā kiñcinna sidhyati | na cāpyanyaḥ prakāro 'sti tena vākyena saṅgatau ||
athaitadvāci kalpyeta vākyamanyattathaiva ca | prasaṅgāttatra dūre 'pi nāsambandhātpramucyate ||
tataśca prathamādeva varaṃ jñātumasaṅgatāt | anvayavyatirekau ca pratiṣedhyau pade yathā ||
śrutavākyena sādṛśyaṃ nāśrutasyāsti kiñcana | tasmādanupamānatvamarthasyāpyanayā diśā ||
upamānatvaliṅgatve vākyaṃ prati nivārite | arthe 'pi caivameva syāt, tasmātpūrveṣvasambhavaḥ ||
ataḥ śrutasya vākyasya yadarthapratipādanam | tadātmalābha eva syādvinā netyetadiṣyate ||
etadarthādvinā nāyamityarthaḥ kiṃ na kalpyate | vākyārthavacca kiṃ nāyamāgamārthaḥ pratīyate ||
savikalpakavijñānaiḥ śabdaḥ pūrvaṃ pratīyate | labdhaprayojane vākye paraṃ nāgamikaṃ ca naḥ ||
nanu cāsati sambandhe sati vānavadhārite | gamyajñānamidaṃ vākyaṃ prasajyetāpramāṇakam ||
sambandhasya pramāṇatvaṃ sthitaṃ kiñceśvarājñayā | pratyakṣasya pramāṇatvaṃ kathaṃ vā saṅgatervinā ||
astīndriyārthasambandhastatra cennānapekṣaṇāt | na hi pratyakṣavelāyāṃ sarveṇāsau nirūpyate ||
yenāpi tu nirūpyeta paścādanubhavādasau | na syādeva pramāṇāṅgamasatā tulya eva saḥ ||
aprāpyakāriṇī yeṣāṃ cakṣuḥśrotre ca te yathā | tajjñānasya pramāṇatvamicchantyevaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
tasmādasattve sattve vā sambandhasya yadeva naḥ | jāyetābhaṅguraṃ jñānaṃ tasyaiva syātpramāṇatā ||
na cāpyasyāḥ pramāṇatve kaścidvipratipadyate | bhedābhede visaṃvādaḥ kṛtastatra ca nirṇayaḥ ||
kṛte yatra ca sambandhādbuddhireva na jāyate | tatra ki kriyatāṃ so 'pi prāmāṇye naiva kāraṇam ||
smṛtyā śrutiryā parikalpyate 'sminliṅgādibhiryā viniyojikā ca | phalādibhiryatparipūraṇaṃ ca sambandhadṛktatra na kācidasti ||
tatsarvamityādyasamañjasaṃ syānna cediyaṃ syādanumānato 'nyā | evaṃsvabhāvāpyanumānaśabdaṃ labheta cedasti yathepsitaṃ naḥ ||

§ 5,9 abhāvapariccheda abh

pramāṇapañcakaṃ yatra vasturūpe na jāyate | vastusattāvabodhārthaṃ tatrābhāvapramāṇatā ||
vastvasaṅkarasiddhiśca tatprāmāṇyasamāśrayā | kṣīre dadhyādi yannāsti prāgabhāvaḥ sa ucyate ||
nāstitā payaso dadhni pradhvaṃsābhāva iṣyate | gavi yo 'śvādyabhāvastu so 'nyonyābhāva ucyate ||
śiraso 'vayavā nimnā vṛddhikāṭhinyavarjitāḥ | śaśaśṛṅgādirūpeṇa so 'tyantābhāva ucyate ||
kṣīre dadhi bhavedevaṃ dadhni kṣīraṃ ghaṭe paṭaḥ | śaśe śṛṅgaṃ pṛthivyādau caitanyaṃ mūrtirātmani ||
apsu gandho rasaścāgnau vāyau rūpeṇa tau saha | vyomni saṃsparśitā te ca na cedasya pramāṇatā ||
na ca syādvyavahāro 'yaṃ kāraṇādivibhāgataḥ | prāgabhāvādibhedena nābhāvo bhidyate yadi ||
na cāvastuna ete syurbhedāstenāsya vastutā | kāryādīnāmabhāvaḥ ko yo 'bhāvaḥ kāraṇāditaḥ ||
yadvānuvṛttivyāvṛttibuddhigrāhyo yatastvayam | tasmādgavādivadvastu, prameyatvācca gamyate ||
na caupacārikatvaṃ vā bhrāntirvāpi yadṛcchayā | bhavatyato na sāmānyaviśeṣātmakatā mṛṣā ||
pratyakṣāderanutpattiḥ pramāṇābhāva ucyate | sātmanaḥ pariṇāmo vā vijñānaṃ vākyavastuni ||
svarūpapararūpābhyāṃ nityaṃ sadasadātmake | vastuni jñāyate kaiścidrūpaṃ kiñcitkadā cana ||
yasya yatra yadodbhūtirjighṛkṣā vopajāyate | cetyate 'nubhavastasya tena ca vyapadiśyate ||
tasyopakārakatvena varttate 'śastadetaraḥ | ubhayorapi saṃvittāvubhayānugamo 'sti hi ||
ayameveti yo hyeṣa bhāve bhavati nirṇayaḥ | naiṣa vastvantarābhāvasaṃvittyanugamādṛte ||
nāstītyapi ca saṃvittirna vastvanugamādṛte | jñānaṃ na jāyate kiñcidupaṣṭambhanavarjitam ||
pratyakṣādyavatārastu bhāvāṃśo gṛhyate yadā | vyāpārastadanutpatterabhāvāṃśe jighṛkṣite ||
na tāvadindriyaireṣā nāstītyutpadyate matiḥ | bhāvāṃśenaiva saṃyogo yogyatvādindriyasya hi ||
nanu bhāvādabhinnatvātsamprayogo 'sti tena ca | na hyatyantamabhedo 'sti rūpādivadihāpi naḥ ||
dharmayorbheda iṣṭo hi dharmyabhede 'pi naḥ sthite | udbhavābhibhavātmatvādgrahaṇaṃ cāvatiṣṭhate ||
idameva nimittaṃ ca vivekasya pratīyate | bhāvābhāvadhiyorakṣaiḥ sambandho 'kṣānapekṣaṇam ||
rūpāderapi bhedaṃ ca ke cidgrāhakabhedataḥ | varṇayanti yathaikasya puṃsaḥ putrādirūpatām ||
buddhimātrakṛto bhedo rūpādau nityameva hi | na ca deśādyabhinnānāṃ samudāyāvakalpanā ||
sadguṇadravyarūpeṇa rūpāderekateṣyate | svarūpāpekṣayā caiṣāṃ parasparavibhinnatā ||
yadi tadvadapekṣātra na syādbhedo 'tra naiva hi | sadasadrūpatā buddherbhavedanyataratra naḥ ||
tatsambandhe sadityevaṃ tadrūpatvaṃ pratīyate | nāstyatredamitīdaṃ tu tadasaṃyogahetukam ||
gṛhītvā vastusadbhāvaṃ smṛtvā ca pratiyoginam | mānasaṃ nāstitājñānaṃ jāyate 'kṣānapekṣaṇāt ||
svarūpamātraṃ dṛṣṭvāpi paścātkiñcitsmarannapi | tatrānyanāstitāṃ pṛṣṭastadaiva pratipadyate ||
na cāpyatrānumānatvaṃ liṅgābhāvātpratīyate | bhāvāṃśo nanu liṅgaṃ syāt, tadānīṃ nājighṛkṣaṇāt ||
abhāvāvagaterjanma bhāvāṃśe hyajighṛkṣite | tasmin pratīyamāne tu nābhāve jāyate matiḥ ||
na caiṣa prakṣadharmatvaṃ padavatpratipadyate | saha sarvairabhāvaiśca bhāvo naikāntato gataḥ ||
kva cidbhāve 'pi sadbhāvo jñāto yasya kadā cana | tasyābhāvo 'pi tatraiva kadā cidavagamyate ||
yatrāpyadṛṣṭapūrvatvaṃ yadabhāvasya tatra ca | tadabhāvamatirdṛṣṭā sambandhe 'kṣānapekṣayā ||
kasya cidyadi bhāvasya syādabhāvena kena cit | sambandhadarśanam, tatra sarvamānaṃ prasajyate ||
gṛhīte 'pi ca bhāvāṃśe naivābhāve 'nyavastunaḥ | sarvatra matirityevaṃ vyabhicārādaliṅgatā ||
sambandhe gṛhyamāṇe ca sambandhigrahaṇaṃ dhruvam | tatrābhāvamatiḥ kena pramāṇenopajāyate ||
tadānīṃ na hi liṅgena sambandhigrahaṇaṃ bhavet | tatrāvaśyamabhāvasya pramāṇāntarato gatiḥ ||
pratyakṣāderanutpattirna tu liṅgaṃ bhaviṣyati | na viśeṣaṇasambandhastasyāḥ sāmānyato bhavet ||
na cāpyabhāvasāmānye pramāṇamupajāyate | vyabhicārādviśeṣāstu pratīyeran kathaṃ tayā ||
na cānavagataṃ liṅgaṃ gṛhyate cedasāvapi | abhāvatvādabhāvena gṛhyetānyena hetunā ||
sa cānyena grahītavyo nāgṛhīte hi liṅgatā | tadgṛhītirhi liṅgena syādanyenetyanantatā ||
liṅgābhāve tathaiva syādanavastheyamityataḥ | kvāpyasya syātpramāṇatvaṃ liṅgatvena vinā dhruvam ||
nāstīti dhīḥ phalaṃ caiṣā pratyakṣāderajanmanaḥ | tasyaiva ca pramāṇatvamānantaryātpratīyate ||
trilakṣaṇena yā buddhirjanyate sānumeṣyate | na cānutpattirūpasya kāraṇāpekṣitā kva cit ||
mānaṃ kathamabhāvaścet, prameyaṃ cāsya kīdṛśam | meyo yadvadabhāvo hi mānamapyevamiṣyatām ||
bhāvātmake tathā meye nābhāvasya pramāṇatā | tathābhāvaprameye 'pi na bhāvasya pramāṇatā ||
bhāvātmakasya mānatvaṃ na ca rājājñayā sthitam | paricchedaphalatvāddhi prāmāṇyaṃ syāddvayorapi ||
yadi cāsya pramāṇatvamabhāvatvena neṣyate | vastunaḥ kāraṇatvaṃ hi dṛṣṭamityabhimānitā ||
na liṅgatvaprameyatve bhavetāṃ tadvadeva hi | tathā sati ca pūrvokto vyavahāro na sidhyati ||
pramāṇānāmanutpatternābhāvasyāpi dharmatā | yatrābhāvo 'sti tenāsyāḥ sambandho naiva vidyate ||
yo na sannihitastatra tasya dharmo bhavediyam | na ca tasya prameyatvaṃ dharmadharmitvavarjanāt ||
abhāvena tu sambandho bhavettadviṣayatvataḥ | tajjānādviṣayatvaṃ ca jñāne meyaṃ na vidyate ||
saṃyogasamavāyādisambandho naiva vidyate | nāgṛhīte hi dharmatvaṃ gṛhīte siddhasādhanam ||
abhāvaśabdavācyatvātpratyakṣādeśca bhidyate | pramāṇānāmabhāvo hi prameyāṇāmabhāvavat ||
abhāvo vā pramāṇena svānurūpeṇa mīyate | prameyatvādyathā bhāvastasmādbhāvātmakātpṛthak ||
karmāṇi sarvāṇi phalaiḥ samastaiḥ sarvairyathāvacca yadaṅgakāṇḍaiḥ | na saṅgatānīha parasparaṃ ca nāṅgaṃ tadetatprabhavaṃ kratūnām ||
yuktyāgamābhyāmiti tarkito 'yaṃ pramāṇaṣaṭkaṃ pravibhajya bhāṣye | tato 'dhikaṃ yaddvayamiṣṭamanyairbhedo na tasyetyapi siddhametat ||
iha bhavati śatādau sambhavādyāsahasrānmatiraviyutabhāvātsānumānādabhinnā | jagati bahu na tathyaṃ nityamaitihyamuktaṃ bhavati tu yadi satyaṃ nāgamādbhidyate tat ||

§ 5,10 citrākṣepavāda cav

paralokaphalāḥ pūrvamākṣiptāścodanāḥ paraiḥ | idānīmaihikākṣepaḥ, sūtrakāreṇa codyate ||
citrāpaśuphalatvādiviṣayāścodaṇā mṛṣā | pratyakṣādyadhikāre 'pi tairarthāsaṅgatiryataḥ ||
yadīdṛktanmṛṣā dṛṣṭaṃ vipralipsoryathā vacaḥ | nadītīre phalānīti tatrādṛśyāni tāni cet ||
na vā paśuphalā citrā svakāle tadadānaḥ | snānabhujyādivatte 'pi tatsādhyā na bhavanti vā ||
tadutpattāvasadbhāvātsvarge tṛptisukhādivat | vaidharmyeṇobhayatrāpi bhavetāṃ sukhamardane ||
ānantaryamayuktaṃ cet, na sāmarthyāvabodhanāt | śabdaikadeśabhūtena tena tatpratipāditam ||
kālāntarānupādānātkarmasvābhāvyato 'pi ca | codyamānasya citrāderānantaryaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||
atra tāvadasaṃvādo virodhaścottarasya tu | svargayānaviruddho hi bhasmībhāvo 'tra dṛśyate ||
yajñāyudhivaco mithyā pratyakṣeṇa virodhataḥ | sādharmyeṇa śilāvākyaṃ vaidharmyeṇāptabhāṣitam ||
śarīrādyadi cānyaḥ syānnāsau yajñāyudhī bhavet | na cāsya yajamānatvaṃ sadbhāvo 'pi ca durlabhaḥ ||
yadi syādvidhiśabdo 'tra naivādarśanato bhavet | viśeṣo 'syeti bhedena nopāttaṃ syādidaṃ tataḥ ||
vidhiśabde bhaviṣyattvaṃ phalasya parikalpya hi | virodhaparihāraḥ syādvartamāne 'pi nāstyasau ||
phalaṃ ca na bhavedevaṃ bhasmībhāvādvidhāvapi | tatsāmarthyena yā cānyā kalpanā tāṃ niṣedhati ||
prāyaścaivamprakāratvamarthavādeṣu dṛśyate | mantreṣu ceti te sarve pakṣīkāryāḥ prayatnataḥ ||
evaṃ satyagnihotrādivākyeṣvapi mṛṣārthatā | vedavākyaikadeśatvāccitrādivacaneṣvapi ||

§ 5,11 sambandhākṣepavāda sav

svapakṣasādhanaṃ tāvat na mṛṣā vaidikaṃ vacaḥ | svārthe vaktranapekṣatvātpadārthapadabuddhivat ||
tatkṛtaḥ pratyayaḥ samyaṅ nityavākyodbhavatvataḥ | vākyabuddhivadeva atra pūrvoktāścāpi hetavaḥ ||
nityān śabdārthasambandhānāśrityoktena hetunā | svataḥ prāmāṇyasiddhyarthamaprāmāṇye nirākṛte ||
asambandhodbhavatvena paro mithyātvamabravīt | sambandho 'sti ca nityaścetyuktamautpattikādinā ||
mithyā tvasya nirāsārthaṃ tatparairneṣyate dvayam | naiva cāstyatra sambandhaḥ kṛtako veti vakṣyate ||
