asambhavena śeṣāṇāṃ saṃśleṣaḥ pariśiṣyate | asminneva ca sambandhe pratītirlaukiko dhruvā ||
tanniṣedhamataḥ prāha na śabdo 'rthena saṅgataḥ | taddeśānantarādṛṣṭervindhyo himavatā yathā ||
evamartho dvayaṃ vāpi sādhanīyamasaṅgatam | kṣuretyādi ca siddhyarthahetoruktamathāparaḥ ||
śaktirūpaṃ gṛhītvāha saṃśleṣo yadi vāryate | sambandhasiddhasādhyatvamatha sambandhamātrakam ||
pitāputrādisambandhairanekāntaḥ prasajyate | ekabhūmyādisambandhāddṛṣṭānte sādhyahīnatā ||
vācyavācakasambandhaniṣedhe lokabādhanam | virodhaśca svavākyena na hi sambandhavarjitaiḥ ||
pratijñārthaṃ padaiḥ śākyaḥ pratīpādayituṃ paraḥ | abhidhānakriyāyāṃ hi karmatvaṃ vācyasaṃśritam ||
śabdānāṃ karaṇatvaṃ vā kartṛtvaṃ vā nirūpitam | pratipattāvupādānātsāhitye ca vivakṣite ||
niyamyate yadekasyāṃ sambandhaḥ so 'rthaśabdayoḥ | tatra yadyapyasambandhaḥ kārakāṇāṃ parasparam ||
tathāpi yatkriyā tasyāmupakāryopakāritā | sa kriyāsaṅgateḥ paścātsambandhaḥ kīrtyate tayoḥ ||
na cātrāpyavinābhāva upayogīti sādhitam | saṃjñeti gamakatvaṃ cenna tadaṅgamiyaṃ bhavet ||
gamayantīṃ śrutiṃ dṛṣṭvā kalpyate vyavahārataḥ | na caiṣā gamayatyarthaṃ sambandhe 'navadhārite ||
tasmādgamakatā paścāddhūmāderiva jāyate | sānaṅgaṃ tadvadeva syādneyaṃ dhūmādibhiḥ samā ||
nirūpite 'vinābhāve tatra tatkāritā hyasau | gamakatvena pūrvaṃ ca tatra notpadyate matiḥ ||
iha vācakatāyāḥ prāṅ nāvinābhāvitāmatiḥ | yadeva ceha sambandhaṃ vṛddhebhyaḥ pratipadyate ||
tadaiva gamako 'syāyamiti nānyasvarūpataḥ | kathayanti kva cittāvadboddhavyo 'smādayaṃ tviti ||
kva cidvācaka ityevaṃ vācyo 'yamiti cocyate | kva ciduccaritācchabdāddṛṣṭvārthaviṣayāṃ kriyām ||
keṣāñcittatra boddhṛtvamanumānātpratīyate | etenāsmādyataḥ śabdādartho 'yamavadhāritaḥ ||
tena nūnamimau siddhau vācyavācakaśaktikau | itthaṃ vācakatā siddhā saṅkīrṇāpi tataḥ param ||
anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ niṣkṛṣṭe 'rthe niyamyate | bahujātiguṇadravyakarmabhedāvalamvinaḥ ||
pratyayātsahasā jātā śrautalākṣaṇikātmakāt | na lokaḥ kāranābhāvānnirdhārayitumicchati ||
balābalādisiddhyarthaṃ vākyajñāstu viviñcate | kakṣāntaritasāmānyaviśeṣeṣu hi durbalaḥ ||
sāmānyavacanaḥ śabdo jāyate lakṣaṇābalāt | tenāvaśyaṃ vivektavyaṃ jāyate lakṣaṇābalāt ||
kiyadvā nityasambandhādabhidheyena lakṣyate | tatra prayogabāhulyāttadviśeṣeṣvasatsvapi ||
prayogātparasāmānye sati vācyaprayogataḥ | sāsnādyekārthasambandhigotvamātrasya vācakaḥ ||
gośabda iti vijñānamanvayavyatirekajam | tasmādgamakataivādau abhidhāyakatā punaḥ ||
tannimitteti sambandhaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñitvalakṣaṇaḥ | sambandhaniyamo 'yaṃ tu yā 'vinābhāvitocyate ||
sambandhagrahaṇātpūrva yasmānna gamayatyataḥ | gavādernābhidhāśaktirdevadattapade yathā ||
yathaiva gamakaḥ śabdo vyavahārātpratīyate | tathaiva śaktivijñānaṃ tasyopāyo 'vagamyate ||
svarūpagrahaṇaṃ cāsya yathā vyāpriyate phale | tathā sambandhivijñānaṃ nāśaktistatkṛtā bhavet ||
yatsādhakatamatvena kasya citkiñciducyate | tasyānugrāhakāpekṣā na svaśaktivighātinī ||
na hi tatkāraṇaṃ loke vede vā kiñcidīdṛśam | itikartavyatāsādhye yasya nānugrahe 'rthitā ||
pratyātmaniyatatvācca yathaiva karaṇaṃ bhavet | bāhyāntaravibhāgena kva citsyādvā vivakṣayā ||
udvigno hyandhakāreṇa kaścidevaṃ bravītyapi | kiṃ cakṣuṣā mamaitena dṛṣṭaṃ dīpena yanmayā ||
nityavṛttau tu nāndhānāṃ dṛṣṭirdīpaśatairapi | rūpādidarśane yasmāttasmāccakṣuḥ prakāśakam ||
śarīrātmamanoyogādasādhāraṇatābalāt | vijñānāsattibhāvācca cakṣuḥ kāraṇamiṣyate ||
tathaivehāpi sambandhajñānamaṅgaṃ prasiddhitaḥ | gauravātkaraṇatvena mataṃ cetkena vāryate ||
yathā cakṣuritīdaṃ tu vyabhicāritvamucyate | devadatte 'pi cāvyaktāṃ śaktimicchanti yuktitaḥ ||
prakāśe 'vasthite bāhye nāndho rūpaṃ pratīyate | phalānantaryataścāpi cakṣuḥ karaṇamiṣyate ||
puruṣādhīnavijñānastebhyaḥ prāganirūpitaḥ | yaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhaḥ sa ceṣṭaśceddhruvaṃ kṛtaḥ ||
bhinnadeśādyadhiṣṭhānādyathā rajjughaṭādiṣu | samaṃ nāstyanayoḥ kiñcittenāsaṅgatatā svataḥ ||

§ 5,12 sphoṭavāda sph

ādhārātmani vijñāte sukhamādheyabodhanam | tasyaiva tāvatprastāvādatha gaurityato 'bravīt ||
pratyakṣe 'pi visaṃvādo yeṣāṃ kaḥ svayamuttaram | tebhyo dadyāditi jñātvā vṛddhānāṃ matamabravīt ||
tatrārthapratyayadvāraṃ kṛtaṃ śabdanirūpaṇam | yairāsatāṃ tu te tāvatpratyakṣeṇa parīkṣyate ||
pratyakṣaṃ nāsamarthaṃ nastena cārthe 'vadhārite | na heturbalavānanyaḥ parīkṣyeta yatastataḥ ||
tasmāc chrotraparicchinno yadyarthaṃ gamayenna vā | sarvathā tasya śabdatvaṃ lokasiddhaṃ na hīyate ||
yadi tvarthagatau śaktirna syādasya tataḥ punaḥ | vastvantaraṃ prakalpyeta vinā śabdaprasiddhitaḥ ||
agnyādīngamayanto 'pi śabdā dhūmādayo na hi | na vā 'pratyāyakatvātsyādekavarṇeṣvaśabdatā ||
na ca prāgarthavijñānāśchotragrāhye na śabdadhīḥ | na cārthajñānataḥ paścādaśrautre 'pi ca śabdatā ||
parasparānapekṣāśca śrotrabuddhyā svarūpataḥ | varṇā evāvagamyante na pūrvāparavastunī ||
alpīyasāpi yatnena śabdamuccaritaṃ matiḥ | yadi vā gṛhṇāti varṇaṃ yadi vā sakalaṃ sphuṭam ||
pṛthaṅ na copalabhyante varṇasyāvayavāḥ kva cit | na ca varṇeṣvanusyūtā dṛśyante tantuvatpaṭe ||
teṣāmanupalabdheśca na jñātā liṅgasaṅgatiḥ | nāgamastatparaścāsti nādṛṣṭe copamā kva cit ||
na cāpyanupapattiḥ syādvarṇasyāvayavairvinā | yathānyāvayavānāṃ hi vināpyavayavāntaraiḥ ||
pratyakṣeṇāvabuddhaśca varṇo 'vayavavarjitaḥ | kiṃ na syād, vyomavaccātra liṅgaṃ tadrahitā matiḥ ||
tadvaccāsyaikabuddhitvāddeśabhede 'pyabhinnatā | nanu bhedamatirna syāt, tavāpyekatvadhīḥ kutaḥ ||
sāmānyeṣu mamaikā dhīstadvyaktiṣu ca bhedadhīḥ | na hīṣṭaṃ bhedamātraṃ hi na syādekatvadhīryataḥ ||
vyaktestāvanna sāmānyaṃ bhinnarūpaṃ pratīyate | varṇeṣvanyatra śabdatvānnānyaccedvarṇa eva saḥ ||
sa eveti matirnāpi sādṛśyam, na ca tatkva cit | vināvayavasāmānyādvarṇeṣvavayavā na ca ||
pratyakṣaviṣayatvācca nānyāpoho 'pi yujyate | vācakaścātra liṅgaṃ vā na tadānīṃ pratīyate ||
gakārādiṣu sāmānyaṃ śabdatvaṃ kalpyate yathā | gotvaṃ ca śābaleyādau tathaitatkiṃ na kalpyate ||
śābaleyagakārādīnniṣpannānvyaktirūpataḥ | sāmānyadhīrna gṛhṇātītyato jātirapīṣyate ||
na tu drutādibhede 'pi niṣpannā sampratīyate | gavyaktyantaravyāvṛttā gavyaktiraparā sphuṭā ||
tenaikatvena varṇasya buddhirekopajāyate | viśeṣabuddhisadbhāvo bhavedvyañjakabhedataḥ ||
yathaiva tava gatvādi gamyamānaṃ drutādibhiḥ | viśeṣairapi nānekamevaṃ varṇo 'pi no bhavet ||
tvayāpi vyañjakavyaktibhedādbhedo 'bhyupeyate | mamāpi vyañjakairnādairbhedabuddhirbhaviṣyati ||
tena yatprārthyate jāte tadvarṇādeva labhyate | vyaktilabhyaṃ ca nādebhya iti gatvādidhīryathā ||
kalpayitvāpi tatpaścādvibhutvaikatvanityatāḥ | pratyekavṛttitā cāsya bhaveyurmahataḥ śramāt ||
dvayasiddhastu varṇātmā nityatvādi yathaiva ca | kalpitasyeṣyate tadvatsiddhasyaivābhyupeyatām ||
pratyekasamavāye ca kleśo naiva bhaviṣyati | vyañjaneṣu ca dhībhedo naiva tādṛkpratīyate ||
dṛśyate 'janurāgeṇa bhedo yo nāma, tatra naḥ | vivedo 'styeva na hyeṣa kevalānāṃ pratīyate ||
akṣvapyevaṃ paropādhirdrutādipratyayo yathā | varṇā ''śritatvādvarṇatvavyañjanapratyayo yathā ||
gakāro 'tyantaniṣkṛṣṭagatvādhāro na gamyate | gānyabuddhyanirūpyatvātparaiḥ kalpitagatvavat ||
avastutvena sādhyatvānniṣedhāddhetusādhyayoḥ | sapakṣe 'nyatarāsiddhirna doṣāyātra jāyate ||
varṇatvāccāpi sādhyo 'yaṃ yakārādivadeva ca | vyatirekasya cādṛṣṭernātra dṛṣṭaṃ nivartakam ||
gotvādivāraṇe tveva dṛṣṭabādhaḥ sphuṭo bhavet | nānyathā hi matistatra syātsāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ ||
na cāpyatraikavastutve bhedo vyañjakabhedataḥ | na piṇḍavyatirekeṇa vyañjako 'tra dhvaniryathā ||
piṇḍavyaṅgyaiva gotvādirjātirnityaṃ pratīyate | tena bhinneṣu piṇḍeṣu jātirekā pratīyate ||
nanu yasya dvayaṃ śrotraṃ tasya buddhidvayaṃ bhavet | bhavato 'tīndriyatvāttu kathaṃ nādairviśeṣadhīḥ ||
nādena saṃskṛtāc chrotrādyadā śabdaḥ pratīyate | tadupaśleṣastat asya bodhaṃ ke citpracakṣate ||
naiva vā grahaṇaṃ teṣāṃ śabde buddhistu tadvaśāt | saṃskārānukṛteḥ so 'pi mahatvādyavabudhyate ||
madhuraṃ tiktarūpeṇa śvetaṃ pītatayā tathā | gṛhṇanti pittadoṣeṇa viṣayaṃ bhrāntacetasaḥ ||
tathā vegena dhāvanto nāvyārūḍhāśca gacchataḥ | parvatādīnvijānanti bhrameṇa bhramataśca tān ||
maṇḍūkavasayāktākṣā vaṃśānuragabuddhibhiḥ | vyaktyalpatvamahattvābhyāṃ sāmānyaṃ ca tadāśrtayam ||
gṛhṇanti yadvadetāni nimittagrahaṇādvinā | vyañjakasthamabudhvaiva vyaṅgye bhrāntirbhaviṣyati ||
varṇāntaratvamevāhuḥ ke ciddīrghaplutādiṣu | na hi drutādivattatra prayoho nāntarīyakaḥ ||
tathā ca sati sāmānyaṃ triṣvatvaṃ kaiścidiṣyate | sāmānyakalpanā tvanyairna yuktetyabhidhīyate ||
atvamityucyamānaṃ hi na dīrghaplutayorbhavet | ātvaṃ na hrasvaplutayostraimātryaṃ na ca pūrvayoḥ ||
sarvasādhāraṇatvena tadvijñātuṃ na śakyate | pratyekaṃ śābaleyādirūpe gotvaṃ yathā sphuṭam ||
avarṇakulaśabdo 'pi sthānasāmyādvanādivat | samudāyārthavācīti na jātivacano bhavet ||
svato hrasvādibhedastu nityavāde virudhyate | sarvadā yasya sadbhāvaḥ sa kathaṃ mātrikaḥ svayam ||
tasmāduccāraṇaṃ tasya mātrākālaṃ pratīyate | dvimātraṃ vā trimātraṃ vā na varṇo mātrikaḥ svayam ||
dīrghādernanvanaṅgatvaṃ vācakādharmato bhavet | itthaṃ pratīyamānāḥ syurvarṇā na pratipādakāḥ ||
yādṛśātpūrvadṛṣṭo 'sāvartho gamyate tādṛśāt | bhrāntyā kathaṃ pratītiścet, nāsāvarthamiti prati ||
yathāśvādijavaḥ puṃsāṃ kāryāṅgatvaṃ prakalpayet | paradharmo 'pi varṇānāṃ dhvanidharmāstathaiva naḥ ||
nanu dīrghādyanityatvādanityo vācako bhavet | ānupūrvīvadevāsya parihāro bhaviṣyati ||
tathodāttādibhedānāṃ saṃskāravaśagā matiḥ | teṣāṃ dīrghādivadbhedo na kadā citpratīyate ||
tatraikavarṇarūpatve bhedo 'pi syāddrutādivat | nātra varṇāntaravyaktiriva dhvanyantarodbhavaḥ ||
ta eva mṛdutīvratvaśīghratvādisamanvitāḥ | abhede cāpi varṇasya dhvanīnāṃ dviprakāratā ||
ke citsvarūpabodhārthāḥ ke cidbodhānuvartinaḥ | yugapatkramarūpeṇa saṃskārotpādahetavaḥ ||
tatra dīrghādibodhaḥ syātpūrveṣāṃ pracayo yadā | varṇātmaiva hi kālena tāvatā taiḥ pratīyate ||
yugapatpracitaistaiśca syādudāttādikalpanā | pracaye tvitareṣāṃ syādvatibhedo drutādikaḥ ||
varṇātmanyavabuddhe 'pi tadrūpāmeva te matim | śanairutpādayanti, iti nānyo varṇaḥ pratīyate ||
vyaktyākṛtikṛto bhedo yadyapyekāntato bhavet | varṇeṣu jaimineḥ pakṣastathāpi na virudhyate ||
nityatvayatnaḥ sarvo 'pi gatvādiṣu bhaviṣyati | gakārādivacaścaitatteṣveva na virotsyate ||
vicchinnayatnavyaṅgyaiśca nityaiḥ sarvagatairapi | vyatiriktapadārambho varṇairnātropapadyate ||
anārabdhe ca gośabde gośabdatvaṃ kathaṃ bhavet | varṇasāmānyavaccāpi na tatkalpanamarhati ||
varṇātmanāmabhedācca siddhā sāmānyadhīrapi | samudāyo 'pi tebhyo 'syo vāraṇīyo 'nayā diśā ||
abhedasamudāyastu teṣāṃ dharmo na duṣyati | teṣāmasti hi sāmarthyamarthapratyāyanaṃ prati ||
yāvanto yādṛśo ye ca yadarthapratipādane | varṇāḥ prajñātasāmarthyāste tathaivāvabodhakāḥ ||
teṣāṃ tu guṇabhūtānāmarthapratyāyanaṃ prati | sāhityamekakartrādikramaścāpi vivakṣitaḥ ||
kartraikatve nimitte ca krame sati niyāmakam | prayuñjānasya yatpūrvaṃ vṛddhebhyaḥ kramadarśanam ||
yaugapadyaṃ tvaśakyatvānnaiva teṣāmihāśritam | kartṛbhedaśca tatra syāt, na caivaṃ dṛśyate 'bhidhā ||
yugapaddṛśyasāmarthyā naiva śaktāḥ krame yathā | bhāvāstathā krame śaktā yaugapadye na śaknuyuḥ ||
dṛṣṭaśca pūrṇamāsādeḥ kramaḥ saṃhatyakāriṇaḥ | abhyāsānāṃ ca loke 'pi svādhyāyagrahaṇādiṣu ||
sādhanāditrayāṇāṃ ca vyāpārasyaikakālatā | sarvatrāstīti neha syādupālambhaḥ kramaṃ prati ||
niṣpannā eva dṛśyante vyāpārāḥ sarva eva hi | sūkṣmā vyāpārabhedāstu dṛśyate na kadā cana ||
ekasādhanasāṃsthāśca vyāpārāvayavā yadā | svarūpato nirīkṣyante yaugapadyamasattadā ||
kiṃ punarbahavo bhinnā bhinnasādhanasaṃśritāḥ | bhaveyuryaugapadyena vyāpārāḥ kramavartinaḥ ||
yadā tvādyaparispandād prabhṛtyā phalalābhataḥ | kriyā pūrvaparībhūtā lakṣyate varttate tadā ||
tenātrāpi vivakṣātaḥ prabhṛtyā 'rthāvabodhanāt | sākalyenekṣyamāṇe syādvyāpāre varttamānatā ||
pratyekaṃ ye punastatra vyāpārāstannirūpaṇam | phalāniṣpattito na syānnāstitvaṃ na ca tāvatā ||
phalānumeyatāyāṃ ca vyāpārasya phalaṃ prati | kārakāṇāṃ yathāsthānaṃ vyāpāre vartamānatā ||
avaśyam bhāvinī nityaṃ pratyāsattiśca kasya cit | na tāvatā vyapetatvāt itareṣāmanaṅgatā ||
dvyantaraikāntaratvena gakārau kārayordhruvam | arthaṃ pratyāyane śaktistatra sthau gamakau yataḥ ||
yathā visarjanīyasya vyavadhāne na śaktatā | tathaivetarayoḥ śaktirānantarye na vidyate ||
na ca yatraikaśo 'śaktistatra sarveṣvaśaktatā | tathā hyaṅgāni dṛśyante śālyādivahanādiṣu ||
śaktistatrāsti kā ciddhi vahane sā samṛddhyate | saṅghātena tu varṇānāṃ pratyekaṃ kā cidīkṣyate ||
na hyarthāvayavaḥ kaścitpratyekaṃ taiḥ pratīyate | samastasyātha vā kaścidbodhaleśo 'tra jāyate ||
rathasyāpi tu yatkāryaṃ śālyādivahanaṃ na tat | pratyekaṃ dṛśyate kiñcinmanāgapi yathehitam ||
atha yatkiñciducyeta vahane tadihāpi naḥ | svātmapratyayahetutvaṃ varṇeṣvarthe 'pi vā kva cit ||
yasyānavayavaḥ sphoṭo vyajyate varṇabuddhibhiḥ | so 'pi paryanuyogena vaivaitena vimucyate ||
tatrāpi prativarṇaṃ hi padasphoṭo na gamyate | na cāvayavaśo vyaktistadabhāvānna cātra dhīḥ ||
pratyekaṃ cāpyaśaktānāṃ samudāye 'pyaśaktayā | tatra yaḥ parihāraste sa no 'trāpi bhaviṣyati ||
sadbhāvavyatirekau ca tathāvayavavarjanam | tavādhikaṃ bhavettasmādyatno 'sāvarthabuddhiṣu ||
nānyathānupapattiśca bhavedarthamatiṃ prati | tadevāsyā nimittaṃ syājjāyate yadanantaram ||
sā ca varṇadvayajñāne 'tīte 'ntyajñānataḥ parā | bhavatītīdṛgevāsyā nimittamavakalpate ||
vinā saṃskārakalpena tadanantaravṛttitaḥ | kṛtānugrahasāmarthyo varṇo 'ntyaḥ pratipādakaḥ ||
eṣa eva tu saṃskāra iti ke citpracakṣate | adṛṣṭakalpanātītaṃ tāvanmātraṃ hi dṛśyate ||
atha vā vāsanaivāstu saṃskāraḥ, sarva eva hi | dṛḍhajñānagṛhīte 'rthe saṃskāro 'stīti manvate ||
tasyārthabuddhihetutve visaṃvādo 'sya nirṇaye | tadbhāvabhāvitāheturanyatreva pratīyate ||
saṃskāre niṣpramāṇe tu pūrvavṛttattvakalpanam | niṣpramāṇakameveti nānugrahaphalaṃ bhavet ||
yadyapi smṛtihetutvaṃ saṃskārasya vyavasthitam | kāryāntareṣu sāmarthyaṃ na tasya pratiṣidhyate ||
tena saṃskārasadbhāvo nānenaivaṃ prakalpyate | tasyārthabuddhihetutvamadṛṣṭaṃ kevalaṃ kṛtam ||
śabdapakṣe 'pi taccaitadadṛṣṭatvānna mucyate | kāryabodhanaśaktatvaṃ tulyaṃ saṃskāraśabdayoḥ ||
kṣīṇārthāpattirevaṃ ca na sphoṭaṃ parikalpayet | saṃskārakalpanā pūrvamavaśyam bhāvinī hi te ||
dhvanibhyo 'pyaparastāvanneṣyetārthamatiṃ prati | te vā yadyupalabhyeranvarṇāḥ pratyakṣato na ca ||
varṇānāṃ yaugapadyena yadi cāvaśyamarthitā | nityatvātsarvadā tatsyānna tu kāraṇatā tathā ||
itthaṃ kramagṛhītānāṃ yugapadyātha vā parā | sthitiḥ sā kāraṇaṃ tu syānnityamarthadhiyaṃ prati ||
yadvā pratyakṣataḥ pūrvaṃ kramajñāneṣu yatparam | samastavarṇavijñānaṃ tadarthajñānakāraṇam ||
tatra jñāne ca varṇānāṃ yaugapadyaṃ pratīyate | nāvaśyaṃ yaugapadyena pratyakṣasthena tadbhavet ||
citrarūpāṃ ca tāṃ buddhiṃ sadasadvarṇagocarām | ke cidāhuryathā varṇo gṛhyate 'ntaḥ pade pade ||
antyavarṇe 'pi vijñāte pūrvasaṃskārakāritam | smaraṇaṃ yaugapadyena sarveṣvanye pracakṣate ||
sarveṣu caivamartheṣu mānasaṃ sarvavādinām | iṣṭaṃ samuccayajñānaṃ kramajñāneṣu satsvapi ||
na cettadābhyupeyeta kramadṛṣṭeṣu naiva hi | śatādirūpaṃ jāyeta tatsamuccayadarśanam ||
tena śrotramanobhyāṃ syātkramādvarṇeṣu yadyapi | pūrvajñānaṃ parastāttu yugapatsmaraṇaṃ bhavet ||
tadārūḍhāstato varṇā na dūre 'rthāvabodhanāt | śabdādarthamatistena laukikairabhidhīyate ||
citrabuddhyānayā bhrāntyā varṇebhyo vyatirekataḥ | paścādgauriti vijñānaṃ pratyakṣaṃ kaiścidiṣyate ||
vailakṣaṇyaṃ tu tasyeṣṭamekaikajñānataḥ sphuṭam | varṇarūpāvabodhāttu na tadarthāntaraṃ bhavet ||
yadi cārthāntaratvaṃ syādekaikasmād trayasya tat | varṇatrayaparityāge buddhirnānyatra jāyate ||
gaurityekamatitvaṃ tu naivāsmābhirnivāryate | tadgrāhyaikārthatābhyāṃ ca śabde syādekatāmatiḥ ||
śaidhyādalpāntaratvācca gośabde sābhavedapi | devadattādiśabdeṣu sphuṭo bhedaḥ pratīyate ||
na gauṇaḥ śabda ityevaṃ granthasambandhanaṃ bhavet | asyakṣareṣu hetutvaṃ tatparaṃ vacanaṃ hi tat ||
śabdāditi ca hetutvaṃ pañcamyātrābhidhīyate | bhavatpakṣe 'pi caikāntājjñānena vyavadhirbhavet ||
gauṇo 'nyathā prasiddho vā prayujyetānyathā yadi | na cānyādṛṅnimittatvaṃ kasya citsampratīyate ||
svavyāpāravyavāyo hi sarvasminneva kārake | dṛṣṭo vyāpāra īdṛktu śabdasyetyavyavetatā ||
gakārāderyadā cānyo na loke śabda ucyate | tadā tasmātpratīte 'rthe śabdāditi kathaṃ bhavet ||
śabdajñānādisaṃskāravyaktasphoṭakṛte 'tha vā | pratyaye śabdajanyatvamiti gauṇaṃ prasajyate ||
saṃskārajananārthaṃ ca na śabdoccāraṇaṃ matam | arthapratītimuddiśya prayuktasya kramādayam ||
tasmāttādarthyataḥ śabdaḥ phalena vyapadiśyate | samuccayāvabodhe tu vyavadhānaṃ na kena cit ||
yadi cāpūrvasaṃskāra itikartavyateṣyate | varṇo 'ntyo gamakastasya śabdatvānmudhyatā bhavet ||
varṇā vā dhvanayo vāpi sphoṭaṃ na padavākyayoḥ | vyañjanti vyañjakatvena yathā dīpaprabhādayaḥ ||
sattvādghaṭādivacceti sādhanāni yathāruci | laukikavyatirekeṇa kalpite 'rthe bhavanti hi ||
nārthasya vācakaḥ sphoṭo varṇebhyo vyatirekataḥ | ghaṭāvivat, na dṛṣṭena virodho dharmasiddhitaḥ ||
pratiṣedhettu yo varṇān tajjñānānantarodbhavān | dṛṣṭabādho bhavettasya śaśicandraniṣedhavat ||
varṇotthā vārthadhīreṣā tajjñānānantarodbhavā | yedṛśī sā tadutthā hi dhūmāderiva bahnidhīḥ ||
dīpavadvā gakārādirgavādeḥ pratipādakaḥ | dhruvaṃ pratīyamānatvāt, tatpūrvaṃ pratipādanāt ||
varṇātiriktaḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ padeṣu mandaṃ phalamādadhāti | kāryāṇi vākyāvayavāśrayāṇi satyāni kartuṃ kṛta eṣa yatnaḥ ||

§ 5,13 ākṛtivāda akv

ākṛtivyatirikte 'rthe sambandho nityatāsya ca | na sidhyetāmiti jñātvā tadvācyatvamihocyate ||
tatsadbhāvaprasiddhyarthamatra tāvatprayatyate | vācyatve vakṣyate yuktirvyaktyā saha balābale ||
jātimevākṛtiṃ prāhurvyaktirākriyate yayā | sāmānyaṃ tacca piṇḍānāmekabuddhinibandhanam ||
tannimittaṃ ca yatkiñcitsāmānyaṃ śabdagocaram | sarva evecchatītyevamavirodho 'tra vādinām ||
sarvavastuṣu buddhiśca vyāvṛttyanugamātmikā | jāyate dvyātmakatvena vinā sā ca na siddhyati ||
viśeṣamātra iṣṭe ca na sāmānyamatirbhavet | sāmānyamātrabodhe tu nirnimittā viśeṣadhīḥ ||
na cāpyanyatarā bhrāntirupacāreṇa ceṣyate | dṛḍhatvātsarvadā buddherbhrāntistadbhrāntivādinām ||
mukhyayoścāpyadṛṣṭatvānnopacāreṇa kalpanā | bāhyārthaviṣayatvaṃ ca buddhīnāṃ pratipāditam ||
anyonyāpekṣitā nityaṃ syātsāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ | viśeṣāṇāṃ ca sāmānyaṃ te ca tasya bhavanti hi ||
nirviśeṣaṃ na sāmānyaṃ bhavec chaśaviṣāṇavat | sāmānyarahitatvācca viśeṣāstadvadeva hi ||
tadanātmakarūpeṇa hetū vācyāvimau punaḥ | tena tātyantabhedo 'pi syātsāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ ||
sāmānyabuddhiśaktitvaṃ viśeṣeṣveva yo vadet | vinā vastvantarāt, tena vācyā śaktistu kīdṛśī ||
grāhyā kiṃ vāpyasambodhā bhinnaikā vā tathaiva ca | gṛhyate yadi saikā ca jātirevānyaśabdikā ||
bhavennirviṣayā buddhiryadi śaktirna gṛhyate | na hi sadbhāvamātreṇa viśayaḥ kaścidiṣyate ||
parasparavibhinnatvādviśeṣā naikabuddhibhiḥ | gṛhyante viṣayāsattvāc chaktiścaiṣāṃ na vidyate ||
bhinnatve vāpi śaktīnāmekabuddhirna labhyate | viśeṣaśaktyabhede ca tāvanmātramatirbhavet ||
bhinnā viśeṣaśaktibhyaḥ sarvatrānugatāpi ca | pratyekaṃ samavetā ca tasmājjātirapīṣyatām ||
tenātmadharmo bhedānāmekadhīviṣayo 'sti naḥ | sāmānyamākṛtirjātiḥ śaktirvā so 'bhidhīyatām ||
nanu bhinne 'pi sattādau sāmānyamiti jāyate | buddhirvināpi sāmānyādanyasmātsā kathaṃ bhavet ||
vanopanyāsatulyo 'yamupanyāsaḥ kṛtastvayā | bhrāntitvena hi naitasyā bhrāntirgotvādidhīrapi ||
śabdātpūrvaṃ hi sarveṣu gavādāviva naikadhīḥ | vastutvaṃ cātra sāmānyaṃ dharmaṃ ke citpracakṣate ||
evaṃ tu kalpyamāne syātsāmānyānāmanantatā | punastena sahānyeṣu sāmānyamatirasti hi ||
viśeṣeṣvapi vastutvātsāmānyamiti dhīrbhavet | sattādiṣviva, tenaitatsāmānyaṃ nopapadyate ||
tasmādekasya bhinneṣu yā vṛttistannibandhanaḥ | sāmānyaśabdaḥ sattādāvekadhīkaraṇena vā ||
piṇḍeṣveva ca sāmānyam, nāntarā gṛhyate yataḥ | na hyākāśavadicchanti sāmānyaṃ nāma kiñcana ||
yadvā sarvagatatve 'pi vyaktiḥ śaktyanurodhataḥ | śaktiḥ kāryānumeyā hi vyaktidarśanahetukā ||
tena yatraiva dṛśyeta vyaktiḥ śaktaṃ tadeva tu | tenaiva ca na sarvāsu vyaktiṣvetatpratīyate ||
bhinnatve 'pi hi kāsāñcic chaktiḥ kāścidaśaktikāḥ | na ca paryanuyogo 'sti vastuśakteḥ kadā cana ||
vahnirdahati nākāśaṃ ko 'tra paryanuyujyatām | na cānyā mṛgyate yuktiryathā sandṛśyate tathā ||
na hi yuktyantaraṃ nāstītyetajjñānamanarthakam | dharmaścāvyabhicāryasya na mṛgya upalakṣaṇe ||
nānumānāvagamyaṃ tat, pratyakṣe lakṣaṇena kim | svābhāvikaśca sambandho jātivyaktyorna hetumān ||
tenaitasya prasiddhyarthaṃ nānyatsāmānyamiṣyate | śaktisiddhivadetasya svabhāvo 'tra na vāryate ||
yadvā naimittikatve 'pi tāvanmātrapratīkṣaṇāt | viśeṣeṣveva labdheṣu keṣu cinnānyavāñchanam ||
na vyañjantyapare kasmād, yatasteṣu na dṛśyate | tebhyo 'pi na nivṛttyarthaṃ mṛgyo hetuḥ svabhāvataḥ ||
sāmānyaṃ nānyadiṣṭaṃ cettasya vṛtterniyāmakam | gotvenāpi vinā kasmādgobuddhirna niyamyate ||
yathā tulye 'pi bhinnatve keṣu cidvṛttyapekṣitā | gotvāderanimitte 'pi tathā buddhirbhaviṣyati ||
viṣayeṇa hi buddhīnāṃ vinā notpattiriṣyate | viśeṣādanyadicchanti sāmānyaṃ tena taddhruvam ||
tā hi tena vinotpannā mithyāḥ syurviṣayādṛte | na tvanyena vinā vṛttiḥ sāmānyasyeha duṣyati ||
aniṣyamāṇe sāmānye vṛttiḥ śabdānumānayoḥ | naiva syāt, na hi sambandho bhedairānantyato bhavet ||
anubhūtatayā vāsau puruṣasyopayujyate | jātivyaktyostu sambandhe nānubhūtyā prayojanam ||
siddhe viṣayarūpe ca gotvādāvindriyaiḥ punaḥ | arthāpattyupalabdhā syāc chaktirekā niyāmikā ||
na cātmahetumevāsau siddhaṃ bādhitumarhati | śaktiśca naitayā buddhyā, nendriyaiḥ sā hi gṛhyate ||
sāmānyāntarayogānāmaniṣṭhā yā ca varṇyate | tayā sāmānyanāśaḥ syātsa ca dṛṣṭena bādhyate ||
sambandhastasya heturvā tadgrahe na ca kāraṇam | svarūpato gṛhīte 'rthe paścādetadvikalpyate ||
sāsnādyekārthasambandhi gotvamityupalakṣaṇam | na ca svasamavāyyeva kevalaṃ cihnamiṣyate ||
sāsnādibhyastu piṇḍasya bhedo nātyantato yadā | sāmānyasya ca piṇḍebhyastadā syādetaduttaram ||
kasmātsāsnādimatsveva gotvaṃ yasmāttadātmakam | tādātmyamasya kasmāccetsvabhāvāditi gamyatām ||
upalabdhyanusāreṇa vyavasthāsiddhirīdṛśī | svato gotvādibhedastu na tu vyañjakabhedataḥ ||
sā bhūddrutādivanmithyā, nyañjakasya tu kiṃkṛtaḥ | bhedo hastyādipiṇḍebhyaḥ, svataścet, iha tatsamam ||
vyaṅgyajātiviśeṣāccet, prāptamanyonyasaṃśrayam | tasmātsvābhāviko bhedo jātivyaktyoḥ pratīyate ||
anekānanyavṛttittvānna sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ | ekavastvātmatā yuktā varaṃ tenaupacārikam ||
bhinnebhyaścāpyabhinnatvādbhedastatsvātmavadbhavet | ekasmādvāpyabhinnatvādvyaktyekatvaṃ pratīyate ||
ekānekatvamekasya tathānyānanyatā katham | tatsāmānyaṃ viśeṣaścetyevamādi ca duṣkaram ||
virodhastāvadekāntādvaktumatra na yujyate | sāmānyānanyavijñāte viśeṣe naikavṛttitā ||
sāmānyānanyavṛttitvaṃ viśeṣātmaikabhāvataḥ | evañca parihartavyā bhinnābhinnatvakalpanā ||
kena ciddhyātmanaikatvaṃ nānātvaṃ cāsya kena cit | sāmānyasya tu yo bhedaṃ brūte tasya viśeṣataḥ ||
darśayitvābhyupetavyam, viśeṣaikyaṃ ca jātitaḥ | yathā kalmāṣavarṇasya yatheṣṭaṃ varṇanigrahaḥ ||
citratvādvastuno 'pyevaṃ bhedābhedāvadhāraṇam | sāmānyāṃśe tu niṣkṛṣya bhedo yena prasādhyate ||
tasya hetorasiddhatvaṃ siddhaścetsiddhasādhanam | bhedebhyo 'nanyarūpeṇa sāmānyaṃ gṛhyate yadā ||
tadāviśeṣamātreṇa vastu pratyavabhāsate | tadudbhūtyā ca sāmānyaṃ tadbhāvānuguṇaṃ sthitam ||
sadapyagrāhyarūpatvādasadvatpratibhāti naḥ | viśeṣānapi sāmānyādyadā bhedena buddhyate ||
tadā sāmānyamātratvamevameva pratīyate | yadā tu śabalaṃ vastu yugapatpratipadyate ||
tadānyānanyabhedādi sarvameva pralīyate | na ca tattādṛśaṃ kaścic chabdaḥ śaknoti bhāṣitum ||
sāmānyāṃśānapoddhṛtya padaṃ sarvaṃ pravarttate | samastavastvapekṣāṃ ca padārthānāmapoddhṛtim ||
ke cidāhurasadrūpam, aṃśatvaṃ tu na vāryate | sārūpyameva sāmānyaṃ piṇḍānāṃ yena kalpyate ||
tena sārūpyaśabdena kiṃ punaḥ pratipadyate | samānarūpabhāvaścejjātiḥ sāsmābhiriṣyate ||
sādṛśyamatha sārūpyaṃ kasya keneti kathyatām | na tāvacchālaleyena bāhuleyādayaḥ samāḥ ||
viśeṣarūpataḥ, ye 'pi tatsaṃsthānādibhiḥ samāḥ | śābaleya iveti syāttatra buddhirna gauriva ||
śābaleyo 'yamiti vā bhrāntyā gauriti nāsti dhīḥ | śābaleyasvarūpaṃ ca na gaurityavatiṣṭhate ||
tadanyeṣu hi gobuddhirna syātsusadṛśeṣvapi | dṛśyate sā na cānyatra gorūpaṃ tatra vidyate ||
na cānyo gauḥ prasiddho 'sti tatsādṛśyena dhīrbhavet | na cāpi sa iti jñānaṃ sadṛśeṣvasti sarvadā ||
sarvapuṃsāmato bhrāntirnaiṣā bādhakavarjanāt | sarvajñānāni mithyā ca prasajyante 'tra kalpane ||
viśeṣagrahaṇābhāvādeva gauḥ kaśca kathyatām | babhūva yadyasau pūrvamasmadādestadagrahāt ||
sādṛśyāvadhṛtirnāstītyato godhīrna labhyate | na cāvayavasāmānyairvinā sādṛśyakalpanā ||
sāmānyapratyayotpādo na viśeṣeṣu jāyate | vyaktitaścātireko 'sya syānna veti vicārite ||
sāmānyameva sādṛśyaṃ bhavedvā vyaktimātrakam | tena nātyantabhinno 'rthaḥ sārūpyamiti varṇitam | granthe vindhyanivāsena bhrānteḥ sādṛśyamucyate ||

§ 5,14 apohavāda apv

agonivṛttiḥ sāmānyaṃ vācyaṃ yaiḥ parikalpitam | gotvaṃ vastveva tairuktamago 'pohagirā sphuṭam ||
bhāvāntaramabhāvo hi purastātpratipāditaḥ | tatrāśvādinivṛttyātmā bhāvaḥ ka iti kathyatām ||
neṣṭo 'sādhāraṇastāvadviṣayo nirvikalpanāt | tathā ca śābaleyādeḥ, asāmānyaprasaṅgataḥ ||
śābaleyādirūpaṃ hi na sāmānyaṃ parasparam | na vaikamitareṣāṃ vastatrānantārthatā bhavet ||
na ca sākṣādviśeṣasya te 'pohyā iti yuktimat | na śābaleyavijñānamagovyāvṛttibandhanam ||
nivṛttyā bāhuleyādestadvijñānaṃ pravartate | kuryādagonivṛttiṃ cennāpohetātmavaddhi tān ||
tenāṃśenānapohaśca svarūpeṇāpyapohanam | kalpyate cedvirodhaḥ syātsamamākṣepavāraṇe ||
tasmātprātyātmikai rūpairago 'poho na yujyate | samudāye 'pi naiteṣāmagovyāvṛttisambhavaḥ ||
sarvopalabdhau tadbuddhirvyāsajyaivaṃ pravartate | na pratyekaṃ bhavedeṣā, na samasteṣvaśaktitaḥ ||
tasmātsarveṣu yadrūpaṃ pratyekaṃ pariniṣṭhitam | gobuddhistannimittā syādgotvādanyacca nāsti tat ||
nanu ca prāgabhāvādau sāmānyaṃ vastu neṣyate | sattaiva hyatra sāmānyamanutpattyādirūṣitā ||
tāmutpattyādyanusyūtāṃ satteti pratijānate | anyāpohānuviddhā tu saivābhāvaḥ pratīyate ||
anityatvaṃ vināśākhyakriyāsāmānyamucyate | abrāhmaṇatvaṃ kin tu syādbhinneṣu kṣattriyādiṣu ||
puruṣatvaṃ catuḥsaṃstham, viśeṣeṣu ca nāstidhīḥ | sāmānyapratyayaścaiṣu pratyekamupajāyate ||
tenātra brāhmaṇābhāvaḥ sāmānyaṃ syādavastu tat | gotvādāvapi tenaiva sāmānyapratyayo bhavet ||
kaiścittvatraikaśabdatvamakṣādāviva kalpitam | jātitrayasya, naivaṃ tu sambhavatyaghaṭādiṣu ||
nātra hyanantake bhede sādhāraṇyaṃ nirūpyate | tasmātkriyāguṇāḥ ke ciddhetavo 'nanyavartinaḥ ||
puruṣatvaṃ nañā caitadbrāhmaṇebhyo nivartitam | cāturvarṇyaprasaktaṃ sadgamyate 'rthādibhiryathā ||
yadyapyavāntarā nāsti triṣu jātirvyavasthitā | nañsāmārthyānnaratvaṃ tu tryādhāraṃ sampratīyate ||
śabdasāmarthyabhedena varṇeṣu matibhinnatā | puṃstve tricaturādhāre paryudāsasvarūpataḥ ||
dūrāntike kṣaṇe śaktirgṛdhravāyasacakṣuṣoḥ | yathā rūpe tathā puṃstve pumabrāhmaṇaśabdayoḥ ||
brāhmaṇavyatiriktārthavṛtti puṃstvamitīdṛśam | vākyaṃ yatra pravarteta tatrābrāhmaṇadhīpade ||
pārthivatvādisāmānyamevamevāghaṭādiṣu | ghaṭatvādivinirmuktaṃ viṣayaḥ sampratīyate ||
asādhāraṇabhāvācca nañā śabdo viśeṣitaḥ | tāvanmātreṇa rahite sāmānye vyavatiṣṭhate ||
viśeṣe pratiṣiddhe hi sāmānyaṃ yadanantaram | sāmānyākāṅkṣiṇaṃ śabdaṃ niruṇaddhi tadātmani ||
prathamātikrame tasya kāraṇaṃ naiva vidyate | brāhmaṇatvādato 'petaṃ naratvamavaśiṣyate ||
vyudasya brāhmaṇatvaṃ ca nañi jāte viśeṣaṇe | naratvodasanaṃ yattu kalpetāśrutameva tat ||
tasmādyasyaiva te bhedā niṣiddhyeraṃstadarthataḥ | bhedāntarasthaṃ sāmānyam, loke 'pyevaṃ pratīyate ||
prasaṅginyāṃ ca tadbuddhau niṣedho 'rthādapīṣyate | tanmātrarahite cārthe sādṛśyāttanmatirbhavet ||
sādṛśyameva vā vācyamiṣṭamabrāhmaṇādiṣu | taccāvayavasāmānyād, vināpyetena lakṣyate ||
kva cidvināpi sādṛśyātsāhacaryādihetukā | nañyuktaśabdavṛttiḥ syādyathā vakṣyatyanīkṣaṇe ||
īkṣaṇavyatiriktā hi kriyā tatrāpyapekṣitā | pratyāsatterna saṅkalpamatikramya pratīyate ||
nāmadhātvarthayogī ca naiva nañ pratiṣedhakaḥ | vadato 'brāhmaṇādharmāvanyamātravirodhinau ||
yatrāpyākhyātasambandhātpratiṣedhaḥ pratīyate | tatraudāsīnyavastveva pratipattā 'valambate ||
tasmādvastunyapohāḥ syuḥ, api cāvastukalpane | prāgantyebhyo viśeṣebhyo na kiñcidvastu labhyate ||
na cāntyairvyavahāro 'sti, śakyaṃ naiṣāṃ nirūpaṇam | apohaśabdavācyātha śūnyatānyaprakārikā ||
tasyāṃ cāśvādibuddhīnāmātmāṃśagrahaṇaṃ bhavet | tatrānyāpohavācyatvaṃ mudhaivābhyupagamyate ||
sāmānyaṃ vasturūpaṃ hi buddhyākāro bhaviṣyati | śabdārtho 'rthānapekṣo hi vṛthāpohaḥ prakalpitaḥ ||
vasturūpā ca sā buddhiḥ śabdārtheṣūpajāyate | tena vastveva kalpeta vācyaṃ buddhyanapohakam ||
asatyapi ca bāhye 'rthe vākyārthapratibhā tathā | padārthe 'pi tathaiva syātkimapohaḥ prakalpyate ||
buddhyantarādvyavacchedo na ca buddheḥ pratīyate | svarūpotpādamātrācca nānyamaṃśaṃ bibharti sā ||
bhinnasāmānyavacanā viśeṣavacanāśca ye | sarve bhaveyuḥ paryāyā yadyapohasya vācyatā ||
nanu bhedādapohānāṃ prasaṅgo 'yaṃ na yujyate | sāmānyāpohakḷptyā cedvastumātre samaṃ tava ||
bhidyante mama vastutvātsāmānyāni parasparam | asaṅkīrṇasvabhāvāni na caikatvaṃ vitanvate ||
saṃsṛṣṭaikatvanānātvavikalparahitātmanām | avastutvādapohānāṃ tava syādbhinnatā katham ||
yadi vā bhidyamānatvādvastvasādhāraṇāṃśavat | avastutve tvanānātvātparyāyatvānna mucyate ||
nanu cāpohyabhedena bhedo 'pohasya setsyati | na viśeṣaḥ svatastasya parataścaupacārikaḥ ||
tenaivādhārabhedenāpyasya bhedo na yujyate | na hi sambandhibhedena bhedo vastunyapīṣyate ||
kimutāvastvasaṃsṛṣṭamanyataścānivartitam | anavāptaviśeṣāṃśaṃ yatkimapyanirūpitam ||
tasmādyathaiva bhede 'pi piṇḍānāṃ naiva bhidyate | tathaivāpohyabhede 'pi nāneko 'yaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
bhede vā pratipiṇḍaṃ syādago 'pohaḥ, tathā sati | sāmānyaṃ śābaleyāderiti neṣṭaṃ prasidhyati ||
saṃsargiṇo 'pi cādhārā yaṃ na bhindanti rūpataḥ | apohyaiḥ sa bahirbhūtairbhidyetetyatikalpanā ||
agavyaśvātirekaḥ syādanaśvaśca gavādhikaḥ | śeṣaṃ hastyādyapohyaṃ tu dvayorapi na bhidyate ||
tatraikabhedādbhedo 'stu bahvabhedādabhinnatā | bhūyasāṃ syātsadharmatvamityabhedaḥ prasajyate ||
gauśca hastyādyapohena nāśvarūpādviśeṣyate | karoti tadapohaṃ cedaikarūpyaṃ virudhyate ||
sarvaśabdeṣu caikaikamapohyamatiricyate | tatrāsādhāraṇatvena tanmātrāpohyatā bhavet ||
tato 'śvāpoharūpatvātsiṃhādiḥ sarva eva te | tannimittamago 'pohaṃ bibhraducyeta gauriti ||
sarvāpoho yadīṣyeta, sa vaktavyaḥ kathaṃ punaḥ | yadi pratyekarūpeṇa nāpohyānantatā bhavet ||
bhinnatvāccāpyapohyānāṃ bhinno 'pohaḥ prasajyate | tatraikasminbhavetpiṇḍe 'nantajātisamanvayaḥ ||
tato gauriti sāmānyaṃ vācyamekaṃ na sidhyati | jātyantaramatiścaiṣu bhavejjātyantareṣviva ||
samudāyātmanā nāpi bhavedeṣāmapohyatā | samudāyo hi naikena vinā dharmeṇa jāyate ||
nāpyekadeśatā teṣāmasti nāpyekakālatā | vyatiriktaśca saṅghātasteṣāṃ kaścinna vidyate ||
yadi tvavyatiriktaḥ syādānanyaṃ tadavasthitam | yadi sāmānyarūpeṇa te 'pohyante, na vastutā ||
kathaṃ vā vastvapohyeta, nābhāvo bhāvamṛcchati | apohyamāne cābhāve bhāva evāvaśiṣyate ||
apohyabhedakḷptiśca nābhāvābhedato bhavet | tadbhedo 'pohabhedāccet, prāptamanyonyasaṃśrayam ||
gosāmānyasya bhinnatvādagaurityeṣa bhidyate | agaurityasya bhedena gosāmānyaṃ ca bhidyate ||
agāvo 'śvādayaśca syuste 'pyabhāvātmakāḥ punaḥ | karkādyapekṣayā te 'pi tathetyevaṃ na gamyate ||
kimapohyam, kva cāpohaḥ, gopiṇḍeṣvevameva ca | tatra syāddvayamapyetadantyeṣu paramāṇuṣu ||
na cāntyeṣu dvayorasti vyavahāro bhidāṃ prati | gavāśvaparamāṇūnāṃ viśeṣaśca na vidyate ||
svarūpajātisaṃsthānaparimāṇādilakṣaṇaḥ | kimapohyaṃ kva cāpohastatrāpi na viśiṣyate ||
na cāprasiddhasārūpyānapohaviṣayātmanā | śaktaḥ kaścidapi jñātuṃ gavādīnaviśeṣataḥ ||
apohyānapi cāśvādīnekadharmānvayādṛte | na nirūpayituṃ śaktistatrāpoho na siddhyati ||
na cānvayavinirmukte pravṛttirliṅgaśabdayoḥ | tābhyāṃ ca na vināpoho na cāsādhāraṇe 'nvayaḥ ||
apohaścāpyaniṣpannaḥ sāhacaryaṃ kva dṛśyatām | tasminnadṛśyamāne ca na tayoḥ syātpramāṇatā ||
na cādarśanamātreṇa tābhyāṃ pratyāyanaṃ bhavet | sarvatraiva hyadṛṣṭatvātpratyāyyaṃ nāvaśiṣyate ||
athāsatyapi sārūpye syādapohasya kalpanā | gavāśvayorayaṃ kasmādago 'poho na kalpyate ||
śābaleyācca bhinnatvaṃ bāhuleyāśvayoḥ samam | sāmānyaṃ nānyadiṣṭaṃ cetkvāgo 'pohaḥ pravartatām ||
indriyairnāpyago 'pohaḥ prathamaṃ vyavasīyate | nānyatra śabdavṛttiśca kiṃ dṛṣṭvā sa prayujyatām ||
pūrvoktena prabandhena nānumāpyatra vidyate | sambandhānubhavo 'pyasya tena naivopapadyate ||
nivṛttivācinaḥ śabdā na prasiddhāśca yān prati | teṣāmagorasiddhatvānna sāmānyanirākriyā ||
agośabdābhidheyatvaṃ gamyatāṃ ca kathaṃ punaḥ | na dṛṣṭo yatra gośabdaḥ sambandhānubhavakṣaṇe ||
ekasmāttarhi gopiṇḍādyadanyatsarvameva tat | bhavedapohyamityevaṃ na sāmānyasya vācyatā ||
siddhaścāgaurapohyeta goniṣedhātmakaśca saḥ | tatra gaureva vaktavyo nañā yaḥ pratiṣidhyate ||
sa cedagonivṛttyātmā bhavedanyonyasaṃśrayaḥ | siddhaścedgaurapohyārthaṃ vṛthāpohaprakalpanā ||
gavyasiddhe tvagaurnāsti tadabhāve ca gauḥ kutaḥ | nādhārādheyavṛttyādisambandhaścāpyabhāvayoḥ ||
na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu gamyate 'pohavattayā | kathaṃ vā parikalpyeta sambandho vastvavastunoḥ ||
svarūpasattvamātreṇa na ca kiñcidviśeṣaṇam | svabuddhyā rajyate yena viśeṣyaṃ tadviśeṣaṇam ||
na cāpyaśvādiśabdebho jāyate 'pohabodhanam | viśiṣṭabuddhiriṣṭeha na cājñātaviśeṣaṇā ||
na cānyarūpamanyādṛkkuryājjñānaṃ viśeṣaṇam | kathaṃ cānyādṛśe jñāte taducyeta viśeṣaṇam ||
athānyathā viśeṣye 'pi syādviśeṣaṇakalpanā | tathā sati hi yatkiñcitprasajyeta viśeṣaṇam ||
abhāvarūpagamye ca na viśeṣye 'sti vastutā | viśeṣitamapohena vastu vācyaṃ na te 'styataḥ ||
yadyapyapohanirmukte na vṛttiḥ śabdaliṅgayoḥ | yuktā tathāpi buddhistu jñāturvastvavalambate ||
na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu buddhau viparivarttate | na cāpi nirvikalpatvāttasya yuktā viśeṣyatā ||
śabdenāgamyamānaṃ ca viśeṣyamiti sāhasam | tena sāmānyameṣṭavyaṃ viṣayo buddhiśabdayoḥ ||
yadā cāśabdavācyatvānna vyaktīnāmapohyatā | tadāpohyeta sāmānyaṃ tasyāpohācca vastutā ||
nāpohyatvamabhāvānāmabhāvābhāvavarjanāt | vyakto 'pohāntare 'pohastasmātsāmānyavastunaḥ ||
abhāvasya ca yo 'bhāvaḥ sa cettasmādvilakṣaṇaḥ | bhāva eva bhavenno cedgauragauste prasajyate ||
yadyapyaneṣu śabdeṣu vastunaḥ syādapohyatā | sacchabdasya tvabhāvākhyānnāpohyaṃ bhinnamiṣyate ||
tatrāsato 'pi bhāvatvamitikleśo mahānbhavet | tadasiddhau na sattāsti na cāsattā prasidhyati ||
na cāpi vāsanābhedādbhedaḥ sadrūpatāpi vā | apohānāṃ prakalpyeta, na hyavastuni vāsanā ||
smṛtiṃ muktvā na cāstyasyāḥ śaktiyogaḥ kriyāntare | tasmānnānyādṛśe sārthe karotyanyādṛśīṃ matim ||
bhavadbhiḥ śabdabhedo 'pi tannimitto na labhyate | na hyasādhāraṇaḥ śabdo vācakaḥ prāgadṛṣṭitaḥ ||
bhinnatvāccāpi naivaikā vāsanā taiḥ prakalpyate | na cāsti śabdavastvekaṃ vāsanāṃ yatkariṣyati ||
tatra śabdāntarāpohe sāmānye parikalpite | tathaivāvasturūpatvāc chabdabhedo na kalpyate ||
vācakānāṃ yathā caivaṃ vācyavācakayormithaḥ | na cāpyapohyabhedena bhedo 'stītyupapāditam ||
nāgṛhītaśca gamakaḥ śabdāpohaḥ kathañcana | pratyakṣaṃ na ca tacchaktaṃ na ca sto liṅgavācakau ||
yataḥ syādgrahaṇaṃ tasya, liṅgādīnāṃ ca kalpane | na vyavastheti vācyaivaṃ vinā pratyakṣamūlataḥ ||
na gamyagamakatvaṃ syādavastutvādapohayoḥ | bhavatpakṣe, yathā loke khapuṣpaśaśaśṛṅgayoḥ ||
vṛṣṭimeghāsatordṛṣṭvā yadyanaikāntikaḥ vadet | vastvevātrāpi matpakṣe bhavatpakṣe 'pyadaḥ kutaḥ ||
vidhirūpaśca śabdārtho yena nābhyupagamyate | na bhavedvyatireko 'pi tasya tatpūrvako hyasau ||
niṣedhadvayayogitvādasato yāpyabhāvatā | savastuke bhavetsāpi na tucche buddhyasambhavāt ||
nanu yuktyānayaivāyaṃ vastunāpi na bhidyate | apohastena doṣo 'tra pūrvokto na bhaviṣyati ||
siddhamevaṃ madiṣṭaṃ syāt, naivānyā gatirasti hi | abhāve vastubuddhirvā yadvā vastunyabhāvadhīḥ ||
tatrābhāvātmakatve syānnirnimittaiva vastudhīḥ | vastunyabhāvabodhastu sidhyatyanyamapekṣya tu ||
apohamātravācyatvaṃ yadi cābhyupagamyate | nīlotpalādiśabdeṣu śabalārthābhidhāyiṣu ||
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvasāmānādhikaraṇyayoḥ | na siddhiḥ, na hyanīlatvavyudāse 'nutpalacyutiḥ ||
nāpi tatretarastasmānna viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇe | śabdayornāpi te syātāmabhidheyānapekṣayoḥ ||
sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca na bhinnatvādapohayoḥ | arthataścaitadiṣyeta kīdṛśyādheyatā tayoḥ ||
na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu gamyate 'nyacca nāsti te | agamyamānamaikārthyaṃ śabdayoḥ kvopayujyate ||
athānyāpohavadvastu vācyamityabhidhīyate | tatrāpi paratantratvādvyāptiḥ śabdena durbalā ||
khaṇḍe bhinnavyapohyatvādyathaiva madhurādibhiḥ | śuklādivyāptyabhāvena nākṣepo na viśeṣaṇam ||
tathaivāsadvyudāsāṃśāvacchinnārthāvadhāraṇe | nāghaṭādinivṛttyaṃśavyāptiḥ śabdātpratīyate ||
vyāptiścedartharūpeṇa sattayaivaṃ hi sā bhavet | na ghaṭatvādimānarthaḥ kaścinna vyāpyate tayā ||
na ca vastutayā vyāptistayā śabdasya vāryate | pratītiṃ prati tulyastu vyāpāro vastvavastunoḥ ||
nirbhāgo 'pi hi vastvātmā śabdairbhāgena gamyate | na hi sacchabdavijñānādghaṭādyarthaḥ pratīyate ||
tenānākṣepadoṣo 'sti, bhāktadoṣaśca vidyate | viśeṣaṇatvānmukhyatvamapohasya hi jātivat ||
tasmāttadvati gauṇatvānnābhidheyatvasambhavaḥ | avastutvānna mukhyaścet, na syādevaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||
bhedāścāpohavantaḥ syusteṣāṃ cāvācyatoditā | ānantyavyabhicārābhyām, anyo nāsti tvapohavān ||
nāpohavattvamanyaddhi bhedāpohāntare 'sti te | taccāpi kalpyamānaṃ syādabhāvo bhāva eva vā ||
vastu cejjātireva syādavastutve 'pi pūrvavat | sambandho vaiṣa kalpyeta tasya ceṣṭā na vācyatā ||
na caiko 'pohavānartho vartate 'rthāntare kva cit | tasmādapi na sāmānyaṃ vācyaṃ na ca viśeṣaṇam ||
nātmanyavidyamānatvādviśeṣo 'pohasūcakaḥ | tasmānna tairviśeṣyatvaṃ prakṛṣṭatvena nīlavat ||
arthākṣepo 'pi nāstyeva sandehālliṅgaliṅgivat | na sāmānyātmanāpohastairvinā na ca siddhyati ||
evameva tvanākṣepaḥ syādapohena vastunaḥ | yataḥ śaśaviṣāṇe 'pi tadapohasya sambhavaḥ ||
liṅgasaṃkhyādisambandho na vāpohasya vidyate | vyakteravyapadeśyatvāttaddvāreṇāpi nāstyasau ||
na hyasādhāraṇatvena sāpohenāpi gamyate | na cāpyagamyamānasya vastunaḥ syādviśeṣyatā ||
liṅgasaṃkhyādyapohānāṃ nopakāraḥ svarūpataḥ | vastunaścopakāryatvaṃ kathaṃ śabdaiḥ pratīyate ||
na vinānupalabdhyā ca syādabhāvamatiḥ kva cit | na cābhāvaprameyatvaṃ gotvāderiha gamyate ||
ākhyāteṣu ca nānyasya nivṛttiḥ sampratīyate | na paryudāsarūpaṃ hi niṣedhyaṃ tatra vidyate ||
na neti hyucyamāne 'pi niṣedhasya niṣedhanam | pacatītyaniṣiddhaṃ tu svarūpeṇāvatiṣṭhate ||
sādhyatvapratyayaścātra tathābhūtādirūpaṇam | niṣpannatvādapohasya nirnimittaṃ prasajyate ||
vidhyādāvartharāśau ca nānyāpohanidarśanam | nañaścāpi nañā yuktādapohaḥ kīdṛśo bhavet ||
cādīnāmapi nañyogo naivāstītyanapohanam | vākyārtho 'nyanivṛttiśca vyapadeṣṭuṃ na śakyate ||
ananyāpohaśabdādau vācyaṃ na ca nirūpyate | prameyajñeyaśabdāderapohyaṃ kuta eva tu ||
apohyakalpanāyāṃ tu varaṃ vastveva kalpitam | jñānākāraniṣedhācca nāntarārthābhidheyatā ||
na cāpyapohyatā, tasmānnāpohasteṣu sidhyati | evamityādiśabdānāṃ na vāpohyaṃ nirūpyate ||
virodhitvena bhedānāmapoho yadi kalpyate | virodho 'pohatastatra virodhāccāpyapohanam ||
na sāmānyāpahāritvaṃ vidhirūpeṇa tatra te | palaśādīnapohyāto vṛkṣaṃ harati śiṃśapā ||
sāmānyādyanapohaśca nāvirodhena kalpyate | na hi śabdasvarūpāṇāṃ syādviruddhāviruddhatā ||
na ca vastusvarūpeṇa tasya śabdairasaṅgateḥ | prākśabdavyāpṛternāpi sāpohānāṃ pratīyate ||
anyenānavabuddhe 'rthe sadā śabdaḥ pravartate | sāmānyātmakatā tasya kena rūpeṇa gamyate ||
śabdānurūpataścetsyādanyāpohanirūpaṇam | bhinnatvādvṛkṣatarvāderapohaḥ kena vāryate ||
śabdaspṛṣṭervināpoho na ca liṅgena gamyate | na viruddhāviruddhatvaṃ tasya liṅgācca sidhyati ||
adṛṣṭatvādvyudāsastu purastādeva vāritaḥ | sāmānyaśabdo bhedena neṣyate vācakātmanā ||
vyudāsastatra durvāraḥ, kathañciddṛṣṭatā punaḥ | brāhmaṇe kṣattriyasyāpi paryudāsaḥ prasajyate ||
ākāṅkṣaṇādathātyāgastulyo dravyakriyādiṣu | vṛkṣeṇāto 'napohaḥ syāttiṣṭhatyāderasaṃśayam ||
puruṣasya tathā rājño vyudāse na viśeṣyatā | avyudāsatvapakṣe ca syānnīlotpalatulyatā ||
vṛkṣatvapārthivadravyasajjñeyeṣu yaducyate | prātilomyānulomyena vidhau sarvārthabodhanam ||
tadayuktam, na sarvo hi śabdaḥ sarvatra dṛśyate | deśāvibhāgato vṛttirnetrasyāpi rasādiṣu ||
grāhakatvena vṛttistu pratijāti vyavasthitā | cakṣurādivadevātra saṅkaro na bhaviṣyati ||
nivṛttaceṣṭe śabde ca vyāptyavyāptikṛtaṃ punaḥ | sattvāderbodhakatvaṃ syādekanyūnātirekataḥ ||
tavaiva doṣaḥ syādeṣa viśeṣe yasya varttate | sāmānyaśabdaḥ, vācyānāṃ bhedo nāpyasti vastutaḥ ||
api caikatvanityatvapratyekasamavāyitāḥ | nirupākhyeṣvapoheṣu kurvato 'sūtrakaḥ paṭaḥ ||
tasmādyeṣveva śabdeṣu nañyogasteṣu kevalam | bhavedanyanivṛttyaṃśaḥ svātmaivānyatra gamyate ||
jñeyārthānyānapohatvaṃ pramāṅgatvāttvagādivat | yenoktaṃ tasya nañyuktaiḥ śabdaiḥ syādvyabhicāritā ||
pakṣīkuryādyadā sarvāṃstadāthāvītahetubhiḥ | anaikānto virodhaśca sarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ ||
nāpohata itīdaṃ ca kārakatvena cedbhavet | kevalāpohabuddhervā tataḥ syātsiddhasādhyatā ||
athānyāpohavatyarthe vṛttirnāstīti sādhyate | tataḥ prākpakṣabādhaḥ syādgotve 'thāśvādyabhāvataḥ ||
sādhyahīnaśca dṛṣṭāntaścakṣurādyapi tasya hi | varttate 'pohavatyeva taṃ yadyapi na budhyate ||
athānyāpohanirbhāsā na buddhiḥ siddhasādhanam | apoharūpamapyetadvastvityeva hi gamyate ||
athāpohanimittāsya vṛttirarthe niṣidhyate | vyatirekāṅgateṣṭatvātpunaḥ prākpakṣabādhanam ||
anumāne tathā caitadityanaikāntiko bhavet | sandehabādhajātena pratyakṣeṇāpi cetasā ||
viruddhatā ca hetoḥ syāt, śabdaḥ śrotrādivadyataḥ | ātmāntaḥ karaṇākāśaiḥ svavācitvaṃ jahāti vāḥ ||
vidhirūpapravṛttirvā śabdo 'pohena varttate | anumānāṅgabhūtatvādyathaiva pratiṣedhakaḥ ||
jātiṃ vā na bravītyeṣa vyaktiṃ vā tadviśeṣitām | pramāyāmaṅgabhūtatvāttvakśrotrādi yathaiva ca ||
evaṃ sādhanamārgeṇa vācyāvācyanirūpaṇā | nāvātiṣṭhata ityatra kathyate lokavartmanā ||

§ 5,15 vanavāda vav

sāsnādibhirviśiṣṭatvamākṛterucyate katham | yadāvayavisambandhi gotvaṃ nāvayave sthitam ||
ekāvayavisambandhasteṣāṃ gotvena vidyate | tenāsādhāraṇatvātte syurgotvasyopalakṣaṇam ||
piṇḍe sattādijātīnāṃ bahvīnāṃ samavetatā | tābhyo viśiṣyate gotvaṃ sāsnādibhirasaṃśayam ||
na caite vyañjakāstasya guṇavadvā viśeṣaṇam | tathā hi nāgṛhīteṣu teṣu syādgotvabodhanam ||
teṣāṃ ca vyañjakaiḥ svaiḥ syātpunargrahaṇakalpanā | tathā satyanavasthā syāt na syādgotvāvadhāraṇam ||
sarveṣu ca gṛhīteṣu sāsnādiṣu bhavenmatiḥ | gotve, na caiṣu sarveṣu yugapadbuddhisambhavaḥ ||
tasmātsadbhāvamātreṇa mahattvādau yathaiva dhīḥ | kriyate 'vayavaiḥ piṇḍe tathā jātiguṇādiṣu ||
yadyevamagṛhīteṣu teṣu kiṃ sā na jāyate | taddeśavyatirekeṇa grāhyaṃ yena na vidyate ||
gṛhyamāṇe tu gotvādau nāntarīyakahetukaḥ | sāsnādeḥ kasya cidbodhastaddeśatvena jāyate ||
tadanatyantabhedādvā tadviśiṣṭeti kīrtyate | bādhaḥ parānumānasya na pratyakṣeti bodhyate ||
pareṣāṃ sādhanaṃ hyatra nākṛtiḥ piṇḍataḥ pṛthak | taddhīhānāvavijñānātpaṅktiyūthavanādivat ||
sarvatra lokasiddhatvānna vācyaṃ sādhanaṃ svayam | niṣedhatāṃ pareṣāṃ tu virodhaṃ lokato vadet ||
visaṃvādo na dṛśyeta yadi pratyakṣatākṛteḥ | pramāṇe 'pi visaṃvādāttārkikeṣu kuto nviyam ||
rūpādāvapi teṣāṃ hi pratyakṣatvena sammate | vivādaḥ, naiva lokastu jātau vipratipadyate ||
vyavahārā hi dṛśyante sāmānyārthanibandhanāḥ | dadhitakrādidānādau kauṇḍinyabrāhmaṇādiṣu ||
ākṛtirjātirevātra saṃsthānaṃ na prakalpyate | na hi vāyvagniśabdādau kiñcitsaṃsthānamiṣyate ||
anyadanyacca saṃsthānaṃ pratipiṇḍaṃ pratīyate | saṃyogātmakatāyāṃ tu vibhāgeṣu vinaśyati ||
atha saṃsthānasāmānyam, aśvādāvapi tatsamam | na gotvena vinā hyetadvyavacchinnaṃ pratīyate ||
sarvapratikṛtīnāṃ ca saṃsthāne satyapīdṛśe | na gotvādimatirdṛṣṭā, tasmājjātiḥ pṛthaktataḥ ||
rucakādiṣu sāmānyaṃ rucakatvādyudāhṛtam | bhinneṣu caiṣu sāmānyaṃ suvarṇatvaṃ pratīyate ||
vardhamānakabhaṅge ca rucakaḥ kriyate yadā | tadā pūrvārthinaḥ śokaḥ prītiścāpyuttarārthinaḥ ||
hemārthinastu mādhyasthaṃ tasmādvastu trayātmakam | notpādasthitibhaṅgānāmabhāve syānmatitrayam ||
na nāśena vinā śoko notpādena vinā sukham | sthityā vinā na mādhyasthyam, tena sāmānyanityatā ||
mudgamāṣatilādau ca yatra bhedo na lakṣyate | tatraikabuddhinirgrāhyā jātirindriyagocaraḥ ||
ārāddṛṣṭe ca puruṣe sandeho brāhmaṇādiṣu | na syādyadi na gṛhyeta sāmānyaṃ cakṣurādinā ||
tasyopalakṣaṇaṃ cāpi kva citkena cidiṣyate | rūpādīnāṃ viśeṣeṇa deśakālādyapekṣayā ||
suvarṇaṃ bhidyate rūpāttāmratvāderasaṃśayam | tailādghṛtaṃ vilīnaṃ ca gandhena ca rasena ca ||
bhasmapracchādito vahniḥ sparśanenopalabhyate | aśvatvādau ca dūrasthe niścayo jāyate svanaiḥ ||
saṃsthānena ghaṭatvādi brāhmaṇatvādi yonitaḥ | kva cidācārataścāpi samyagrājānupālitāt ||
pratyekasamavetatvaṃ dṛṣṭatvānna virotsyate | tathā satyapi nānātvaṃ naikabuddherbhaviṣyati ||
na hi sambandhibhedena svarūpaikatvabādhanam | vibhutvāvayavābhāvau pratipādyau ca śabdavat ||
yathā ca vyatirekaiva dṛśyamānā punaḥ punaḥ | kālabhede 'pyabhinnaiva jātirbhinnāśrayā satī ||
kārtsyāvayavaśo vṛttiḥ praṣṭuṃ jātau na yujyate | na hi bhedavinirmukte kārtsnyabhāgavikalpanam ||
tasmādvyaktiṣu jātīnāṃ vṛttirastīti gamyate | viśeṣāvasarābhāvāttanmātraivāvatiṣṭhate ||
yā cāvayavaśo vṛttiḥ sraksūtrādiṣu dṛśyate | bhūtakaṇṭhaguṇādeśca pratipiṇḍaṃ samāptitaḥ ||
tatrāvayavayogitvamavibhutvaṃca kāraṇam | ākṛtestadabhāvena na prasaktamado dvayam ||
na ca dvaividhyameveti vṛtterasti niyāmakam | trividhāpi hi dṛṣṭatvātsambhaveddvividhā yathā ||
itaratra na dṛṣṭaṃ cetsragādiṣvapi tatsamam | naiva hyanyonyatulyatvaṃ tayornāpyanayā saha ||
na hyanyasminnadṛṣṭatvādvahnerauṣṇyaṃ praṇaśyati | na cānumānagamyeyaṃ vāñchedyena nidarśanam ||
svarūpataśca dṛṣṭāyā vṛtterna pararūpataḥ | nirākriyopapadyeta tadviśeṣamapaśyatām ||
aṅgāṅgāsambhavāccāpi yā pradhānanirākriyā | sā 'yuktaiva, anumānena pratyakṣajñānabādhanāt ||
tasmādasambhavo yasya tanmātrasyaiva bādhanam | yuktaṃ na tāvatānyo 'pi sambhavanbādhamarhati ||
tena vaiśeṣikoktāpi jātiḥ sarvagatā satī | vyajyate yatra piṇḍena varṇavattatra gṛhyate ||
tasmātpiṇḍeṣu gobuddhirekagotvanibandhanā | gavābhāsaikarūpyābhāmekagopiṇḍabuddhivat ||
na śābaleyādgobuddhistato 'nyālambanāpi vā | tadabhāve 'pi sadbhāvādghaṭe pārthivabuddhivat ||
pratyekasamavetārthaviṣayā vāpi gomatiḥ | pratyekaṃ kṛtsnabuddhitvātpratyekavyaktibuddhivat ||
pratyekasamavetāpi jātirekaikabuddhitaḥ | nañyukteṣvapi vākyeṣu brahmaṇādinivartanam ||
na ca sādṛśyaviṣayā godhīstādrūpyajanmataḥ | prāmāṇye sati yadvaddhi pratyabhijñaikavastuni ||
naikarūpamatirgotve mithyā vaktuṃ ca śakyate | nātra kāraṇadoṣo 'sti bādhakapratyayo 'pi vā ||
yadā vyaktyatirekeṇa grāhyatvādanyatākṛteḥ | vanavannāstyanaikāntāttatrāsambaddhatā katham ||
sādhanaṃ cenmayocyeta yujyeta vyabhicāritā | dūṣaṇatvadhiyā tvetadasambaddhatvamucyate ||
nāstitvahetoruktaiṣā pratyakṣeṇa viruddhatā | parasya sādhanaṃ hyatra yattatpūrvamudāhṛtam ||
pratyakṣābhāsatā cātra naivāsti vanabuddhivat | kasya cinna hi mithyātvātsarvaṃ mithyetyasaṅgatiḥ ||
yathā vanādibuddhīnāṃ mithyātvānna rasādidhīḥ | mithyaivaṃ jātibuddhiḥ syādviśeṣo vābhidhīyatām ||
vṛkṣebhyo vyatirekeṇa vane yaikamatirbhavet | dūratvadoṣāttatra syādākṛtau tu na vidyate ||
sannikṛṣṭasya vṛkṣeṣu buddhyekatvaṃ nivartate | kena cittu prakāreṇa jātibuddhirna naśyati ||
yaikatvadhīrvinā śabdātsaivaṃ tāvannirākṛtā | vanaśabdānuraktā tu madhyasthasyāpi jāyate ||
mithyātvakalpanā tvasyāḥ pratyakṣāderasambhavāt | jātiḥ sarvapramāṇaistu tadrūpaivāvagamyate ||
pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭe ca padamarthe prayujyate | tasmāddṛṣṭe prayuktasya mithyātvaṃ syādvanādiṣu ||
ke cinnityaṃ vanaikatvaṃ śabdagamyaṃ samāśritāḥ | anyaiḥ saṅgatyabhāve 'pi satyaṃ tatsyādrasādivat ||
mithyātvaṃ yadasaṅgatyā tadajñāne prasajyate | jñāyamānasya doṣastu na tu kaścidasaṅgateḥ ||
pramāṇāntaragamye 'rthe padaṃ nityaṃ prayujyate | dharmo 'yaṃ na ca sarveṣāṃ padānāmabhyupeyate ||
astyeva saṅgatiścātra vṛkṣā hi bahavo vanam | te pramāṇāntarājjñātāḥ, saṃkhyā caiṣānyavastuni ||
nānekasyaikaśabdyaṃ ced, ekaśeṣavadiṣyatām | tatra saṃkhyāvivṛddhiśced, astu tanmātravarjanam ||
tasmātsāmānyadṛṣṭena siddhaikatvasya saṅgatiḥ | tenānyānavagamyāpi saṃkhyā syātsūryayānavat ||
ke cidbahutvasāmānyamāhurvṛkṣasthitaṃ vanam | tatra caikatvamastyeva, vanatvaṃ vāpi vidyate ||
vināpyekāśrayatvena yathaivāvayavo tathā | asaṃyuktairabhivyaktirdṛṣṭatvānna virotsyate ||
anyatrāpi ca tadbuddheḥ sāmānyaṃ tadbhaviṣyati | yathā ca bhramaṇatvādibhaṅgiṣvavayaveṣvapi ||
vyaktaṃ nānāśrayatve 'pi gṛhyate vanatā tathā | yadvaikakāryahetutvādekagośabdavadvanam ||
nityaṃ ye vyastavijñātā vṛkṣā neṣṭā hi te vanam | yadvā lakṣaṇayaikatvaṃ deśakālakriyādibhiḥ ||
dravyaikatvādvināpīṣṭaṃ paṅktiyūthavanādiṣu | vṛkṣāṇāṃ samudāye ca vanadhīrjāyate yathā ||
naivaṃ gosamudāye 'pi gotvadhīrupajāyate | yādṛśī vṛkṣadhīstatra gotvadhīrapi tādṛśī ||
vanavannāpṛthaksiddheḥ samudāyatvakalpanā | na ca sāsnādisaṅghātastadbuddhyālambanaṃ bhavet ||
kṣīṇeṣu piṇḍabuddhyaiṣu tatsāmānye hi gotvadhīḥ | tenāvayavyabhāve 'pi sāmānyaṃ vyatiricyate ||
pūrvoktādeva tu nyāyātsidhyedatrāvayavyapi | tasyāpyatyantabhinnatvaṃ na syādavayavaiḥ saha ||
vyaktibhyo jātivaccaiṣa na niṣkṛṣṭaḥ pratīyate | kaiścidavyatiriktatvaṃ kaiścicca vyatiriktatā ||
dūṣitā sādhitā vāpi na ca tatra balābalam | kadā cinniścitaṃ kaiścittasmānmadhyasthatā varam ||
tato 'nyānanyate nasya sto na staśceti kīrttyate | tasmāccitravadevāsya mṛṣā syādekarūpatā ||
vastvanekatvavādācca na sandindhāpramāṇatā | jñānaṃ sandihyate yatra tatra na syātpramāṇatā ||
ihānaikāntikaṃ vastvityevaṃ jñānaṃ suniścitam | niṣkṛṣyāvayavānbuddhyā yāvayavyapratītatā ||
buddhisthatvādvināśasya saulūkyasyāpi yujyate | vṛttiścāvayaveṣvasya vyāsajyaiva pratīyate ||
tataḥ kārtsnyādisampraśnaḥ pratyākhyeyo 'tra jātivat | sāsnādiguṇahetuścennānyasmingotvadhīrbhavet ||
bhinna eva hi sāsnādiḥ piṇḍātpiṇḍāntareyataḥ | na cāvayavasāmānyaṃ pareṣāmupapadyate ||
tasmātsāsnādito 'nyena gotvadhīrupajanyate | vanāntareṣa yā buddhirvanamityupajāyate ||
tasyāstadeva vṛkṣatvaṃ grāhyaṃ bahvāśrayaṃ viduḥ | ekatve 'pyākṛteryadvadbahutvaṃ vyaktyapekṣayā ||
bahutve hi tathā vyakterekatvaṃ jātyapekṣayā | ekānekābhidhāne ca śabdā niyataśaktayaḥ ||
ke cidvyaktiṃ tvasaṃkhyākāṃ gamayantyambarādiṣu | eko vrīhiḥ suniṣpannaḥ iti jātiṃ svasaṃkhyayā ||
patnīsannahanādau tu vyaktimākṛtisaṃkhyayā | kapiñjalādijātestu pratītirvyaktisaṃkhyayā ||
vyaktijātī vadantyanye dravyāvayavasaṃkhyayā | asmāniti yathaikasmin pāśānaditirityapi ||
tatra vrīhyādiśabdānāṃ saṃkhyāyogo yathāruci | vanadārādiśabdāstu pravartante vyavasthayā ||
jaṅgame sthāvare cārthe yathā yūthavanādayaḥ | tatra vyaktau ca jātau ca dārādiścetprayujyate ||
vyakteravayavānāṃ ca saṃkhyāmādāya vartate | vanaśabdaḥ punarvyaktīrjātisaṃkhyāviśeṣitāḥ ||
bahvīrāhātha vā jātiṃ bahuvyaktisamāśrayām | evaṃ paṅktyādiśabdānāṃ saṃyogādi viśeṣaṇam ||
sarveṣāṃ kiñcidastīti na nirālambanaikadhīḥ | tulyaṃ pratyakṣayā ''kṛtyā vane yattadasadyadi ||
vṛkṣāstatra tayā tulyā iti śūnyatvavāditā | pratyakṣābhāsagamyatvādvṛkṣebhyo 'nyattu tadvanam ||
nā''kṛtyā saha tasyāsti sparddhā pratyakṣagamyayā | athā''kṛtyā vanaṃ tulyaṃ sadbhāvena prasajyate | jātipakṣavimokena vanasiddhāntadūṣaṇam ||
iti nigaditametallokasiddhaiḥ padārthairvyavahṛtiriha śāstre na svatantrābhyupetaiḥ | bhavati ca janadṛṣṭyā jātipaṅktyādibhedo yadi tu na ghaṭate 'sau naiva bādho 'sti kaścit ||

§ 5,16 sambandhākṣepaparihāra sap

bhavetāṃ nāma śabdārthau yāvetāvuditau tvayā | yadarthastu prayāso 'yaṃ sa sambandho nirūpyatām ||
pūrvamevopadiṣṭaḥ san sambandhaḥ kin tu pṛcchyate | svarūpākathanāccaitaduttaraṃ nopapadyate ||
kimauṣadhaṃ jvarasyeti pṛṣṭo yadi vadedidam | yenāsau naśyatītyevaṃ kiṃ tena kathitaṃ bhavet ||
tatra ke cidvadantyeva pūrvatrāparitoṣataḥ | praśnaḥ punarupakrāntaḥ sambandhāntaramicchatā ||
yaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhaḥ sa pratītyuttaro yataḥ | sā cānyapūrvikā tasmānnāsya pratyāyanāṅgatā ||
ajānāno 'pi saṃjñātvaṃ sambandhāntaradarśanāt | buddhyate 'rthaṃ tataḥ paścātkaścitsaṃjñeti manyate ||
tamevānyo 'vinābhāvamatra sambandhamicchati | na hi tasmādvinā śabde jñāte syādarthabodhanam ||
tattvayuktam, na bhāṣye 'sti tādṛksambandhakīrtanam | yadi hyetāvatocyeta kiṃ nānuktaḥ pratīyate ||
prayuktaścāvinābhāvasaṃjñā lokāttu gamyate | saṃjñetyagamyamāne 'pi gamakatvaṃ pratīyate ||
tasmātsa eva śabdārthacintāvyavahito 'dhunā | nityānityavicārārthaṃ sambandhaḥ smāryate punaḥ ||
yacchabde jñāta ityevaṃ śaktirevātra kīrtyate | kartṛtvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ vā yattasyārthābhidhāṃ prati ||
svato naivāsti śaktatvaṃ vācyāvācakayormithaḥ | pratītiḥ samayātpuṃsāṃ bhavedakṣinikocavat ||
samayaḥ pratimartyaṃ yā pratyuccāraṇameva vā | kriyate jagadādau vā sakṛdekena kena cit ||
pratyekaṃ vāpi sambandho bhidyetaiko 'tha vā bhavet | ekatve kṛtako na syād, bhinnaścedbhedadhīrbhavet ||
bhinnatve pratisambandhaṃ śaktiḥ kalpyābhidhā prati | ekasminjñātaśaktau vā nānyenārthamatirbhavet ||
atha yo yasya puṃsaḥ syātsa tena pratipadyate | yasyānekena sambandhaḥ kṛtastasya kathaṃ bhavet ||
ekārthānāṃ vikalpaścet, netarātyantabādhanāt | samuccayo 'pi naiteṣāṃ vyavahāre 'vagamyate ||
kiñcidevaikamādāya vyavahāro hi dṛśyate | bahubhiḥ kṛtasambandhe na caiko gamako bhavet ||
śabdārthayorabhede 'pi pumbahutve 'pi kartari | nāyaṃ veti matirdṛṣṭā vikalpo 'to na yujyate ||
gośabde sakṛdukte ca bhinneṣu pratipattṛṣu | vikalpyamāne sambandhe kaścidbudhyeta netare ||
samuccayo nṛbhedāccet, na, vaktraikyādasambhavāt | vaktṛśrotṛdhiyorbhedādvyavahāraśca duṣyati ||
vakturanyo hi sambandho buddhau śrotustathāparaḥ | śrotuḥ kartuṃ ca sambandhaṃ vaktā kaṃ pratipadyatām ||
pūrvadṛṣṭo hi yastena śroturnaiva karoti tam | yaṃ karoti navaṃ so 'pi na dṛṣṭaḥ pratipādakaḥ ||
sarvathā śrotṛsiddhiśced, asiddhaṃ netaro vadet | ghaṭādāvapi tulyaṃ cet, na, sāmānyaprasiddhitaḥ ||
yadyapi jñātasāmarthyā vyaktiḥ kartuṃ na śakyate | kriyate yā na tasyāśca śaktiḥ kārye 'vadhāritā ||
tathāpyākṛtitaḥ siddhā śaktirutpādanādiṣu | tasyā na cādimattāsti, sambandhastvādimāṃstava ||
yadi tatrāpi sāmānyaṃ nityamabhyupagamyate | tathāpyasmanmataṃ siddham, na tu dvyākārasambhavaḥ ||
śaktireva hi sambandho bhedaścāsyā na vidyate | sā hi kāryānumeyatvāttadbhedamanuvartate ||
anyathānupapattyā ca śaktisadbhāvakalpanam | na caikayaiva siddhe 'rthe bahvīnāṃ kalpaneṣyate ||
sambandhākhyānakāle ca gośabdādāvudīrite | ke citsambandhabuddhyārthaṃ buddhyante nāpare tathā ||
tatra sambandhanāstitve sarvo 'rthaṃ nāvadhārayet | astitve sarvabodhaścet, na kaiścidanupagrahāt ||
jñāpakatvāddhi sambandhaḥ svātmajñānamapekṣate | tenāsau vidyamāno 'pi nāgṛhītaḥ prakāśakaḥ ||
vidyamānasya cārthasya dṛṣṭamagrahaṇaṃ kva cit | na tvatyantāsato 'stitvaṃ kāṃścitpratyupapadyate ||
viruddhau sadasadbhāvau na syātāmekavastuni | nanu tulyaṃ virodhitvaṃ jñātājñātatvayorapi ||
jñānaṃ hi puruṣādhāraṃ tadbhedānna virotsyate | puruṣāntarasaṃsthaṃ ca nājñānaṃ tena bādhyate ||
sambandhādhāratāyāṃ ca virodhaḥ sadasattvayoḥ | pratyuktatvācca bhedasya tadvaśānnāvirodhitā ||
andhānandhasamīpasthaḥ śuklo 'ndhairnāvagamyate | gamyate cetaraistasya sadasattvena tāvatā ||
śaktyaśaktyornarāṇāṃ tu bhedāttatrāvirodhitā | na hyanyo darśanasyāsti sambandhāddheturatra hi ||
evamevendriyaistulyaṃ vyavahāropalambhanam | yeṣāṃ syātte 'vabhotsyante tato 'rthaṃ netare 'ndhavat ||
ādhānavatsakṛścaitattantreṇopakariṣyati | smaraṇaṃ bhetsyate cāsya vahnipraṇayanādivat ||
sarveṣāmanabhijñānāṃ pūrvapūrvaprasiddhitaḥ | siddhaḥ sambandha ityevaṃ sambandhādirna vidyate ||
pratyuccāraṇanirvṛttirbhāṣya eva nirākṛtā | sargādau ca kriyā nāsti, tādṛkkālo hi neṣyate ||
yadi tvādau jagatsṛṣṭvā dharmādharmau sasādhanau | yathā śabdārthasambandhānvedān kaścitpravartayet ||
jagaddhitāya vedasya tathā kiñcinna duṣyati | sarvajñavattu dussādhamityatraitanna saṃśritam ||
yadā sarvamidaṃ nāsītkvāvasthā tatra gamyatām | prajāpateḥ kva vā sthānaṃ kiṃ rūpaṃ ca pratīyatām ||
jñātā ca kastadā tasya yo janānbodhayiṣyati | upalabdhervinā caitatkathamadhyavasīyatām ||
pravṛttiḥ kathamādyā ca jagataḥ sampratīyate | śarīrādervinā cāsya kathamicchāpi sarjane ||
śarīrādyatha tasya syāt, tasyotpattirna tatkṛtā | tadvadanyaprasaṅgo 'pi, nityaṃ yadi tadiṣyate ||
pṛthivyādāvanutpanne kimmayaṃ tatpunarbhavet | prāṇināṃ prāyaduḥkhā ca sisṛkṣāsya na yujyate ||
sādhanaṃ cāsya dharmādi tadā kiñcanna vidyate | na ca nissādhanaḥ kartā kaścitsṛjati kiñcana ||
nādhāreṇa vinā sṛṣṭirūrṇanābherapīṣyate | prāṇināṃ bhakṣaṇāccāpi tasya lālā pravarttate ||
abhāvāccānukampyānāṃ nānukampāsya jāyate | sṛjecca śubhamevaikamanukampāprayojitaḥ ||
athāśubhādvinā sṛṣṭiḥ sthitirvā nopapadyate | ātmādhīnābhyupāye hi bhavetkiṃ nāma dṛṣkaram ||
tathā cāpekṣamāṇasya svātantryaṃ pratihanyate | jagaccāsṛjatastasya kiṃ nāmeṣṭaṃ na sidhyati ||
prayojanamanuddiśya na mando 'pi pravartate | evameva pravṛttiśceccaitanyenāsya kiṃ bhavet ||
krīḍārthāyāṃ pravṛttau ca vihanyeta kṛtārthatā | bahuvyāpāratāyāṃ ca kleśo bahutaro bhavet ||
saṃhārecchāpi caitasya bhavedapratyayātpunaḥ | na cakaiścidasau jñātuṃ kādā cidapi śakyate ||
svarūpeṇopalabdhe 'pi sraṣṭṛtvaṃ nāvagamyate | sṛṣṭyādyāḥ praṇino ye ca budhyantāṃ kiṃ nu te tadā ||
kuto vayamihotpannāḥ iti tāvanna jānate | prāgavasthāṃ ca jagataḥ sraṣṭṛtvaṃ ca prajāpateḥ ||
na ca tadvacanenaiṣāṃ pratipattiḥ suniścitā | asṛṣṭvāpi hyasau brūyādātmaiśvaryaprakāśanāt ||
evaṃ vedo 'pi tatpūrvastatsadbhāvādibodhane | sāśaṅko na pramāṇaṃ syāt, nityasya vyāpṛtiḥ kutaḥ ||
yadi prāgapyasau tasmādarthādāsīnna tena saḥ | sambaddha iti tasyānyastadartho 'nyaprarocanā ||
stutivākyakṛtaścaiṣa janānāṃ mativibhramaḥ | paurvāparyāparāmṛṣṭaḥ śabdo 'nyāṃ kurute matim ||
upākhyānādirūpeṇa vṛttirvedavadeva naḥ | dharmādau bhāratādīnāṃ bhrāntistebhyo 'pyato bhavet ||
ākhyānānupayogitvātteṣu sarveṣu vidyate | stutinindāśrayaḥ kaścidvedastaccodito 'pi vā ||
vedasyādipravṛttau ca nākṛtatvamatirbhavet | pralayeṣu sthitiścāsya sāśaṅkā syātprajāpatau ||
kartṛsargavināśānāmathānāditvakalpanā | saivaṃ yuktāyathedānīṃ bhūtānāṃ dṛśyate kramāt ||
pralaye 'pi pramāṇaṃ naḥ sarvocchedātmake na hi | na ca prayojanaṃ tena syātprajāpatikarmaṇā ||
na ca karmavatāṃ yuktā sthitistadbhogavarjitā | karmāntaraniruddhaṃ hi phalaṃ na syātkriyāntarāt ||
sarveṣāṃ tu phalāpetaṃ na sthānamupapadyate | na cāpyanupabhogo 'sau kasya citkarmaṇaḥ phalam ||
aśeṣakarmanāśe vā punaḥ sṛṣṭirna yujyate | karmāṇāṃ vāpyabhivyaktau kiṃ nimittaṃ tadā bhavet ||
īśvarecchā yadīṣyeta, saiva syāllokakāraṇam | īśvarecchāvaśitve hi niṣphalā karmakalpanā ||
na cānimittayā yuktamutpattuṃ hīśvarecchayā | yadvā tasyā nimittaṃ yattadbhūtānāṃ bhaviṣyati ||
sanniveśaviśiṣṭānāmutpattiṃ yo gṛhādivat | sādhayeccetanādhiṣṭhāṃ dehānāṃ tasya cottaram ||
kasya ciddhetumātratvaṃ yadyadhiṣṭhātṛteṣyate | karmabhiḥ sarvajīvānāṃ tatsiddheḥ siddhasādhanam ||
icchāpūrvakapakṣe 'pi, tatpūrvatvena karmaṇām | icchānantarasiddhistu dṛṣṭānte 'pi na vidyate ||
anekāntaśca hetuste taccharīrādinā bhavet | utpattimāṃśca taddeho dehatvādasmadādivat ||
atha tasyāpyadhiṣṭhānaṃ tenaivetyavipakṣatā | aśarīro hyadhiṣṭhātā nātmā muktātmavadbhavet ||
kumbhakārādyadhiṣṭhānaṃ ghaṭādau yadi ceṣyate | neśvarādhiṣṭhitatvaṃ syād, asti cetsādhyahīnatā ||
yathāsiddhe ca dṛṣṭānte bhaveddhetorviruddhatā | anīśvaravināśyādikartṛmattvaṃ prasajyate ||
kulālavacca naitasya vyāpāro yadi kalpate | acetanaḥ kathaṃ bhāvastadicchāmanurudhyate ||
tasmānna paramāṇvāderārambhaḥ syāttadicchayā | puruṣasya ca śuddhasya nāśuddhā vikṛtirbhavet ||
svādhīnatvācca dharmādestena kleśo na yujyate | tadvaśena pravṛttau vā vyatirekaḥ prasajyate ||
svayaṃ ca śuddharūpatvādasattvāccānyavastunaḥ | svapnādivadavidyāyāḥ pravṛttistasya kiṃ kṛtā ||
anyenopaplave 'bhīṣṭe dvaitavādaḥ prasajyate | svābhāvikīmavidyāṃ tu nocchettuṃ kaścidarhati ||
vilakṣaṇopapāte hi naśyetsvābhāvikī kva cit | na tvekātmābhyupāyānāṃ heturasti vilakṣaṇaḥ ||
pumānakartā yeṣāṃ tu teṣāmapi guṇaiḥ kriyā | kathamādau bhavet, tatra karma tāvanna vidyate ||
mithyājñānaṃ na trāsti rāgadveṣādayo 'pi vā | manovṛttirhi sarveṣāṃ na cotpannaṃ tadā manaḥ ||
karmaṇāṃ śaktyavasthānāṃ yairuktā bandhahetutā | sā na yuktā na kāryaṃ hi śaktisthātkāraṇādbhavet ||
dadhiśaktirna hi kṣīre dādhikārambhamarhati | dadhyārambhasya sā hetustato 'nyā dādhikasya tu ||
kāraṇāc chaktyavasthācca yadi kāryaṃ prajāyate | bandhaḥ punaḥ prasajyeta phale datte 'pi karmaṇā ||
śaktyavasthatvameveṣṭaṃ vināśe 'pi hi karmaṇām | prākcāpi śaktisadbhāvādanuṣṭhānaṃ vṛthā bhavet ||
śaktyavasthaṃ ca rāgādi kiṃ neṣṭaṃ bandhakāraṇam | karmādattaphalatvāccet, nāvyaktimapi tadvrajet ||
tacchaktyapratiyogitvānna jñānaṃ mokṣakāraṇam | karmaśaktyā na hi jñānaṃ virodhamupagacchati ||
yadyapyajñānajanyatvaṃ karmaṇāmavagamyate | rāgādivattathāpyeṣāṃ na jñānena nirākriyā ||
karmakṣayo hi vijñānādityetaccāpramāṇavat | phalasyālpasya vā dānaṃ rājaputrāparādhavat ||
adyatve 'pi hi śaktisthaṃ yadi syātkarmakāraṇam | tataḥ pradhānakāle 'pi yujyate kāraṇābhidhā ||
manovṛttiridānīṃ tu heturnāsti ca sā tadā | manasāṃ saṅkarāccāpi tadā syātkarmasaṅkaraḥ ||
gasmānnaiṣo 'dhikārākhyo bandhahetuḥ prakalpate | yogyatve 'pyadhikārākhye viprayogo na yujyate ||
caitanyaṃ yogyatā puṃsaḥ prakṛtestadanātmatā | bhoktṛbhogyatvayoste ca na tābhyāmapagacchataḥ ||
utpattau karmaṇāṃ ceṣṭamajñānaṃ kāraṇaṃ yadi | tannāśātsyādanutpattisteṣāṃ na phalavarjanam ||
jñānaṃ mokṣanimittaṃ ca gamyate nendriyādinā | na ca sāṅkhyādivijñānānmokṣo vedena codyate ||
ātmā jñātavya ityetanmokṣārthaṃ na ca coditam | karmapravṛttihetutvamātmajñānasya lakṣyate ||
vijñāte cāsya pārārthye yāpi nāma phalaśrutiḥ | sārthavādo bhavedeva na svargādeḥ phalāntaram ||
sukhopabhogarūpaśca yadi mokṣaḥ prakalpyate | svarga eva bhavedeṣa paryāyeṇa, kṣayo ca saḥ ||
na hi kāraṇavatkiñcidakṣayitvena gamyate | tasmātkarmakṣayādeva hetvabhāve na mucyate ||
na hyabhāvātmakaṃ muktvā mokṣanityatvakāraṇam | na ca kriyāyāḥ kasyāścidabhāvaḥ phalamiṣyate ||
tatra jñātātmatattvānāṃ bhogātpūrvakriyākṣaye | uttarapracayāsattvāddeho notpadyate punaḥ ||
karmajanyopabhogārthaṃ śarīraṃ na pravartate | tadabhāve na kaściddhi hetustatrāvatiṣṭhate ||
mokṣārthī na pravarteta tatra kāmyaniṣiddhayoḥ | nityanaimittike kuryātpratyavāyajihāsayā ||
prārthyamānaṃ phalaṃ jñātaṃ na cānicchorbhaviṣyati | ātmajñe caitadastīti tajjñānamupayujyate ||
sargapralayavijñānaṃ samastajagadāśrayam | svaśarīravidāṃ puṃsāṃ nādhikyenopayujyate ||
tasmādadyavadevātra sargapralayakalpanā | samastakṣayajanmabhyāṃ na sidhyatyapramāṇikā ||
sarvajñavanniṣedhyā ca sraṣṭuḥ sadbhāvakalpanā | na ca dharmādṛte tasya bhavellokādviśiṣṭhatā ||
na cānanuṣṭhito dharmo nānuṣṭhānamṛte mateḥ | na ca vedādṛte sā syādvedo na ca padādibhiḥ ||
tasmātprāgapi sarve 'mī sraṣṭurāsan padādayaḥ | syāttatpūrvakatā cāsya caitanyādasmadādivat ||
evaṃ ye yuktibhiḥ prāhusteṣāṃ durlabhamuttaram | aneṣyo vyavahāro 'yamanādirvedavādibhiḥ ||
pratyakṣādāvupakṣīṇe yo 'numānena ḍitthavat | sambandhitvānniyoktāraṃ gavādāvapi kalpayet ||
gavādiśabdasambandhaṃ sarvo 'nyasmātprapadyate | madvattadvyavahāritvāttasyaitatpratisādhanam ||
devadattādiśabde 'pi prasaktaivamanāditā | sambandhasya, balīyastvāddṛṣṭabādhānnivartate ||
tatrāpi śaktinityatvam, niyogasya tvanityatā | tadgatāccāpyanityatvāc chaktau bhrāntiḥ pravartate ||
gavādiṣu tu na bhrāntirniyogānāditā yataḥ | yo yo gṛhītaḥ sarvasmātpūrvaṃ sambandhadarśanāt ||
siddhaḥ sambandha ityevaṃ sambandhādirna vidyate | yadā cāptapraṇītatvāc chabdo 'rthaṃ pratipādayet ||
na svaśaktyā tadāptatvaṃ mitau na smaryate katham | yathā bauddhādayo yāvadbuddhādyuktaṃ na jānate ||
na tāvatpratipadyante bodhe vākyena satyapi | samaye kathyamāne 'nyairasmaranto 'pi pāṇinim ||
ādaicaḥ pratipadyante vṛddhiṃ kartuṃ smṛtirvṛthā | sūtrasthaḥ pāṇinistatra svasaṃjñāṃ pratipādayet ||
gauḥ sāsnādimatītyevaṃ vākyaṃ tvatra na vidyate | asambandhācca sarveṣāmevaṃ kartumasambhavaḥ ||
tasmānna pratipattiḥ syātkathañcitkartṛvarjitā | dṛṣārthavyavahāratvādvṛddhyādau sambhavedapi ||
dharmāya niyamo 'trāpi na vinā pāṇinerbhavet | ākārānugamo yo hi vṛddhyā syādāśvalāyane ||
nāsāvapāṇinīyatve sādhurityavagamyate | dṛṣṭe bhavatu mā vā bhūtkartṛsampratipannatā ||
vaidido vyavahārastu na kartṛsmaraṇādṛte | burgeṣu gavi gośabdaprayogo gamyate katham ||
gatvā cetkena ciddṛṣṭaḥ, sambanddhā kiṃ na gacchati | īśvaratvādgatiścāsya na kva citpratibadhyate ||
bahūnāṃ kāryataścāpi saṅgānaṃ kena vāryate | ekatra kathitaṃ cāpi lokenānyatra nīyate ||
vṛddhyādiva, ato vyākhyā dvitīyaivātra śobhanā | kāṃścitprasiddhasambandhānabhyupetya vadedyadi ||
sambandhakaraṇam, tatra ke siddhā iti durvadam | na tāvadanya evāsan śabdā iti hi yuktimat ||
viśeṣo 'dyatanānāṃ ca gavādīnāṃ na dṛśyate | śabdārthānāditāṃ muktvā sambandhānādikāraṇam ||
na syādanyad, ato vede sambandhādirna vidyate | upāyarahitatvena sambandhakaraṇānumā ||
anākhyānānumānaṃ tu dṛṣṭenaiva viruddhyate | buddhānāṃ dṛśyamānā ca pratipattiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ||
upāya iti taddhānirasiddhāvagatiṃ prati | hastasaṃjñādyupāyo hi siddho nādyakriyāsu naḥ ||
na hyasau jñātasāmarthyo vinānyairvyavahartṛbhiḥ | śabdavṛddhābhidheyāṃśca pratyakṣeṇātra paśyati ||
śrotuśca pratipannatvamanumānena ceṣṭayā | anyathā 'nupapattyā ca buddhyec chaktiṃ dvayāśritām | arthāpattyāvabuddhyante sambandhaṃ tripramāṇakam ||

§ 5,17 citrākṣepaparihāra cap

citrādiniṣphalatve 'pi yaduktaṃ sādhanadvayam | tatra hetorasiddhatvamānantaryaṃ hyacoditam ||
ānantaryaśrutiścātra sāmārthyādapi neṣyate | nāviśeṣā phalotpattiḥ karmaṇā nopapadyate ||
karmaṇāṃ cāpi vaicitryāddeśakālādyapekṣaṇāt | kasya ciccārddhabhuktatvātkarmānyatpratibadhyate ||
tenānantaryaniṣpattiḥ phalasyehāpramāṇikā | pratyakṣādivisaṃvādo na śabde doṣamāsajet ||
ānantaryavisaṃvādo nāviśeṣapravartinīm | codanāṃ bādhituṃ śaktaḥ sphuṭādviṣayabhedataḥ ||
yā tu mardanasādharmyādānantaryā 'numā kṛtā | bādhyate 'nupalabdhyāsau samānaviṣayā yataḥ ||
dṛṣṭārthasyāpi sevāderāyātamapi satphalam | utpadyate cireṇaiva pratibandhena kena cit ||
uptamātre na hi vrīhau phalamutpadyate kva cit | athāṅkuro 'pi tatra syāt, svargo 'pyastīti gamyatām ||
sthūlībhūtaścireṇaiṣa bhogyatvaṃ pratipadyate | sarvasyotpadyamānasya kramaḥ svābhāvikaḥ sthitaḥ ||
anantaraphalatvaṃ tu citrāderyadi sādhyate | tataḥ syātsiddhasādhyatvamanyadā na phalaṃ bhavet ||
vyabhicārācca sevādeḥ paśvādeḥ sādhanāntaram | kimapyadṛṣṭamastyeva tatrānyanniṣpramāṇakam ||
īśvarecchādhikārādiśabdaliṅgādivarjanāt | kṛtaṃ kadā ciccitrādiśabdena tvavagamyate ||
nirnimittā na cotpattiḥ, na hi sarvāpramāṇatā | bodhayanna ca śabdo 'tra prāmāṇyādativarttate ||
yeṣāṃ tviha phalānyeva citrādīnīti kalpanā | nirnimittaṃ phalaṃ teṣāṃ syādihākṛtakarmaṇām ||
citrādīnāṃ phalaṃ tāvatkṣīṇaṃ tatraiva janmani | na ca svargaphalasyeha kaścidaṃśo 'nuvartate ||
naiva hyanyaphalaṃ karma sādhayennaḥ phalāntaram | gautamīye 'pi taccheṣastasmāccitrādyapekṣayā ||
svābhāvikatve siddhe ca karmānantarabhāvyapi | phalaṃ kriyānimittatvaṃ na kathañcitprapadyate ||
tatra mlecchādivatsarve karmākṛtvāpi vaidikam | palaṃ labhanta ityevaṃ naṣṭā vedapramāṇatā ||
anantaraṃ niyogena paśvādi ca bhavedyadi | pratyakṣaphalataiva syāttrivṛtpānavirekavat ||
janmāntarānubhūtaṃ ca na smaryata itīdṛśam | na bhāṣyaṃ na ca sūtraṃ syādaprāpte śāstramarthavat ||
tasmātkālāviśeṣeṇa codanārtho yathā sthitaḥ | sa tathaivānugantavyo nādhiko niṣpramāṇakaḥ ||
sarveṣāṃ karmavaiguṇyātphalābhāvaṃ vadanti ye | ānantaryamupetyaiva te svābhāvikavādinaḥ ||
svargasyāmuṣmikatvaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhādye sthāpayiṣyate | paśvāderniyamābhāvo yogasiddhiritīha tu ||
yadā kadā cidbhavadetadiṣyate phalaṃ hi paśvādi na sāmparāyikam | tathā sthitasyaiva hi tasya sādhanaṃ vidhīyate yo 'pi bhṛśaṃ tvarānvitaḥ ||
sādhāraṇaṃ yattu palaṃ bahūnāṃ svabhāvatastādṛśameva ceṣṭam | sarvasya vā ''sanna tayaiva kāmyaṃ vṛṣṭyādi taccaihikameva yuktam ||
kamipadamaviśiṣṭaṃ yadyapi śrūyate vā bhavati phalaviśeṣī nānyathā kāmyate hi | phalati yadi na sarvaṃ tatkadā cittadaiva dhruvamaparamabhuktaṃ karma śāstrīyamāste ||

§ 5,18 ātmavāda atv

sākṣādyadyapi sambandho nātmano yajñasādhanaiḥ | tathāpi lakṣaṇāvṛttyā śarīradvārako bhavet ||
pratyakṣatvaṃ ca dehasthaṃ bhāktamātmani kalpitam | ātmanaḥ svargayānaṃ vā śarīrasyopacaryyate ||
nairātmyenātra cākṣiptāḥ sarvā eva hi codanāḥ | sādhyasādhanasambandhastadukto na hi siddhyati ||
tā hi kartuḥ phalenāhuḥ sambandhaṃ kvāpi janmani | na ca vijñānamātratve bhoktṛkartṛtvasambhavaḥ ||
śarīravinipātācca paraṃ nānyadyadeṣyate | adattaphalaiṣṭyādau tadā tadvacanaṃ mṛṣā ||
tasmādvedapramāṇārthamātmātra pratipādyate | yadyapi prakṛtaṃ vākyaṃ vyākhyāyetārthavādataḥ ||
śarīrendriyabuddhibhyo vyatiriktatvamātmanaḥ | nityatvaṃ ceṣyate, śeṣaṃ śarīrādi vinaśyate ||
nityaḥ kartṛtvabhoktṛtve pratipanno 'pi sanyadā | na karmaphalasambandhaṃ bhogakāle 'vabudhyate ||
mayā yattu kṛtaṃ karma tasyedaṃ bhujyate phalam | śubhāśubhaṃ mayaiveti tadā ko 'sya raso bhavet ||
aparāmṛśyamāne hi svakarmapratyaye phale | na viśeṣo bhavetkaścitsvaparātmopabhogayoḥ ||
kurvannapyaśubhaṃ karma tenaivaṃ cintayennaraḥ | na smariṣyāmi bhoge 'hamiti naitadvivarjayet ||
tatra nityatvapakṣe 'pi kṛtanāśākṛtāgamau | phalatastulyarūpau cedvṛthā tatpratipādanam ||
naiṣa doṣaḥ, na bhoge hi smṛtirna upayujyate | na pravṛttirnivṛttirvā bhogakāle smṛterbhavet ||
tadaṅgaṃ yaḥ parāmarśastadastitvaṃ ca mṛgyate | prākpravṛttestu so 'styeva viduṣāṃ śāstrataḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
paścādapi ca śāstrajñā vimṛśantyeva ke cana | teṣāmevādhikāraśca mā bhūdaviduṣāṃ tu saḥ ||
parāmarśaśca sarvatra nāsti sarvapramāṇakaḥ | na cānyenāparāmṛṣṭe syādanyasyāpramāṇatā ||
nāvabudhyeta yastvevaṃ mamāsmātkarmaṇaḥ phalam | bhaviṣyatītyavidvattvāddaivādevātra na kriyā ||
aparāmṛśyamāne 'pi svāpakāle sukhāśraye | sambhoge mṛduśayyādau prākpravṛttiśca dṛśyate ||
bhogakāle 'nusandadhyātphalaṃ yadi tu kaścana | rathādikarmavadyāge śāstraṃ syādaprakalpakam ||
tava nityavibhutvābhyāmātmāno niṣkriyā yadi | sukhaduḥkhāvikāryāśca kīdṛśo kartṛbhoktṛtā ||
atha kartṛtvavelāyāṃ duḥkhādeścāpi janmani | prāgrūpādanyathātvaṃ syānnityatāsya virudhyate ||
nānityaśabdavācyatvamātmano vinivāryate | vikriyāmātravācitve na hyucchedo 'sya tāvatā ||
syātāmatyantanāśe 'sya kṛtanāśākṛtāgamau | na tvavasthāntaraprāptau loke bālayuvādivat ||
avasthāntarabhāvyetatphalaṃ mama śubhāśubham | iti jñātvānutiṣṭhaṃśca vijahacceṣṭate janaḥ ||
anavasthāntaraprāptirdṛśyate na ca kasya cit | anucchedāttu nānyatvaṃ bhokturloko 'vagacchati ||
sukhaduḥkhādyavasthāśca gacchannapi naro mama | caitanyadravyasattādirūpaṃ naiva vimuñcati ||
duḥkhinaḥ sukhyavasthāyāṃ naśyeyuḥ sarva eva te | duḥkhitvaṃ cānuvarteta vināśe vikriyātmake ||
tasmādubhayahānena vyāvṛttyanugamātmakaḥ | puruṣo 'bhyupagantavyaḥ kuṇḍalādiṣu svarṇavat ||
na ca kartṛtvabhoktṛtve puṃso 'vasthāsamāśrite | tenāvasthāvatastattvātkarttaivāpnoti tatphalam ||
na cāvasthāntarotpāde pūrvātyantaṃ vinaśyati | uttarānuguṇatvāttu sāmānyātmani līyate ||
svarūpeṇa hyavasthānāmanyonyasya virodhitā | aviruddhastu sarvāsu sāmānyātmā pravartate ||
nairātmyavādapakṣe tu pūrvamevāvabudhyate | madvināśātphalaṃ nasyānmatto 'nyasyātha vā bhavet ||
iti naiva pravṛttiḥ syānna ca vedapramāṇatā | janmānare 'bhyupete 'pi jñānamātrātmavādinām ||
jñānānāṃ kṣaṇikatvāddhi kartṛbhoktranyatā bhavet | niṣkriyatvāvibhutvābhyāṃ na ca dehāntarāśritiḥ ||
kartā ya eva santāno nanu bhoktā sa eva naḥ | vijñānakṣaṇabhedastu tvadavasthāntaraiḥ samaḥ ||
kartṛtvameva duḥsādhaṃ dīrghakāleṣu karmasu | satsu jñānasahastreṣu kulakalpopamaṃ hi tat ||
vyatirikto hi santāno yadi nābhyupagamyate | santānināmanityatvātkartā kaścinna labhyate ||
bhokturatyantabhedācca prasajyetākṛtāgamaḥ | kṛtanāśaṃ tu na brūmaḥ kṛtaṃ naiva hi kena cit ||
santānānanyatāyāṃ tu vācoyuktyantareṇa te | tatra coktam, na cāvastu santānaḥ kartṛtāṃ vrajet ||
santānakṣaṇikatve ca tadeva, akṣaṇikastvatha | siddhāntahāniḥ, evaṃ ca so 'pi dravyāntaraṃ bhavet ||
ekā cāvyatiriktā ca santānibhyo 'tha santatiḥ | bhedābhedau prasaṅktavyau grāhyagrāhakayoryathā ||
tasmādatyantabhedo vā kathañcidvāpi bhinnatā | santānasyetyayaṃ cātmā syādvaiśeṣikasāṃkhyayoḥ ||
santāno 'yaṃ sa eveti na tvabhedādvinā bhavet | vāyudopādisantāne vāyutvādirna bhidyate ||
jñānatvenāpyabhinnatvaṃ śūnyavāde nirākṛtam | tathaiva karmabhirveṣṭā phalārthaṃ cittavāsanā ||
na cātra vāsanākālaṃ kiñciccittamavasthitam | avastutvācca santānaḥ karmabhirnaiva vāsyate ||
tatpāramparyajāte 'pi bhuñjāne karmaṇaḥ phalam | tādātmyena vinā spaṣṭau kṛtanāśākṛtāgamau ||
santānāntarajebhyaśca yo hetuphalabhāvataḥ | viśeṣaḥ so 'pi dussādhaḥ, parihāro na cānayoḥ ||
tasminnasatyapi brūyāḥ parihāraṃ tvamanyathā | samānapṛthivīvāsajñānatvādyaviśeṣataḥ ||
samāna iti nāpyetadekatvānugamādvinā | tena yaccittajaṃ tasya santāna iti vo mṛṣā ||
na hi yacchabdatacchabdau vartete bhinnavastuni | tenaikātmakataiṣṭavyā tatsantānātmavādibhiḥ ||
nanvanyatvaṃ vidanto 'pi putrādiphalasiddhaye | pravartante yathā tadvajjñānasantānino 'pi naḥ ||
anyatve ca samāne 'pi yathā vaṃśāntarodbhavāḥ | na labhante phalaṃ tadvatsantānāntarajāḥ kṣaṇāḥ ||
na tāvadbuddhiratraivam, api cātmaphalecchayā | putrādibharaṇe vṛttiḥ syāttadapyatra nāsti te ||
phalāntaramanuddiśya na ca putrādi bibhrati | vinaṣṭasya tu nātmīyasantānabharaṇātphalam ||
yastvanenaiva mārgeṇa phalāntaramapīcchati | svasantānyantarairbhogyaṃ tatsantānānyupakārakam ||
anavasthedṛśī tasya svopabhogādṛte bhavet | naiva hyanyo 'pi santānī kaścittasyātmavanmataḥ ||
yāvadyāvacca dūrasthe santānini phalaṃ bhavet | tāvattāvacca tannaśyetsutarāṃ viprakarṣataḥ ||
bharaṇaṃ yadapatyānāṃ tiryagādiṣu dṛśyate | ajñānaṃ śaraṇaṃ tatra prājñānāṃ tu na yujyate ||
dehāntare ca buddhīnāṃ sañcāro nopapadyate | pūrvadehādbahirbhāvo na ca tāsāṃ pratīyate ||
vāyunā preryamāṇaṃ hi jvālādyanyatra sañcaret | buddheḥ kāraṇadeśāttu preraṇaṃ nāsti kena cit ||
amūrtatvātsvayaṃ nāsāvutplutyā 'nyatra gacchati | jīvaddehe 'pi tenāsyā gamanaṃ nopapadyate ||
antarābhavadehastu niṣiddho vindhyavāsinā | tadastitve pramāṇaṃ hi na kiñcidavagamyate ||
sahasā jāyate tacca sahasaiva vinaśyati | sūkṣmarūpādiyuktaṃ cetyutprekṣāmātrameva tat ||
satyapi jñānasañcārastatra syānniṣpramāṇakaḥ | tena cānyaśarīreṣu punarnikṣepakalpanā ||
kalalādiṣu vijñānamastītyetacca sāhasam | asañjātendriyatvāddhi na tatrārtho 'vagamyate ||
na cārthāvagateranyadrūpaṃ jñānasya yujyate | mūrcchādāvapi tenāsya sadbhāvo nopapadyate ||
na cāpi śaktirūpeṇa tadā dhīravatiṣṭhate | nirāśrayatvāc chaktīnāṃ sthitirna hyavakalpate ||
yadi bhūtendriyādhārā jñānaśaktirbhavettataḥ | taccaitanyaṃ prasajyeta na ca janmāntaraṃ bhavet ||
pariṇāmavivekādyaiḥ śaktyabhivyaktyanugrahāt | tebhya eva bhavedbuddhirna buddhyantarapūrvikā ||
tathaivottarakāle 'pi pūrvabuddheryaducyate | buddhyantaraprasūtatvaṃ dṛṣṭānto 'tra na vidyate ||
athādhāravinirmuktā śaktiḥ syātkalalādiṣu | paścādvijñānasiddhyarthamātmā śaktyabhidho bhavet ||
śaktyādhāraprakḷptau vā nātmano 'nyaḥ prakalpyate | jvālābudbudavadvṛttirna cādhārādvinā dhiyām ||
jñānaśaktisvabhāvo 'to nityaḥ sarvagataḥ pumān | dehāntarakṣamaḥ kalpyaḥ so 'gacchanneva yokṣyate ||
yajamānatvamapyātmā sakriyatvātprapadyate | na parispanda evaikaḥ kriyā naḥ kaṇabhojivat ||
na ca svasamavetaiva kartṛbhiḥ kriyate kriyā | kriyā dhātvarthamātraṃ syādanyādhāre 'pi kartṛtā ||
sattājñānādirūpāṇāṃ kartā tāvatsvayaṃ pumān | yo 'pi bhūtaparispandastatrādhiṣṭānato bhavet ||
taduddeśapravṛtteśca yā yā dehendriyaiḥ kriyā | kriyate puruṣeṇaiva sā sā sarvā kṛtocyate ||
naiva hyeṣāṃ pravṛttiḥ syātpuruṣeṇāparigrahe | asvātantryādato naiṣāṃ parispande 'pi kartṛtā ||
tatkarmopārjitaiścetaiḥ kriyamāṇeṣu karmasu | kartṛtā yajamānānāmṛtvikparaśukarmavat ||
yathā parikrayāmnānādṛtvigdvārā kriyeṣyate | gamanādividhestadvadbhūtadvāratvamāśritam ||
krayo yathātmano nāsti gamanādi tathaiva hi | vidhīyate ca tenātra paradvārāsya kartṛtā ||
yathā vā devadattasya cchedane kāṣṭhasaṃśrite | kartṛtvamevaṃ puṃsaḥ syāc charīragamanādiṣu ||
vyāpārāntaratastatra kartṛtvaṃ cedihāpi naḥ | saṅkalpasattvavattvābhyāṃ pumāniṣṭaḥ prayojakaḥ ||
sādhāraṇyena kartṛtvaṃ sattvavattvena karmasu | saṅkalpanaiḥ punarbhedātpratikarmāsya kartṛtā ||
na ca sarvatra tulyatvaṃ syātprayojakakarmaṇām | calanena hyasiṃ yoddhā prayuṅkte cchedanaṃ prati ||
senāpatistu vācaiva bhṛtyānāṃ viniyojakaḥ | rājā sannidhimātreṇa viniyuṅkte kadā cana ||
tasmādacalato 'pi syāccalane kartṛtātmanaḥ | yathaivābhidyamānasya devadattasya bhettṛtā ||
karmāntarairyadā dānaṃ svavyāpāraḥ sa eva vā | bhūtakriyāsu puṃsaḥ syāt, tāni bhūtāntaraiḥ punaḥ ||
tāni bhūtāntarebhyaścetyevamādirna vidyate | karmakṣayāttvanātmīyaiḥ kṛtaṃ karma na limpati ||
anvārambhaṇamānādāvaudumbaryādivarttini | svarūpāsambhavādyaṣṭuḥ śarīreṇaiva kartṛtā ||
tasmādyathākṛtau śāstraṃ pravṛttaṃ vyaktimāśrayet | tathā puṃsi pravṛttasya bhūtendriyasamāśrayaḥ ||
parairabhigatān pūrvamātmahetunnirasyati | netyetāvadavacchedyam, vidharmāṇa ime yataḥ ||
ayāvaddehabhāvitvaṃ kārśyāderapi dṛśyate | athāvasthāntaraṃ tatra tathā mṛtyurapīṣyatām |
etāvaniha bhedaḥ syāc charīre dṛḍha eva yā | prāṇādyapagatistatra nimittaṃ na pratīyate ||
guṇo dravyavināśādvā vināśamupagacchati | guṇāntaropapātādvā tasmādutkṛtya nāśyate ||
na tāvattaddvayaṃ mṛtyau sarvasyaivopalabhyate | avinaṣṭaśarīrasya prāṇādiścāpagacchati ||
tasmānna dehadharmatvaṃ prāṇāderiti gamyate | tasmindṛṣṭe 'pyasadbhāvātsragvilepanagandhavat ||
bahirvṛttitvamapyasti prāṇāderiti gamyate | parendriyaiḥ, sukhādistu nāntaratvātpratīyate ||
prahṛṣṭavadanatvādiliṅgagamyaṃ sadaiva hi | antaḥsthiterna dṛṣṭiścet, pāṭite 'pyanupagrahāt ||
antaḥśarīre rūpādi pāṭitasyopalabhyate | na sukhādiḥ, ago 'syāsau na manobuddhivadguṇaḥ ||
guṇatvādāśritatvaṃ hi sukhādeḥ syādrasādivat | ya āśritaḥ sa ātmā, iti bruvāṇasyaitaduttaram ||
puṇānāṃ paratantratvāt guṇavānanumīyate | siddhe guṇatve tattvasmān pratyasiddhaṃ sukhādiṣu ||
bhedena kimupanyastā tulyanyāyecchayā smṛtiḥ | ubhayaṃ na hyadṛṣṭe 'rthe vāsanātaśca siddhyati ||
upalabdhimanāśritya smṛtyaivecchopajāyate | upalabdhisamāno 'syāḥ kartā naikāntato bhavet ||
upalabdhyanusāreṇa smṛtyātmā punariṣyate | samānastena kartāsti tadarthaṃ punarucyate ||
tatrāpi tu samānāyāṃ santatau vāsanā yataḥ | tasmātsatyapi bhinnatve smaraṇaṃ vyavatiṣṭate ||
hetuṣvevaṃ parokteṣu pratiṣiddheṣu samprati | ahampratyayavijñeyaḥ svayamātmopapādyate ||
ahaṃ yāmītyahaṃśabdaḥ śarīrārthaḥ prayujyate | gantṛtvāttasya, na hyātmā gamanaṃ pratipadyate ||
smaraṇapratyabhijñāne bhavetāṃ vāsanāvaśāt | anyārthaviṣaye, jñātuḥ pratyabhijñā tu durlabhā ||
ahaṃ vedmītyahaṃ buddhirjñātāramadhigacchati | tatra syādjñātṛvijñānaṃ tadādhāro 'tha vā pumān ||
kṛtaṃ bhūtendriyāṇāṃ ca caitanyapratiṣedhanam | samastavyastasaṅghātavivekapariṇāminām ||
sāṅkhyādibhiḥ, aśuddhatvātsaṅghātātsanniveśataḥ | mṛtavacca śarīratvādbhūtatvādbāhyabhūtavat ||
cetanatve hi sarveṣāṃ na sambandhaḥ parasparam | samatvāt, ekacaitanye 'nyasyāṅgatvaṃ virudhyate ||
saṅghātasanniveśau ca na staḥ pārārthyavarjitau | bhoktā ca cetanaḥ kaścidastītyatrāviruddhatā ||
yadi syādjñānamātraṃ ca kṣaṇikaṃ jñātṛ tatra vaḥ | na bhavetpratyabhijñānaṃ pūrvajñātari samprati ||
jñātavānahamevedaṃ puredānīṃ ca vedmyaham | tasya jñānakṣaṇaḥ ko nu viṣayaḥ parikalpyatām ||
pūrvavṛtte hi viṣaye jñātavāniti sambhavet | jānāmīti na satyaṃ syānnedānīṃ vettyasau tataḥ ||
yadīdānīntano grāhyo jānāmītyupapadyate | jñātavānityado 'satyaṃ naivājñāsīdayaṃ yataḥ ||
ubhayagrāhyatāyāṃ tu dvayamapyanṛtaṃ bhavet | na hyetau jñātavantau vā jānīto vādhunā punaḥ ||
santāno na ca tadgrāhyo dvairūpyasyāsambhavāt | jñātavānna hyasau pūrvamavastutvānna vādhunā ||
sāmānyaṃ na ca kiñcitte jñātṛ pūrvāparakṣaṇe | sādṛśyātpratyabhijñā cenna syādasadṛśeṣu sā ||
gāmahaṃ jñātavān pūrvamaśvaṃ jānāmyahaṃ punaḥ | atha jñātṛtvasāmānyaṃ tatsyāddehāntareṣvapi ||
tatra sarveṇa vijñāte bhavedahamiti smṛtiḥ | ekasantānaje cāpi sa iti syātkṣaṇe matiḥ ||
yathā dehāntarajñāne ghaṭādau vā bahiḥ sthite | jñātari pratyabhijñāṃ ca vāsanā kartumarhati ||
nātasmin sa iti jñānaṃ na hyasau bhrāntikāraṇam | na cāhampratyayo bhrāntiriṣṭo bādhakavarjanāt ||
jñāturanyaśca viṣayastasya na syātsvabhāvataḥ | ahaṃ pratyayavijñeyo jñātā naḥ sarvadaiva hi ||
guruḥ sthūlaḥ kṛśo vāhamiti dehe 'pi yā matiḥ | bhrāntiḥ sā, bhedarūpaṃ hi guru me taditīṣyate ||
idaṃ mamedṛśaṃ cakṣurmano me bhrāntamityapi | indriyeṣvapi bhedena vyavahāraśca dṛśyate ||
ajñātṛtvasya siddhatvādvirodhādbhedavatyapi | pratyāsattinimittastu syādabhedamatirbhramaḥ ||
mamātmeti matirbhedavyapadeśena yātmanaḥ | tatrāvasthātmanā bhedaṃ jñānasyāśritya kalpanā ||
mametyetasya mukhyārtho nātmano 'nyaḥ pratīyate | tenāsau bhedahetuḥ syād, bhedaśca jñānahetukaḥ ||
ye cehājñātanānātvāsteṣāṃ deheṣvahaṃ matiḥ | tatrāpyātmābhimānenetyahambuddhirdhruvātmani ||
ye tu vijñātanānātvāste deheṣvanahaṃkṛtāḥ | jānāmyahamitīdaṃ tu jñānaṃ naiva nivarttate ||
tannivṛttau na teṣāṃ syāddhyānaṃ śiṣyopadeśane | pravṛttirdṛśyate sā ca, tenātmā taiḥ pratīyate ||
śāstrādavardhavijñāte yadyahaṃ jñātavāniti | nāvagacchettataḥ sarvaḥ pravartetāditaḥ punaḥ ||
tenāsmātpratyabhijñānātsarvalokāvadhāritāt | nairātmyavādabādhaḥ syāt, ete ca pratihetavaḥ ||
hyastanāhammatigrāhyo jñātādyāpyanuvarttate | ahaṃpratyayagamyatvādidānīntanaboddhṛvat ||
eṣa vā hyo bhavejjñātā jñātṛtvāttata eva vā | hyastanajñātṛvat, teṣāṃ pratyayānāṃ ca sādhyatā ||
ekasantānasambandhijñātrahampratyayatvataḥ | hyastanādyatanāḥ sarve tulyārthaścaikabuddhivat ||
vedādevātmanāstitvaṃ yo nāma pratipadyate | virodhaṃ vātmanā brūyāttaṃ prati brāhmaṇābhidhā ||
anyathānupapatteśca vidhinātmanyapekṣite | astitvadyotanādetairarthākṣiptasamarthanam ||
śāntāyāṃ vācyaśaktāyāmātmā kena prakāśyate | ātmanaiva prakāśyo 'yamātmā jyotiritīritam ||
agrāhya iti sāmānyātsarveṇeti pratīyate | ātmajyotiṣṭvavacanātparairityavatiṣṭhate ||
arthādevārthabuddhiryā sā śuddhaivopamocyate | sādṛśyabodhanaṃ śabdairupamānāgamau punaḥ ||
ātmajñānāvinābhūtadṛṣṭaceṣṭānirūpaṇāt | pareṣāmātmavijñānamanumānādudāhṛtam ||
sadasannāśyanāśātmaparikīrtanamūḍhayā | coditaḥ pūrvapakṣo 'yamiti siddhāntamabravīt ||
avināśī svarūpeṇa puruṣo yā tu nāśitā | mātrāṇāṃ sā 'dhikārāṇām, bhūtādīnāmasaṃjñitā ||
